------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Xhosa Bible: Ezekiel

<span id="an_1:1">1:1</span> Ke kaloku, ngomnyaka wamashumi omathathu,
ngenyanga yesine, ngolwesihlanu usuku enyangeni leyo, ndakubon’ ukuba
ndiphakathi kwabathinjiweyo ngasemlanjeni oyiKebhare, avuleka amazulu,
ndabona imibono kaThixo.

<span id="an_1:2">1:2</span> Ngolwesihlanu enyangeni leyo (ingumnyaka ke
wesihlanu wokuthinjwa kokumkani uYehoyakin lowo),

<span id="an_1:3">1:3</span> kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kuHezekile unyana
kaBhuzi, umbingeleli, ezweni lamaKaledi, ngasemlanjeni oyiKebhare; saba
phezu kwakhe apho isandla sikaYehova.

<span id="an_1:4">1:4</span> Ndabona ke, nanko kusiza umoya ovuthuzayo,
uvela ngasentla, unelifu elikhulu nomlilo obumbeneyo njengembumbulu,
nobumhlophe obungeenxa zonke kulo, obuphuma ngaphakathi kwawo,
bubonakala ngathi yigolide evuthiweyo emlilweni phakathi.

<span id="an_1:5">1:5</span> Ngaphakathi kwawo yimfano yezinto
eziphilileyo ezine. Nantsi ke imbonakalo yazo: zibe zinemfano yomntu;

<span id="an_1:6">1:6</span> inye ibinobuso obune, inye kuzo apho
ibinamaphiko amane.

<span id="an_1:7">1:7</span> Imilenze yazo ibiyimilenze ethe nkqo;
umphantsi weenyawo ubunjengomphantsi wenqina lethole; zidangazela
zibonakala ngathi lubhedu olubengezelisiweyo.

<span id="an_1:8">1:8</span> Zazinezandla zomntu ngaphantsi kwamaphiko
azo emacaleni azo omane; zone ke zinobuso namaphiko;

<span id="an_1:9">1:9</span> amaphiko azo abehlangene, elaleyo nelaleyo;
bezingajiki ekuhambeni kwazo, bezihamba, iyileyo iye kwicala
elikhangelene nobuso bayo.

<span id="an_1:10">1:10</span> Imfano yobuso bazo ibe ibubuso bomntu;
zinobuso bengonyama zone ngasekunene; zinobuso benkomo zone ngasekhohlo,
zinobuso bokhozi zone;

<span id="an_1:11">1:11</span> ubuso bazo namaphiko azo abe ahlukene
ngaphezulu; iyileyo inamabini ehlangene nawaleyo, namaphiko amabini ke
egubungele imizimba yazo.

<span id="an_1:12">1:12</span> Zahamba ke, iyileyo yaya kwicala
elikhangelene nobuso bayo; apho sukuba ubusiya khona umoya, zaya khona;
azajika ekuhambeni kwazo.

<span id="an_1:13">1:13</span> Imfano yezinto eziphilileyo ezo,
imbonakalo yazo, ibingathi ngamalahle omlilo abasiweyo; ibingathi
yimbonakalo yezikhuni ezitshangazayo; wona wahambahamba phakathi
kwezinto eziphilileyo ezo; umhlophe ke umlilo lowo, emlilweni kuphuma
imibane.

<span id="an_1:14">1:14</span> Izinto eziphilileyo bezigidima zibuye,
ngokokubonakala kokuphambaphamba kombane.

<span id="an_1:15">1:15</span> Ndazibona izinto eziphilileyo; nanko ke,
kukho iivili emhlabeni, ecaleni kwezinto eziphilileyo, zinganye iivili
kubuso ngobuso bazo obune.

<span id="an_1:16">1:16</span> Ukubonakala kweevili nokusetyenzwa kwazo
kwakunjengembonakalo yekrizolite, zimfani-nye zone; ukubonakala kwazo
nokusetyenzwa kwazo kungathi ivili ingaphakathi kwevili.

<span id="an_1:17">1:17</span> Ekuhambeni kwazo zaphambela kumacala azo
omane; azajika ekuhambeni kwazo.

<span id="an_1:18">1:18</span> Iifeleni zazo beziphakamile,
bezisoyikeka; iifeleni zazo bezizele ngamehlo ngeenxa zonke kuzo zone.

<span id="an_1:19">1:19</span> Zakuhamba izinto eziphilileyo, zahamba
nazo iivili ecaleni lazo; zakusuka izinto eziphilileyo emhlabeni, zasuka
nazo iivili.

<span id="an_1:20">1:20</span> Apho sukuba usiya khona umoya, zaya apho
sukuba umoya ubusiya khona; zasuka iivili kunye nazo; ngokokuba umoya
wezinto eziphilileyo ubukho ezivilini ezo.

<span id="an_1:21">1:21</span> Zakuhamba, zahamba nazo; zakuma, zema
nazo; zakusuka emhlabeni, zasuka iivili kunye nazo; ngokokuba umoya
wezinto eziphilileyo ubukho ezivilini ezo.

<span id="an_1:22">1:22</span> Naphezu kweentloko zezinto eziphilileyo
bekukho into efana nesibhakabhaka, ngathi ngembonakalo yikristale
eyoyikekayo, sanekiwe phezu kwentloko yazo ngaphezulu.

<span id="an_1:23">1:23</span> Ngaphantsi kwesibhakabhaka amaphiko
ayethe tye, elo lasinga kwelo; iyileyo inamabini ayigubungeleyo, iyileyo
inamabini ayigubungeleyo emzimbeni.

<span id="an_1:24">1:24</span> Ndeva ke isandi samaphiko azo,
sinjengesandi samanzi amaninzi, ngathi lilizwi loSomandla, ekuhambeni
kwazo; izwi elinengxolo ngathi sisandi somkhosi; zakuma, zawayeka ehla
amaphiko azo.

<span id="an_1:25">1:25</span> Kwabakho ke izwi liphuma ngaphaya
kwesibhakabhaka, esibe siphezu kweentloko zazo; zakuma, zawayeka ehla
amaphiko azo.

<span id="an_1:26">1:26</span> Ngaphezu kwesibhakabhaka esibe siphezu
kweentloko zazo, kwabonakala umfanekiselo wetrone, wanga lilitye
lesafire; ngaphezu komfanekiselo wetrone kwabakho umfanekiselo ongathi
yimbonakalo yomntu phezu kwayo ngaphezulu.

<span id="an_1:27">1:27</span> Ndabona ke, ngathi yimbonakalo yegolide
evuthiweyo, ngathi yimbonakalo yomlilo, ngaphakathi kwayo nangeenxa
zonke kuyo, kwathabathela embonakalweni yesinqe kwenyusa; kwathabathela
embonakalweni yesinqe kwehlisa, ndabona ke ngathi yimbonakalo yomlilo,
kumhlophe ke ngeenxa zonke.

<span id="an_1:28">1:28</span> Ngathi yimbonakalo yomnyama obakhoyo
efini mini ngemvula, yabe injalo imbonakalo yobumhlophe ngeenxa zonke.
Leyo yimbonakalo yomfanekiselo wobuqaqawuli bukaYehova. Ndabona ke,
ndawa ngobuso, ndaliva izwi lothethayo.

<span id="an_2:1">2:1</span> Wathi kum, Nyana womntu, yima ngeenyawo
zakho, ndithethe nawe.

<span id="an_2:2">2:2</span> Kwangena ke uMoya kum, xa abethetha nam,
wandimisa ngeenyawo zam, ndamva othetha kum.

<span id="an_2:3">2:3</span> Wathi kum, Nyana womntu, ndikuthuma
koonyana bakaSirayeli, kwiintlanga ezingabagwiliki, abagwilikileyo kum;
bona nooyise babo bakreqile kum, kwada kwayile mini.

<span id="an_2:4">2:4</span> Oonyana baziingwanyalala ubuso, balukhuni
intliziyo. Ndikuthuma kubo; uze uthi kubo, Itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_2:5">2:5</span> Ke bona (nokuba bathe beva, nokuba bathe
bala, kuba beyindlu eneenkani) baya kwazi ukuba bekukho umprofeti
phakathi kwabo.

<span id="an_2:6">2:6</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, musa ukuboyika,
ungawoyiki amazwi abo; nangani usemarhawini nasemeveni, uhleli phezu
koonomadudwane, musa ukuwoyika amazwi abo, ungaqhiphuki umbilini bubuso
babo, kuba bayindlu eneenkani.

<span id="an_2:7">2:7</span> Wathethe ke kubo amazwi am, nokuba bathe
beva, nokuba bathe bala; ngokuba baneenkani.

<span id="an_2:8">2:8</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, yiva endikuthethayo
kuwe; ungabi nankani, njengale ndlu ineenkani; yakhamisa, udle
endikunikayo.

<span id="an_2:9">2:9</span> Ndabona, naso isandla solulelwe kum; nantso
kuso incwadi esongwayo.

<span id="an_2:10">2:10</span> Wayitwabulula phambi kwam; yaye ke
ibhaliwe ngaphakathi nangaphandle, kubhalwe kuyo izimbonono, nezikhwino,
nezimema.

<span id="an_3:1">3:1</span> Wathi ke kum, Nyana womtu, kudle
okufumanayo yidle le ncwadi isongwayo, uye uthethe kwindlu kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_3:2">3:2</span> Ndawuvula ke umlomo wam, wandidlisa loo
ncwadi isongwayo;

<span id="an_3:3">3:3</span> wathi kum, Nyana womntu, dlisa isisu sakho,
uzalise umbilini wakho ngaloo ncwadi isongwayo ndikunikayo. Ndayidla ke,
yaba nencasa emlonyeni wam, njengobusi.

<span id="an_3:4">3:4</span> Wathi kum, Nyana womntu, hamba uye kwindlu
kaSirayeli, uthethe kubo ngamazwi am.

<span id="an_3:5">3:5</span> Ngokuba akuthunyelwa kubantu abantetho
inzulu, abalulwimi lunzima; uthunyelwa kwindlu kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_3:6">3:6</span> Andikuthumeli kwizizwe ezininzi, ezintetho
inzulu, ezilulwimi lunzima, ezimazwi ungaweviyo; ndikuthumele kuzo ezi
zinokukuphulaphula zona.

<span id="an_3:7">3:7</span> Ke indlu kaSirayeli ayiyi kuvuma
ukukuphulaphula; ngokokuba abavumi ukundiphulaphula nam; kuba yonke
indlu kaSirayeli ilukhuni ibunzi, igogotyile ngentliziyo.

<span id="an_3:8">3:8</span> Yabona, ndibenza lukhuni ubuso bakho,
kwanjengobuso babo; ibunzi lakho libe lukhuni, Kwanjengebunzi labo;

<span id="an_3:9">3:9</span> ndilenza libe njengedayiman, elukhuni
ngaphezu kweqhwitha, ibunzi lakho. Uze ungaboyiki, ungaqhiphuki umbilini
phambi kwabo; ngokuba bayindlu eneenkani.

<span id="an_3:10">3:10</span> Wathi kum, Nyana womntu, onke amazwi am
endiya kuwathetha kuwe, wamkelele entliziyweni yakho, uweve ngeendlebe
zakho;

<span id="an_3:11">3:11</span> uhambe uye kubathinjwa, koonyana babantu
bakowenu, uthethe kubo uthi kubo, Itsho iNkosi uYehova; nokuba bathe
beva, nokuba bathe bala.

<span id="an_3:12">3:12</span> Wandifunqula uMoya, ndeva ngasemva kwam
isandi sendudumo enkulu, sisithi, Mabubongwe ubuqaqawuli bukaYehova,
endaweni yabo.

<span id="an_3:13">3:13</span> Kananjalo ndeva nesandi samaphiko ezinto
eziphililileyo, elo lifikelela kwelo, nesandi seevili ngakuzo, nesandi
sendudumo enkulu.

<span id="an_3:14">3:14</span> Wandifunqula uMoya, wandisusa; ndahamba
ndikrakra bubushushu bomoya wam. Saye ke isandla sikaYehova siphezu
kwam, siqinile.

<span id="an_3:15">3:15</span> Ndafika ke eTelabhibhi, kubathinjwa
ababehleli emlanjeni oyiKebhare, apho babehleli khona; ndahlala phantsi
khona iintsuku zasixhenxe, ndimangalisiwe, phakathi kwabo.

<span id="an_3:16">3:16</span> Kwathi ekupheleni kweentsuku ezisixhenxe,
kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_3:17">3:17</span> Nyana womntu, ndikwenze umboniseli
kwindlu kaSirayeli; live ke ilizwi emlonyeni wam, ubavuselele ngokuvela
kum.

<span id="an_3:18">3:18</span> Xa ndithi kongendawo, Inene, uya kufa;
usuke wena ungamvuseleli, ungathethi ukuze umvuselele ongendawo, ukuze
aphume endleleni yakhe engendawo, aphile; wofa ongendawo lowo
ngobugwenxa bakhe, kodwa lona igazi lakhe ndolibiza esandleni sakho.

<span id="an_3:19">3:19</span> Wena ke, xa uthe wamvuselela ongendawo,
akabuya endleleni yakhe, endleleni yakhe engendawo: wofa ngobugwenxa
bakhe, kodwa wena uwuhlangule umphefumlo wakho.

<span id="an_3:20">3:20</span> Ke, lakubuya ebulungiseni balo ilungisa,
lenze ngobugqwetha, ndibeke isikhubekiso phambi kwalo; lofa lona; xa
uthe akwalivuselela, lofa ngenxa yesono salo, bungakhunjulwa ubulungisa
balo elabenzayo; kodwa lona igazi lalo ndolibiza esandleni sakho.

<span id="an_3:21">3:21</span> Wena ke, xa uthe walivuselela ilungisa,
ukuba lingoni ilungisa, alona ke: lophila ngokuba livuselelwe, ke wena
uwuhlangule umphefumlo wakho.

<span id="an_3:22">3:22</span> Sabakho apho isandla sikaYehova phezu
kwam, wathi kum, Suk’ ume, phuma uye entilini, ndithethe nawe khona.

<span id="an_3:23">3:23</span> Ndesuka ndema, ndaphuma ndaya entilini;
nanko ke, kumi khona ubuqaqawuli bukaYehova obunjengobuqaqawuli obuya
ndabubonayo ngasemlanjeni oyiKebhare; ndawa ngobuso.

<span id="an_3:24">3:24</span> Kwafika uMoya kum, wandimisa ngeenyawo
zam, wathetha nam, wathi, Yiya uzivalele endlwini yakho.

<span id="an_3:25">3:25</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, yabona, baya
kukufaka izintya, bakubophe ngazo, ukuze ungaphumi uye phakathi kwabo.

<span id="an_3:26">3:26</span> Ndiya kulunamathelisa ulwimi lwakho
ekhuhlangubeni lakho, ube sisidenge, ungabi yindoda eyohlwayayo kubo;
ngokuba bayindlu eneenkani.

<span id="an_3:27">3:27</span> Ndakuthetha nawe, ndowuvula umlomo wakho,
uthi ke kubo, Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ovayo makeve, owalayo makale;
ngokuba bayindlu eneenkani.

<span id="an_4:1">4:1</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, thabatha isitena,
usibeke phambi kwakho, ukrole umzi kuso, iYerusalem;

<span id="an_4:2">4:2</span> uwungqinge, uwakhele iinqaba zokubonisela,
uwufumbele udonga lokungqinga; uwenzele iminquba, umisele izinto
zokutyhomfa iindonga ngeenxa zonke.

<span id="an_4:3">4:3</span> Wena ke, thabatha ipani yesinyithi, uyimise
ibe ludonga lwesinyithi phakathi kwakho nomzi lowo; ububhekise ubuso
bakho kuwo, ube selungqingweni wona, uwungqinge wena. Ngumqondiso lo
kwindlu kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_4:4">4:4</span> Wena ke, lala ngecala lakho lasekhohlo,
ububeke ubugwenxa bendlu kaSirayeli phezu kwalo: ngangenani leentsuku
oya kulala ngalo, uya kubuthwala ubugwenxa babo.

<span id="an_4:5">4:5</span> Kuba iminyaka yobugwenxa babo ndiyenza
ukuba kuwe ibe ngangenani leentsuku, iintsuku ezimakhulu mathathu
anamanci asithoba; uya kubuthwala ubugwenxa bendlu kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_4:6">4:6</span> Uya kuthi, wakuba uzifezile ezo, ulale
okwesibini ngecala lakho lasekunene, ubuthwale ubugwenxa bendlu kaYuda
iintsuku ezimashumi mane; ndikwenzela usuku lube ngumnyaka, usuku lube
ngumnyaka.

<span id="an_4:7">4:7</span> Uze ke ububhekise ubuso bakho elungqingweni
lweYerusalem, ingalo yakho ihlutyiwe, uprofetele kuyo.

<span id="an_4:8">4:8</span> Yabona, ndikufaka izintya, ukuze
ungaguqukeli kwelinye icala, ude uzigqibe iintsuku zokungqinga kwakho.

<span id="an_4:9">4:9</span> Wena ke, thabatha ingqolowa, nerhasi,
neembotyi, neentlumayo, namazimba, nespelete, uzigalele ezo zinto
sityeni sinye, uzenzele wena isonka; ngokwenani leentsuku olala ngecala
lakho, uya kusidla iintsuku ezimakhulu mathathu anamanci asithoba.

<span id="an_4:10">4:10</span> Ukudla kwakho oya kukudla koba
ngokomlinganiselo, iishekele ezimashumi mabini ngosuku; uya kusidla
amaxesha ngamaxesha.

<span id="an_4:11">4:11</span> Namanzi wowasela ngomlinganiselo,
isahlulo sesithandathu sehin; uya kusisela amaxesha ngamaxesha.

<span id="an_4:12">4:12</span> Uya kusidla ngokwesonka esiliqebengwana
serhasi, usoje emehlweni abo ngeengqatha eziphuma emntwini.

<span id="an_4:13">4:13</span> Wathi uYehova, Oonyana bakaSirayeli baya
kwenjenjalo ukusidla siyinqambi ezintlangeni, endiya kubagxothela kuzo.

<span id="an_4:14">4:14</span> Ndathi, Awu! Nkosi Yehova! Yabona,
umphefumlo wam awuzanga wenziwe inqambi; into ezifeleyo neqwengiweyo
andizanga ndiyidle, kwasebuncinaneni bam unanamhla; akufikanga nyama
iyimbozisa emlonyeni wam.

<span id="an_4:15">4:15</span> Wathi kum, Uyabona, ndikunika amalongo
enkomo esikhundleni seengqatha zomntu; soje kuwo isonka sakho.

<span id="an_4:16">4:16</span> Wathi kum, Nyana womntu, yabona, ndiya
kuwaphula umsimelelo osisonka eYerusalem, basidle isonka
ngomlinganiselo, benesithukuthezi; bawasele amanzi ngomlinganiselo,
bemangalisiwe;

<span id="an_4:17">4:17</span> ukuze baswele isonka namanzi,
bamangalisane, bangcungcutheke ebugwenxeni babo.

<span id="an_5:1">5:1</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, thabatha ikrele
elibukhali, libe sisitshetshe sokuguya, ulihambise entlokweni yakho
nasesilevini sakho, uthabathe isikali sokulinganisela, uzahlule iinwele.

<span id="an_5:2">5:2</span> Esinye isahlulo sesithathu uze usitshise
ngomlilo esazulwini somzi, zakuzaliseka iintsuku zongqingo; uthabathe
nesinye isahlulo sesithathu, uxabele ngekrele ngeenxa zonke kuso;
nesinye isahlulo sesithathu usichithachithe emoyeni, ndirhole ikrele
emva kwazo.

<span id="an_5:3">5:3</span> Uze uthabathe kuzo zibe mbalwa, uzibophe
esondweni lengubo yakho;

<span id="an_5:4">5:4</span> ubuye uthabathe kuzo, uziphose emlilweni,
uzitshise ngomlilo. Khona apho kuyo kuphuma umlilo, uye kuyo yonke indlu
kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_5:5">5:5</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Le Yerusalem
ndiyimise esazulwini seentlanga, amazwe angeenxa zonke kuyo.

<span id="an_5:6">5:6</span> Ke iwaphikisile ngokungendawo amasiko am
ngaphezu kweentlanga, nemimiselo yam ngaphezu kwamazwe angeenxa zonke
kuyo; ngokuba bawacekisile amasiko am, abahamba ngemimiselo yam.

<span id="an_5:7">5:7</span> Ngako oko, itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ngenxa enokuba nangxola ngaphezu kweentlanga ebezingeenxa zonke kuni,
anahamba ngemimiselo yam, anawenza amasiko am, anenza nangolwamasiko
eentlanga ebezingeenxa zonke kuni:

<span id="an_5:8">5:8</span> ngako oko, itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Yabona, mna, ewe mna, ndikuchasile; ndiya kwenza izigwebo esazulwini
sakho emehlweni eentlanga;

<span id="an_5:9">5:9</span> ndenze kuwe endingazanga ndikwenze,
endingayi kubuya ndikwenze okunjalo, ngenxa yamasikizi akho onke.

<span id="an_5:10">5:10</span> Ngako oko ooyise baya kudla oonyana
esazulwini sakho, oonyana badle ooyise; ndenze izigwebo,
ndiwachithachithe onke amasalela akho emimoyeni yonke.

<span id="an_5:11">5:11</span> Ngako oko, itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ndihleli nje, inyaniso, ngenxa enokuba ingcwele yam uyenze inqambi
ngeento zakho zonke ezinezothe, nangamasikizi akho onke, nam ndiya
kulisusa iliso lam, lingabi nanceba, ndingacongi nam.

<span id="an_5:12">5:12</span> Isahlulo sesithathu kuwe siya kufa
yindyikitya yokufa, siphele nayindlala esazulwini sakho; esinye isahlulo
sesithathu siwe likrele ngeenxa zonke kuwe; esinye isahlulo sesithathu
ndisichithachithe emimoyeni yonke, ndirhole ikrele emva kwabo.

<span id="an_5:13">5:13</span> Wophelela ke kubo umsindo wam,
ndibupholisele kubo ubushushu bam, ndithuthuzeleke; bazi ukuba mna
Yehova ndithethe ndinekhwele, ekubuphleleliseleni ubushushu bam kubo.

<span id="an_5:14">5:14</span> Phezu koko ndokwenza ube linxuwa
nesingcikivo ezintlangeni ezingeenxa zonke kuwe, emehlweni abo bonke
abadlulayo.

<span id="an_5:15">5:15</span> Uya kuba sisingcikivo nesinyeliso, ube
sisithethiso nommangaliso kwiintlanga ezingeenxa zonke kuwe, ekwenzeni
kwam izigwebo kuwe ngomsindo nangobushushu, nangezohlwayo zobushushu;
mna Yehova ndithethile:

<span id="an_5:16">5:16</span> nasekuzithumeni kwam kuwe iintolo ezimbi
zendlala, ezizezolonakaliso, endiya kuzithuma ukuze zinonakalise. Ndiya
kuyandisa indlala phezu kwenu, ndiwaphule umsimelelo asisonka kuni;

<span id="an_5:17">5:17</span> ndithume phezu kwenu indlala
namarhamncwa, akuhluthe abantwana, ifikelele kuwe indyikitya yokufa
negazi, ndikuzisele ikrele; mna Yehova ndithethile.

<span id="an_6:1">6:1</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_6:2">6:2</span> Nyana womntu, bhekisa ubuso bakho
ezintabeni zakwaSirayeli, uprofetele kuzo,

<span id="an_6:3">6:3</span> uthi, Yivani, nina zintaba zakwaSirayeli,
ilizwi leNkosi uYehova. Itsho iNkosi uYehova kwiintaba nakwiinduli,
kwizihlambo nakwimifula, ukuthi, Yabonani, ndinizisela ikrele,
ndizidilize iziganga zenu.

<span id="an_6:4">6:4</span> Ziya kuba ngamanxuwa izibingelelo zenu,
zaphulwe izithixo zenu zelanga; ndibakhahlele ababuleweyo benu phambi
kwezigogo zenu.

<span id="an_6:5">6:5</span> Ndozibeka izidumbu zoonyana bakaSirayeli
phambi kwezigodo zabo, ndiwachithachithe amathambo enu ngeenxa zonke
ezibingelelweni zenu.

<span id="an_6:6">6:6</span> Imizi yoba ngamanxuwa ezindaweni zonke
zokuhlala kwenu, zichithakale iziganga; ukuze zichithakale zibe
ngamanxuwa izibingelelo zenu, zaphulwe ziphele izigodo zenu, zigawulwe
izithixo zenu zelanga, icinywe imisebenzi yenu.

<span id="an_6:7">6:7</span> Uya kuwa obuleweyo esazulwini senu; nazi
ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_6:8">6:8</span> Ndiya kushiya amasalela, ngokuthi kubekho
kuni abasindileyo ekreleni phakathi kweentlanga, ekuchithwachithweni
kwenu emazweni.

<span id="an_6:9">6:9</span> Abasindileyo benu baya kundikhumbula
phakathi kweentlanga abathinjelwe kuzo, xa ndithe ndayaphula intliziyo
yabo ehenyuzayo, eyemkayo kum, namehlo abo abehenyuza ngokulandela
izigodo zabo; bakruquke bububi ababenzileyo ngokusingisele emasikizini
abo onke.

<span id="an_6:10">6:10</span> Baya kwazi ukuba ndinguYehova; andifumane
ndathetha ndathi, Ndiya kubenza obu bubi kubo.

<span id="an_6:11">6:11</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Betha
esandleni sakho, ungqishe ngonyawo lwakho, uthi, Yeha! ngenxa yawo onke
amasikizi amabi endlu kaSirayeli; kuba baya kuwa likrele, nayindlala,
nayindyikitya yokufa.

<span id="an_6:12">6:12</span> Okude uya kufa yindyikitya yokufa,
okufuphi awe likrele, nosale walondolozwa afe yindlala; ndibuphelelisele
kubo ubushushu bam.

<span id="an_6:13">6:13</span> Niya kwazi ukuba ndinguYehova, bakuba
ababuleweyo benu bephakathi kwezigodo zenu ngeenxa zonke ezibingelelweni
zenu, ezindulini zonke eziphakamileyo, ezincotsheni zonke zeentaba,
naphantsi kwemithi yonke eluhlaza, naphantsi kwemiterebhinti ethe
shinyi, ezindaweni ababenikela kuzo ivumba elithozamisayo kwizigodo zabo
zonke.

<span id="an_6:14">6:14</span> Ndosolula isandla sam phezu kwabo;
ndilenze ilizwe kube senkangala yakwankangala, ngaphezu kwentlango
yakwaDibhelata, ezindaweni zonke zokuhlala kwabo; bazi ukuba
ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_7:1">7:1</span> Kananjalo kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum,
lisithi,

<span id="an_7:2">7:2</span> Wena, wena ke nyana womntu, itsho iNkosi
uYehova kumhlaba wakwaSirayeli ukuthi, Isiphelo, isiphelo siwafikele
amasondo omane elizwe.

<span id="an_7:3">7:3</span> Kaloku isiphelo sikufikele; ndiya
kuwukhuphela umsindo wam kuwe, ndikugwebe ngokweendlela zakho, ndiwabeke
phezu kwakho amasikizi akho onke.

<span id="an_7:4">7:4</span> Aliyi kuba nanceba kuwe iliso lam,
ndingakucongi; ke ndiya kukuzisela iindlela zakho, abe sesazulwini sakho
amasikizi akho; nazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_7:5">7:5</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ububi, ububi
obubodwa; yabonani, buyeza.

<span id="an_7:6">7:6</span> Kuza isiphelo, isiphelo sona siyeza,
sikuvukele wena; yabona siyeza.

<span id="an_7:7">7:7</span> Uyakuzela umjojo, mmi welizwe eli; liyeza
ixesha, isondele imini; kusisaqunge, akungamayeyeye emihlali ezintabeni.

<span id="an_7:8">7:8</span> Ngoku kwakufuphi nje ndiya kuthulula phezu
kwakho ubushushu bam, ndiwuphelelisele kuwe umsindo wam, ndikugwebe
ngokweendlela zakho, ndiwabeke phezu kwakho onke amasikizi akho.

<span id="an_7:9">7:9</span> Aliyi kuba nanceba kuwe iliso lam,
ndingakucongi; ke ndiya kuwabeka phezu kwakho ngokweendlela zakho
amasikizi akho phakathi kwakho; nazi ukuba mna Yehova ndingobethayo.

<span id="an_7:10">7:10</span> Nantso imini! Nantso, ifikile! Uphuma
umjojo, luphuma amathupha uswazi, kuyatyatyamba ukukhukhumala.

<span id="an_7:11">7:11</span> Ugonyamelo luphakame lwaba luswazi
lokungendawo; akuyi kubakho namnye kubo osalayo, kungabikho nto
kwingxokolo yabo, kungabikho nto kwintabalala yabo; kungabikho njuze
isalayo kubo.

<span id="an_7:12">7:12</span> Lifikile ixesha, isondele imini;
othengayo makangavuyi, othengisayo makangenzi sijwili; ngokuba ukuvutha
komsindo kuyayizela yonke ingxokolo yakhona.

<span id="an_7:13">7:13</span> Ngokuba othengisayo akayi kubuyela
entweni abethengise ngayo, nokuba ubesadla ubomi phakathi kwabadla
ubomi; ngokuba umbono ongengxokolo yonke yakhona awuyi kubuya umva;
kungabikho bani ubomelezayo ubomi bakhe ebugwenxeni bakhe.

<span id="an_7:14">7:14</span> Bavuthela isigodlo, balungisa konke;
kodwa akukho namnye oya ekulweni; ngokuba ubushushu bam buyizele
ingxokolo yabo yonke.

<span id="an_7:15">7:15</span> Ngekrele ngaphandle, ngendyikitya yokufa
nangendlala ngaphakathi: osendle uya kufa likrele, ophakathi komzi
adliwe yindlala nayindyikitya yokufa.

<span id="an_7:16">7:16</span> Ke abasindileyo kubo bosinda, babe
sezintabeni njengamavukuthu asemifuleni, bedumzela bonke bephela, elowo
edumzela ngobugwenxa bakhe.

<span id="an_7:17">7:17</span> Zonke izandla ziya kuwa, onke amadolo aye
angabi namandla;

<span id="an_7:18">7:18</span> babhinqe ezirhwexayo, bagutyungelwe
kukududuzela, ebusweni bonke ibe kukudana, iintloko zabo zonke zibe
ziinkqayi.

<span id="an_7:19">7:19</span> Isilivere yabo baya kuyiphosa
ezitratweni, negolide yabo ibe yinto engcolileyo kubo. Isilivere yabo
negolide yabo ayiyi kuba nako ukubahlangula ngemini yokuphuphuma
komsindo kaYehova; abayi kuwuhluthisa ngayo umphefumlo wabo, nombilini
wabo bangawuzalisi ngayo; ngokuba yaba sisikhubekiso sokuba babe gwenxa.

<span id="an_7:20">7:20</span> Isivatho sabo esinobukhazikhazi
basimisela ikratshi, benza ngaso imifanekiso yabo engamasikizi,
enezothe; ngenxa yoko ndiyenze yayinto engcolileyo kubo.

<span id="an_7:21">7:21</span> Ndiya kuyinikela esandleni sabasemzini
ukuba iphangwe, nakwabangendawo behlabathi ibe lixhoba, bayihlambele;

<span id="an_7:22">7:22</span> ndibususe ubuso bam kubo, bayihlambele
ingqwebo yam; bafike abatyhobozi, bayihlambele.

<span id="an_7:23">7:23</span> Yenza umxokelelwane, ngokuba ilizwe
liliphalaza igazi elimsulwa, nomzi uzele lugonyamelo.

<span id="an_7:24">7:24</span> Ndozisa abanobubi basezintlangeni,
bazihluthe izindlu zabo, ndiliphelise ikratshi labanamandla, zihlanjelwe
iingcwele zabo.

<span id="an_7:25">7:25</span> Kuyafika ukuxhalaba; bafuna uxolo,
alukho.

<span id="an_7:26">7:26</span> Kuza umeyeliselo phezu komeyeliselo,
kubekho udaba phezu kodaba, bafune umbono kumprofeti, ke umyalelo
utshabalale ungabikho kumbingeleli, neqhinga kumadoda amakhulu.

<span id="an_7:27">7:27</span> Ukumkani uya kwenza isijwili, nesikhulu
sambathe ummangaliso, ziyekelele izandla zabantu belizwe eli. Ndiya
kwenza kubo ngokwendlela yabo, ndibagwebe ngokwezigwebo zabo; bazi ukuba
ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_8:1">8:1</span> Ke kaloku kwathi ngomnyaka wesithandathu,
ngenyanga yesithandathu, ngolwesihlanu enyangeni leyo, ndihleli endlwini
yam, namadoda amakhulu akwaYuda ehleli phambi kwam, sawa phezu kwam
khona isandla seNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_8:2">8:2</span> Ndabona, nantso into efana nendoda
ukubonakala kwayo; kuthabathele esinqeni sayo kwehlisa, kubonakala
ingumlilo; kuthabathele esinqeni sayo kunyuse, ngathi kukubonakala
kokukhazimla, ngathi yimbonakalo yegolide evuthiweyo.

<span id="an_8:3">8:3</span> Wolula into emilise okwesandla, wandibamba
ngesihlwitha sentloko yam; umoya wandifunqula ndaba phakathi komhlaba
nezulu. Wandisa eYerusalem ngemibono kaThixo, ekungeneni kwesango
lentendelezo ephakathi, elibheke ngasentla, apho bekuhleli khona
umfanekiso wobukhwele okhweletisayo.

<span id="an_8:4">8:4</span> Nabo ke bukhona ubuqaqawuli bukaThixo
kaSirayeli, bunjengombono endawubonayo entilini leyo.

<span id="an_8:5">8:5</span> Wathi kum, Nyana womntu, khawuphakamise
amehlo akho, ukhangele ngasentla. Ndawaphakamisa ke amehlo am,
ndakhangela ngasentla: nanko ngasentla kwesango lesibingelelo kukho loo
mfanekiso wobukhwele usekungeneni kwalo.

<span id="an_8:6">8:6</span> Wathi kum, Nyana womntu, uyakubona na
abakwenzayo? Ngamasikizi amakhulu la, iwenzayo apha indlu kaSirayeli,
ukuze ndikhwelele kude nengcwele yam; usaya kubuya ubone amasikizi
amakhulu kunala.

<span id="an_8:7">8:7</span> Wandisa ke ekungeneni kwentendelezo;
ndabona, nango umngxuma eludongeni.

<span id="an_8:8">8:8</span> Wathi kum, Nyana womntu, khawugqobhoze
eludongeni. Ndagqobhoza ke eludongeni, nanko kukho umnyango.

<span id="an_8:9">8:9</span> Wathi kum, Yiza, ubone amasikizi amabi
abawenzayo apha.

<span id="an_8:10">8:10</span> Ndangena, ndabona: nanzo zonke izinto
ezimilise okwesinambuzane nenkomo, izinto ezinezothe, nezigodo zonke
zendlu kaSirayeli, zikroliwe eludongeni ngeenxa zonke.

<span id="an_8:11">8:11</span> Kumi phambi kwazo amadoda angamashumi
asixhenxe kumadoda amakhulu endlu kaSirayeli, noYazaniya unyana kaShafan
emi phakathi kwawo, iyileyo iphethe ngesandla isiqhumiselo, kunyuka
ivumba lelifu lokuqhumisela.

<span id="an_8:12">8:12</span> Wathi kum, Nyana womntu, ukubonile na
akwenzayo emnyameni amadoda amakhulu endlu kaSirayeli, iyileyo
ezingontsini zayo ezinemifanekiso? ngokuba esithi, uYehova akasiboni,
uYehova ulilahlile ilizwe.

<span id="an_8:13">8:13</span> Wathi kum, Usaya kubuya ubone amasikizi
awenzayo amakhulu kunala.

<span id="an_8:14">8:14</span> Wandisa ekungeneni kwesango lendlu
kaYehova elingasentla; nanko kuhleli abafazi apho, belilela uTamuzi.

<span id="an_8:15">8:15</span> Wathi kum, Ubonile na, nyana womntu?
Usaya kubuya ubone amasikizi awenzayo amakhulu kunala.

<span id="an_8:16">8:16</span> Wandisa entendelezweni ephakathi yendlu
kaYehova: nanko, ekungeneni etempileni kaYehova, phakathi kwevaranda
nesibingelelo, kukho amadoda angathi angamashumi amabini anamahlanu,
eyinikele umva itempile kaYehova, ubuso bawo bubheke empumalanga;
aqubuda kwilanga, ebheke empumalanga.

<span id="an_8:17">8:17</span> Wathi kum, Ubonile na, nyana womntu?
Kuncinane na kwindlu kaYuda ukuwenza la masikizi bawenzayo apha, ukuba
ke balizalise ilizwe nangogonyamelo, babuye bandiqumbise? Nabo, besisa
isebe lomdiliya emathatheni abo.

<span id="an_8:18">8:18</span> Nam ndiya kwenza ngobushushu; aliyi kuba
nanceba iliso lam, ndibaconge; nokuba badanduluke ezindlebeni zam ngezwi
elikhulu, andiyi kubeva.

<span id="an_9:1">9:1</span> Wabiza ngelizwi elikhulu ezindlebeni zam,
esithi, Sondelani, baveleli bomzi, elowo ephethe ngesandla izixhobo
zakhe zokutshabalalisa.

<span id="an_9:2">9:2</span> Nanko ke, kusiza amadoda amathandathu
ngendlela yesango eliphezulu, elikhangele entla, iyileyo iphethe
ngesandla izixhobo zayo zokuhlekeza; kukho indoda phakathi kwawo
eyambethe ilinen emhlophe, inezinto zokubhala ethangeni layo; eza ke ema
ecaleni kwesibingelelo sobhedu.

<span id="an_9:3">9:3</span> Ubuqaqawuli bukaThixo kaSirayeli baye
bunyuka, busuka ekerubhini obebuphezu kwayo, baya emnyango wendlu.
Wamemeza endodeni eyambethe ilinen emhlophe, enezinto zokubhala
ethangeni layo.

<span id="an_9:4">9:4</span> Wathi uYehova kuyo, Canda esazulwini somzi,
esazulwini seYerusalem, ubeke uphawu emabunzini amadoda agcunayo,
ancwinayo ngenxa yamasikizi onke awenzekayo esazulwini sayo.

<span id="an_9:5">9:5</span> Wathi kwamanye ezindlebeni zam, Candani
esazulwini somzi emva kwayo, nixabele; malingabi nanceba iliso lenu,
ningabacongi.

<span id="an_9:6">9:6</span> Amaxhego, amadodana nomthinjana, abantwana
nabafazi, babulaleni, ukuze batshabalale; ke bonke abantu abanophawu
olo, musani ukufika kubo; nize niqalele ke engcweleni yam. Aqala ke
ngamadoda amakhulu abephambi kwendlu.

<span id="an_9:7">9:7</span> Wathi ke kuwo, Yenzeni inqambi indlu le,
nizizalise iintendelezo ngababuleweyo; phumani niye. Aphuma ke abulala
kuwo umzi.

<span id="an_9:8">9:8</span> Kwathi, xa ababulalayo, ndisele mna, ndawa
ngobuso, ndakhala, ndathi, Awu! Nkosi Yehova, uya kuwatshabalalisa onke
na amasalela amaSirayeli ngokubuthulula ubushushu bakho phezu
kweYerusalem?

<span id="an_9:9">9:9</span> Wathi kum, Ubugwenxa bendlu kaSirayeli
nobendlu kaYuda bukhulu kakhulu kunene, nelizwe lizele ligazi, nomzi
uzele bubugqwetha; ngokuba besithi, UYehova ulilahlile ilizwe, uYehova
akaboni.

<span id="an_9:10">9:10</span> Ke nam aliyi kuba nanceba iliso lam,
ndibaconge; ndiya kubanika ngokwendlela yabo entlokweni yabo.

<span id="an_9:11">9:11</span> Nantso indoda eyayambethe ilinen
emhlophe, ebinezinto zokubhala ethangeni layo, ibuya nelizwi elithi,
Ndenze njengoko ubundiwisele umthetho ngako.

<span id="an_10:1">10:1</span> Ndabona, nanko, phezu kwesibhakabhaka
esibe siphezu kwentloko yeekerubhi, kunjengelitye lesafire, kubonakala
ngathi ngumfanekiso wetrone; wabonakala phezu kwazo uYehova.

<span id="an_10:2">10:2</span> Wathetha kwindoda eyambethe ilinen
emhlophe, wathi, Yiya phakathi kweevili ezijikelezayo ngaphantsi
kwekerubhi, uzalise izandla zakho ngamalahle omlilo, uwathabathe
phakathi kweekerubhi, uwasasaze phezu kwawo umzi. Yangena ndiyibona.

<span id="an_10:3">10:3</span> Ke iikerubhi bezimi ngasekunene kwendlu,
ekungeneni kwendoda leyo; ilifu layizalisa intendelezo ephakathi.

<span id="an_10:4">10:4</span> Benyuka ubuqaqawuli bukaYehova, besuka
ezikerubhini, baya emnyango wendlu. Yazala indlu lilifu, nentendelezo
yazala bubumhlophe bobuqaqawuli bukaYehova.

<span id="an_10:5">10:5</span> Savakala isandi samaphiko eekerubhi, sada
saya entendelezweni engaphandle, sinjengezwi loSomandla akuthetha.

<span id="an_10:6">10:6</span> Kwathi, akuyiwisela umthetho indoda
eyambethe ilinen emhlophe, esithi, Thabatha umlilo phakathi kweevili
ezijikelezayo, phakathi kweekerubhi, yasuka yangena yema ecaleni
kweevili.

<span id="an_10:7">10:7</span> Ibe isuka ke ikerubhi, isolule isandla
sayo phakathi kweekerubhi, isise emlilweni ophakathi kweekerubhi,
iwuthabathe, iwunikele esandleni sowambethe ilinen emhlophe;
ebewuthabatha ke aphume.

<span id="an_10:8">10:8</span> Kwabonakala ke ezikerubhini into efana
nesandla somntu, phantsi kwamaphiko azo.

<span id="an_10:9">10:9</span> Ndabona, nanzo iivili ezine zisecaleni
leekerubhi, ivili enye isecaleni lekerubhi enye, ivili enye isecaleni
lekerubhi enye, ukubonakala kweevili ngathi yimbonakalo yelitye
lekrizolite.

<span id="an_10:10">10:10</span> Ngokubonakala kwazo zone bezimfani-nye,
kwanga kukho ivili ngaphakathi kwevili.

<span id="an_10:11">10:11</span> Ekuhambeni kwazo zahamba zaya kumacala
azo omane; azajikeleza ekuhambeni kwazo; ngokuba apho sukuba leyo
iphambili ibe ibheka khona, zibe ziyilandela, zingajikelezi ekuhambeni
kwazo.

<span id="an_10:12">10:12</span> Ke umzimba wazo wonke, nomhlana wazo,
nezandla zazo, namaphiko azo, neevili, zibe zizele ngamehlo ngeenxa
zonke; zone bezineevili zazo.

<span id="an_10:13">10:13</span> Iivili ezo zabizwa ezindlebeni zam,
kwathiwa, ziivili ezijikelezayo.

<span id="an_10:14">10:14</span> Inye ibe inobuso obune: ubuso bokuqala
ibubuso bekerubhi, ubuso besibini ibubuso bomntu, obesithathu ibubuso
bengonyama, obesine ibubuso bokhozi.

<span id="an_10:15">10:15</span> Zenyuka iikerubhi; yilaa nto
iphilileyo, ndayibonayo emlanjeni oyiKebhare.

<span id="an_10:16">10:16</span> Ekuhambeni kweekerubhi zahamba iivili
ecaleni lazo; nasekuwaphakamiseni kweekerubhi amaphiko azo, ukuba zisuke
emhlabeni, azijikanga neevili zazo zimke ecaleni lazo.

<span id="an_10:17">10:17</span> Ekumeni kwazo zema nazo; ekusukeni
kwazo ukuba ziphaphazele, zesuka nazo; ngokuba umoya wento ephilileyo
ube ukho kuzo.

<span id="an_10:18">10:18</span> Baphuma ke ubuqaqawuli bukaYehova,
bemka emnyango wendlu, beza kuma phezu kweekerubhi.

<span id="an_10:19">10:19</span> Iikerubhi zawaphakamisa amaphiko azo,
zasuka emhlabeni emehlweni am; ekuphumeni kwazo iivili zazingakuzo. Zema
ekungeneni kwesango lendlu kaYehova elisempumalanga, ubuqaqawuli
bukaThixo kaSirayeli buphezu kwazo ngaphezulu.

<span id="an_10:20">10:20</span> Yilaa nto iiphilileyo, ndayibonayo
phantsi koThixo kaSirayeli emlanjeni oyiKebhare; ndazi ke ukuba
ziziikerubhi.

<span id="an_10:21">10:21</span> Inye ibe inobuso obune inye ibe
inamaphiko amane, imfano yezandla zomntu ingaphantsi kwamaphiko azo.

<span id="an_10:22">10:22</span> Ke imfano yobuso bazo, ibe ibobaa buso
ndabubonayo imlanjeni oyiKebhare, nokubonakala kwazo nazo ngokwazo; zibe
zihamba iyileyo iye kwicala elikhangelene nobuso bayo.

<span id="an_11:1">11:1</span> Wandifunqula uMoya, wandisa esangweni
lendlu kaYehova langasempumalanga, elibheke empumalanga; nanko,
ekungeneni kwesango, kukho amadoda engamashumi amabini anamahlanu.
Ndabona phakathi kwawo uYazaniya unyana ka-Azure, noPelatiya unyana
kaBhenaya, abathetheli babantu.

<span id="an_11:2">11:2</span> Wathi kum, Nyana womntu, ngawo la amadoda
acinga inkohlakalo, aceba amacebo amabi kulo mzi;

<span id="an_11:3">11:3</span> atshoyo ukuthi, Alikasondeli ixesha
lokwakha izindlu; lo mzi yimbiza, thina ke siyinyama.

<span id="an_11:4">11:4</span> Ngako oko profetela kuwo, profeta, nyana
womntu.

<span id="an_11:5">11:5</span> Wandiwela ke uMoya kaYehova, wathi kum,
Yithi, Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Nitshilo nina, ndlu kaSirayeli; nezinto
ezithe qatha emoyeni wenu ndiyazazi mna.

<span id="an_11:6">11:6</span> Ndibandisile ababuleweyo benu kulo mzi,
nazizalisa izitrato zawo ngababuleweyo.

<span id="an_11:7">11:7</span> Ngako oko itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ababuleweyo benu, ebe nibabeka phantsi phakathi kwawo umzi, bayinyama,
wona ke uyimbiza; nina niya kukhutshwa phakathi kwawo.

<span id="an_11:8">11:8</span> Niyaloyika ikrele; ndiya kunizisela
ikrele, itsho iNkosi;

<span id="an_11:9">11:9</span> ndinikhuphe phakathi kwawo, ndininikele
esandleni sabasemzini, ndizenze izigwebo kuni.

<span id="an_11:10">11:10</span> Niya kuwa likrele; ndiya kunigweba
emdeni wakwaSirayeli; nazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_11:11">11:11</span> Wona lo mzi awuyi kuba yimbiza kuni,
aniyi kuba yinyama nina phakathi kwawo; ndiya kunigweba emdeni
wakwaSirayeli,

<span id="an_11:12">11:12</span> nazi ukuba ndinguYehova; imimiselo yam
anihambanga ngayo, namasiko am anawenza; nesuka nenza ngokwamasiko
eentlanga ezingeenxa zonke kuni.

<span id="an_11:13">11:13</span> Kwathi ke ndakuprofeta, wafa uPelatiya
unyana kaBhenaya. Ndawa ngobuso bam, ndakhala ngelizwi elikhulu, ndathi,
Awu! Nkosi Yehova! Uyawagqibela kuphele na wena amasalela akwaSirayeli?

<span id="an_11:14">11:14</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_11:15">11:15</span> Nyana womntu, abazalwana bakho,
abazalwana bakho ngamadoda akowenu, nendlu yonke yakwaSirayeli yonke
iphela, yona leyo bathi ngayo abemi baseYerusalem, Bakude kuYehova;
linikwe thina ilizwe ukuze sime kulo.

<span id="an_11:16">11:16</span> Ngako oko yithi, Itsho iNkosi uYehova
ukuthi, Ekubeni ndibakhwelelisele ezintlangeni, ndabaphangalalisa
emazweni, ke ndoba yingcwele kubo umzuzwana omncinane kuloo mazwe baye
kuwo.

<span id="an_11:17">11:17</span> Ngako oko yithi, Itsho iNkosi uYehova
ukuthi, Ndiya kunibutha ezizweni, ndinihlanganise emazweni enilusali
kuwo, ndininike umhlaba wakwaSirayeli.

<span id="an_11:18">11:18</span> Baya kufika kuwo, bazisuse kuwo zonke
izinto zawo ezinezothe, namasikizi awo onke.

<span id="an_11:19">11:19</span> Ndobanika ntliziyo yimbi, ndibeke umoya
omtsha ngaphakathi kwenu; ndiyisuse intliziyo yelitye enyameni yabo,
ndibanike intliziyo yenyama;

<span id="an_11:20">11:20</span> ukuze bahambe ngemimiselo yam, bagcine
amasiko am bawenze, babe ngabantu bam, mna ndibe nguThixo wabo.

<span id="an_11:21">11:21</span> Ke bona abantliziyo ihamba
ngokwentliziyo yezinto zabo ezinezothe, nezingamasikizi abo, ndiya
kubanika ngokwendlela yabo entlokweni yabo; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_11:22">11:22</span> Iikerubhi zawaphakamisa amaphiko azo,
kwaneevili ezingakuzo; ubuqaqawuli bukaThixo kaSirayeli baba phezu kwazo
ngaphezulu.

<span id="an_11:23">11:23</span> Benyuka ubuqaqawuli bukaYehova, besuka
phakathi komzi, bema entabeni engasempumalanga kuwo umzi.

<span id="an_11:24">11:24</span> UMoya wandifunqula, wandisa
kwelamaKaledi kubathinjwa, ndisembonweni ngoMoya kaThixo. Wenyuka wemka
kum umbono ebendiwubona.

<span id="an_11:25">11:25</span> Ndathetha kubathinjwa onke amazwi
kaYehova, abendibonisile.

<span id="an_12:1">12:1</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_12:2">12:2</span> Nyana womntu, uhleli phakathi kwendlu
eneenkani; banamehlo okubona, ababoni; baneendlebe zokuva, abeva;
ngokuba bayindlu eneenkani.

<span id="an_12:3">12:3</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, zilungiselele
iimpahla zemfuduka, ufuduke emini emehlweni abo, ufuduke endaweni yakho,
uye ndaweni yimbi emehlweni abo, mhlawumbi bobona; ngokuba bayindlu
eneenkani.

<span id="an_12:4">12:4</span> Uze uyikhuphe impahla yakho ngokwempahla
yemfuduka emini, emehlweni abo; ke wena uphume ngokuhlwa emehlweni abo,
njengokuphuma kwabathinjwa.

<span id="an_12:5">12:5</span> Gqobhoza eludongeni emehlweni abo,
uyikhuphe ngakhona.

<span id="an_12:6">12:6</span> Yithwale ngamagxa emehlweni abo, yikhuphe
kwakuba mnyama; bugqubuthele ubuso bakho, ungalikhangeli ilizwe; ngokuba
ndikwenze isimanga kwindlu kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_12:7">12:7</span> Ndenjenjalo, njengoko ndawiselwa umthetho
ngako; ndayikhupha emini impahla yam ngokwempahla yemfuduka; ngokuhlwa
ndazigqobhozela eludongeni ngesandla, ndayikhupha kwakuba mnyama,
ndayithwala ngamagxa eme hlweni abo.

<span id="an_12:8">12:8</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum kusasa,
lisithi,

<span id="an_12:9">12:9</span> Nyana womntu, indlu kaSirayeli, indlu
eneenkani, ayitshongo na kuwe ukuthi, Wenza ntoni na?

<span id="an_12:10">12:10</span> Yithi kubo, Itsho iNkosi uYehova
ukuthi, Esi sihlabo sisingisele kwisikhulu esiseYerusalem, nakwindlu
yonke kaSirayeli, abaphakathi kwayo abathinjiweyo.

<span id="an_12:11">12:11</span> Yithi, Ndisisimanga kuni; njengoko
ndenze ngako, kuya kwenzeka ngokunjalo kubo; baya kufuduswa, bathinjwe.

<span id="an_12:12">12:12</span> Isikhulu esiphakathi kwabo siya
kuyithwala ngamagxa kuthe thsu mnyama, siphume; baya kugqobhoza
eludongeni ukuba bayikhuphe ngakhona; siya kugqubuthela ubuso baso sona,
kuba singayi kulikhangela ilizwe ngamehlo.

<span id="an_12:13">12:13</span> Ndiya kuwutwabulula umnatha wam phezu
kwaso, sibanjiswe ngumgibe wam, ndisise eBhabheli, ezweni lamaKaledi; ke
asiyi kulibona, noko siya kufela khona.

<span id="an_12:14">12:14</span> Ndiya kukuchithachitha emimoyeni yonke
konke esiphahlwe kuko, abancedisi baso namahlelo aso onke, ndirhole
ikrele emva kwabo;

<span id="an_12:15">12:15</span> bazi ukuba ndinguYehova,
ekubaphangalaliseni kwam ezintlangeni, ndibachithachithe emazweni.

<span id="an_12:16">12:16</span> Ndoshiya kubo amadoda ambalwa, asinde
ekreleni, nasendlaleni, nasendyikityeni yokufa; ukuze bawabalise
amasikizi abo onke ezintlangeni abaye kuzo; bazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_12:17">12:17</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_12:18">12:18</span> Nyana womntu, wosidla isonka sakho
ungcangcazela, uwasele amanzi akho ugungqa, unesithukuthezi.

<span id="an_12:19">12:19</span> Wothi ke kubantu belizwe, Itsho iNkosi
uYehova ngokusingisele kubemi baseYerusalem, emhlabeni wakwaSirayeli,
ukuthi, Isonka sabo bosidla benesithukuthezi, bawasele amanzi abo
bemangalisiwe; ukuze ezweni labo kube senkangala, ingabikho inzaliseko
yalo ngenxa yogonyamelo lwabo bonke abahleli kulo.

<span id="an_12:20">12:20</span> Yoba ngamanxuwa imizi emiweyo, kube
senkangala elizweni; nazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_12:21">12:21</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_12:22">12:22</span> Nyana womntu, uyintoni na lo mzekeliso
ninawo emhlabeni wakwaSirayeli, wokuthi, Imihla iyoluka, iyadaka imibono
yonke?

<span id="an_12:23">12:23</span> Ngako oko yithi kubo, Itsho iNkosi
uYehova ukuthi, Ndiya kuwenza uphele lo mzekeliso, bangabi sazekelisa
ngawo kwaSirayeli; ke, yithi kubo, Isondele imihla, nesiphelo semibono
yonke.

<span id="an_12:24">12:24</span> Ngokuba akuyi kuba sabakho namnye
umbono okhohlakeleyo, nokuvumisa okucengacengayo, phakathi kwendlu
kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_12:25">12:25</span> Ngokuba ndinguYehova, ndiya kuthetha;
ilizwi endisukuba ndilithetha liya kwenzeka, lingayi kulibala; ngokuba
ngemihla yenu, ndlundini ineenkani, ndithetha ilizwi, ndilenze; itsho
iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_12:26">12:26</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_12:27">12:27</span> Nyana womntu, yabona, indlu kaSirayeli
ithi, Umbono awubonayo yena lo, ngowemihla emininzi; uprofetele amaxesha
akude.

<span id="an_12:28">12:28</span> Ngako oko yithi kubo, Itsho iNkosi
uYehova ukuthi, Akayi kuba salityaziswa onke amazwi am; ilizwi
endisukuba ndilithetha liya kwenzeka; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_13:1">13:1</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_13:2">13:2</span> Nyana womntu, profeta uchase abaprofeti
bakwaSirayeli abaprofetayo, uthi kwabaprofeta okwentliziyo yabo, Liveni
ilizwi likaYehova.

<span id="an_13:3">13:3</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Yeha ke,
abaprofeti abanobudenge, abalandela owabo umoya, nento abangayibonanga!

<span id="an_13:4">13:4</span> Baba njengeempungutye emanxuweni
abaprofeti bakho, Sirayeli.

<span id="an_13:5">13:5</span> Aninyukanga niye emathutyeni, niyibiyele
ngodonga indlu kaSirayeli, ukuze nakhe uluhlu lokulwa ngomhla kaYehova.

<span id="an_13:6">13:6</span> Babona into ekhohlakeleyo nokuvumisa
okungamanga, abo bathi, Utsho uYehova; uYehova engabathumanga, ukanti
balinda ukuqiniswa kwelo lizwi.

<span id="an_13:7">13:7</span> Anibonanga mbono wankohlakalo na,
nakuvumisa okungamanga na, nisithi nje, Utsho uYehova; ndingathethanga
mna?

<span id="an_13:8">13:8</span> Ngako oko itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ngenxa yokuba nithethe into ekhohlakeleyo, nibona amanga, ngako oko,
yabonani, ndinichasile; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_13:9">13:9</span> Isandla sam sichasa abaprofeti ababona
into ekhohlakeleyo, bavumise amanga. Abayi kubakho ekucweyweni kwabantu
bam, bangabhalwa encwadini yomlibo wendlu kaSirayeli, bangangeni
emhlabeni wakwaSirayeli; nazi ukuba ndiyiNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_13:10">13:10</span> Ngenxa yokuba, ewe, ngenxa yokuba
bebandwendwisile abantu bam, besithi, Luxolo, kungekho luxolo; bathi,
bakwakha udonga bona, yabona, abaya balutyabeka ngodaka oluhlephukayo:

<span id="an_13:11">13:11</span> yithi kwabatyabeka ngodaka
oluhlephukayo, Luya kuwa; kuza isiphango esikhukulayo; nina ke, matye
esichotho, yiwani; wena moya usisaqhwithi, ovuthuvuthuzayo, qhutha.

<span id="an_13:12">13:12</span> Xa ke luthe lwawa udonga, akuyi kuthiwa
na kuni, Kuphi na ukutyabeka enatyabeka ngako?

<span id="an_13:13">13:13</span> Ngako oko itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ndiya kuqhuthisa umoya ovuthuvuthuzayo ngobushushu bam; kuze nesiphango
esikhukulayo ngomsindo wam, namatye ezichotho ngobushushu, ukuze
kugqityelwe kuphele.

<span id="an_13:14">13:14</span> Ndiya kulugungxula udonga enalutyabeka
ngodaka oluhlephukayo, ndiluwise emhlabeni, sityhilekile isiseko salo,
luwe, niphelele kweso sithuba salo; nazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_13:15">13:15</span> Ndobuphelelisela eludongeni ubushushu
bam, nakwabatyabeka ngodaka oluhlephukayo, ndithi kuni, Alusekho udonga,
abasekho abatyabeki balo,

<span id="an_13:16">13:16</span> abaprofeti bakwaSirayeli ababeprofeta
ngeYerusalem, ababebona umbono woxolo, kungekho luxolo; itsho iNkosi
uYehova.

<span id="an_13:17">13:17</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, bhekisa ubuso
bakho kwiintombi zabantu bakowenu, eziprofeta okweentliziyo zazo.

<span id="an_13:18">13:18</span> Uze uprofete ngazo, uthi, Itsho iNkosi
uYehova ukuthi, Yeha ke, abo bathunga izibophelelo ezihlahleni zezandla
zonke, benze izigubungelo ezilingene iintloko zonke, ukuze bathiyele
imiphefumlo! Nithiyele imiphefumlo yabantu bam, nasindisa eyenu
imiphefumlo.

<span id="an_13:19">13:19</span> Nindihlambele kubantu bam ngenxa
yerhasi esutywe ngezandla, nangenxa yamaqhekeza esonka, ukuze nibulale
imiphefumlo ebingeyakufa, nisindise imiphefumlo ebingeyakusindiswa,
ngamanga enu ebantwini bam abava amanga.

<span id="an_13:20">13:20</span> Ngako oko itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Yabonani, ndizichasile izibophelelo zenu, enithiyela ngazo imiphefumlo
njengeentaka. Ndiya kuziqhawula ezingalweni zenu, ndiyindulule
imiphefumlo, kwaimiphefumlo eniyithiyeleyo njengeentaka.

<span id="an_13:21">13:21</span> Ndozikrazula izigubungelo zenu,
ndibahlangule abantu bam esandleni senu, bangabi saba yinto ethiyelwayo
esandleni senu; nazi ukubandinguYehova.

<span id="an_13:22">13:22</span> Ngenxa enokuba niyenze buhlungu
ngobuxoki intliziyo yelungisa, endingalenzanga buhlungu mna; nazomeleza
izandla zongendawo, ukuze angabuyi endleleni yakhe embi, asindiswe:

<span id="an_13:23">13:23</span> ngako oko aniyi kuyibona into
ekhohlakeleyo ningabi savumisa nokuvumisa; ngokuba ndiya kubahlangula
abantu bam esandleni senu; nazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_14:1">14:1</span> Kwafika kum amadoda akumadoda amakhulu
akwaSirayeli, ahlala phantsi phambi kwam.

<span id="an_14:2">14:2</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_14:3">14:3</span> Nyana womntu, la madoda anyuse izigogo
zawo ezintliziyweni zawo, amisa isikhubekiso sokuba abe gwenxa phambi
kobuso bawo; ndingaquqelwa ndiquqelwe ngawo na?

<span id="an_14:4">14:4</span> Ngako oko thetha nawo, uthi kuwo, Itsho
iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Elowo nalowo wasendlwini kaSirayeli, othe wanyusa
izigodo zakhe entliziyweni yakhe, wamisa isikhubekiso sokuba abe gwenxa
phambi kobuso bakhe, weza kubaprofeti: mna Yehova ndoba ngomphendulayo
ngokwam, ngokobuninzi bezigodo zakhe;

<span id="an_14:5">14:5</span> ukuze ndiyixhakamfule indlu kaSirayeli
ngentliziyo yabo, ekubeni beshenxile kum bonke bephela ngezigodo zabo.

<span id="an_14:6">14:6</span> Ngako oko yithi kwindlu kaSirayeli, Itsho
iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Buyani nizibuyise ezigodweni zenu, nibubuyise
ubuso benu kumasikizi enu onke.

<span id="an_14:7">14:7</span> Ngokuba elowo nalowo wasendlwini
kaSirayeli, nowasemzini ophambukele kwaSirayeli, othe wazahlula
ekundilandeleni kwakhe, wanyusa izigodo zakhe entliziyweni yakhe, wamisa
isikhubekiso sokuba abe gwenxa phambi kobuso bakhe, weza kumprofeti
ukuze aquqele kum ngenxa yakhe: mna Yehova ndomphendula ngokwam.

<span id="an_14:8">14:8</span> Ndoyichasa loo ndoda, ndiyiphanzise ibe
ngumqondiso nomzekeliso, ndimnqumle ebantwini bam; nazi ukuba
ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_14:9">14:9</span> Umprofeti, xa athe warhwebeshwa, wathetha
ilizwi, mna Yehova ndimrhwebeshile loo mprofeti: ndosolula isandla sam
phezu kwakhe, ndimtshabalalise phakathi kwabantu bam amaSirayeli.

<span id="an_14:10">14:10</span> Baya kubuthwala ubugwenxa babo;
njengoko bunjalo ubugwenxa boquqela kuye, buya kuba njalo ubugwenxa
bomprofeti lowo;

<span id="an_14:11">14:11</span> ukuze indlu kaSirayeli ingabi
sandwendwa imke ekundilandeleni kwayo; bangabi sazenza iinqambi
ngezikreqo zabo zonke; babe ngabantu bam, ndibe nguThixo wabo; itsho
iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_14:12">14:12</span> Kwafika kum ilizwi likaYehova, lisithi,

<span id="an_14:13">14:13</span> Nyana womntu, xa ilizwe lithe lona kum
lameneza ngobumenemene, ndasolula isandla sam phezu kwalo, ndawaphula
kulo umsimelelo osisonka, ndathumela kulo indlala, ndanqumla kulo umntu
nenkomo;

<span id="an_14:14">14:14</span> ekho phakathi kwalo la madoda
omathathu, ooNowa noDaniyeli noYobhi, wona abeya kuhlangula owawo
umphefumlo kuphela ngobawo ubulungisa; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_14:15">14:15</span> Ndingafanelana ndicandisa amarhamncwa
ezweni, alihlutha abantwana, kwaba senkangala kulo, akwabakho unokucanda
kulo ngenxa yamarhamncwa lawo;

<span id="an_14:16">14:16</span> ekho phakathi kwalo loo madoda
omathathu: ndihleli nje, itsho iNkosi, ebengayi kuhlangula nanyana
nantombi; ebeya kuhlanguleka odwa; ke bekuya kuba senkangala ezweni elo.

<span id="an_14:17">14:17</span> Nokuba ndithe ndalizisela ikrele elo
lizwe, ndathi ikrele malicande kwelo lizwe, ndanqamla kulo umntu
nenkomo;

<span id="an_14:18">14:18</span> ekho phakathi kwalo loo madoda
omathathu: ndihleli nje, itsho iNkosi uYehova, ebengayi kuhlangula nyana
nantombi; ngokuba ebeya kuhlanguleka wona odwa.

<span id="an_14:19">14:19</span> Nokuba ndithe ndathumela indyikitya
yokufa kwelo zwe, ndathulula ubushushu bam phezu kwalo ngegazi, ukuze
ndinqumle kulo umntu nenkomo;

<span id="an_14:20">14:20</span> bekho phakathi kwalo ooNowa noDaniyeli
noYobhi: ndihleli nje, itsho iNkosi uYehova bebengayi kuhlangula nyana
nantombi; bona bebeya kuhlangula owabo umphefumlo kuphela ngobabo
ubulungisa.

<span id="an_14:21">14:21</span> Ngokuba itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Kobeka phi na ke, xa ndithe ndathumela eYerusalem zozine izigwebo zam
ezibi, ikrele, nendlala, namarhamncwa, nendyikitya yokufa, ukuze
kunqumke kuyo umntu nenkomo?

<span id="an_14:22">14:22</span> Yabonani ke, kuya kusala kuyo
abasindileyo, abaya kukhutshwa, abangoonyana neentombi; yabonani, baya
kuphuma beze kuni, niyibone indlela yabo neentlondi zabo; nithuthuzeleke
ngenxa yobubi endayizisela bona iYerusalem, ngenxa yento yonke
endayizisela yona.

<span id="an_14:23">14:23</span> Baya kunithuthuzela, xa niyibonayo
indlela yabo neentlondi zabo; nazi ukuba andifumananga ndikwenze konke
endakwenzayo kuyo; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_15:1">15:1</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_15:2">15:2</span> Nyana womntu, umthi womdiliya uyidlula
ngantoni na yonke eminye imithi, isebe lomdiliya eliphakathi kwemithi
yehlathi?

<span id="an_15:3">15:3</span> Kukha kuthatyathwe umthi yini na kuwo
wokusebenza umsebenzi? Kukha kuthatyathwe nesikhonkwane na kuwo,
sokuxhoma iimpahla nokuba ziziphi?

<span id="an_15:4">15:4</span> Yabona, ufakwa emlilweni ukuba uwutshise;
umlilo utshisa iincam zawo zombini, sirhawuke isibili sawo; wowulungela
na ke umsebenzi?

<span id="an_15:5">15:5</span> Yabona, oko ube usewonke,
ubungenamsebenzi; wobeka phi na ke ukungabi namsebenzi, xa uthe
watshiswa ngumlilo, warhawuka?

<span id="an_15:6">15:6</span> Ngako oko itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Njengomthi womdiliya phakathi kwemithi yehlathi, endiwufaka emlilweni
ukuze utshiswe, ndenjenjalo ukubabeka emlilweni abemi baseYerusalem,
Ndiya kubachasa;

<span id="an_15:7">15:7</span> baya kuphuma emlilweni, umlilo uya
kubatshisa; nazi ukuba ndinguYehova ekubachaseni kwam.

<span id="an_15:8">15:8</span> Ndiya kwenza elizweni kube senkangala,
ngenxa yokuba bemenezile ngobumenemene; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_16:1">16:1</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_16:2">16:2</span> Nyana womntu, yazise iYerusalem amasikizi
ayo, uthi,

<span id="an_16:3">16:3</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova kwiYerusalem,
ukuthi, Ukuvela kwakho nokuzalwa kwakho kokwasezweni lamaKanan; uyihlo
waye engumAmori, unyoko waye engumHetikazi.

<span id="an_16:4">16:4</span> Ukuzalwa kwakho ke, ngemini yokuzalwa
kwakho ayinqunyulwanga imfesane yakho, akuhlanjwanga ngamanzi ukuba
usuleke, akuhlikihlwanga ngatyuwa, akusongelwanga zisongelweni.

<span id="an_16:5">16:5</span> Akubangakho liso linenceba kuwe, ukuze
wenzelwe noko inye kwezo zinto, ngokuba nofefe kuwe; walahlelwa endle
ngokucatshukelwa kwakho ngemini yokuzalwa kwakho.

<span id="an_16:6">16:6</span> Ndagqitha kuwe, ndakubona ugqushagqusha
egazini lakhe, ndathi kuwe, Usegazini lakho njalo, phila; usegazini
lakho njalo, phila!

<span id="an_16:7">16:7</span> Ndakwenza waba yinyambalala,
njengokuntshula kwentsimi; wanda, wakhula, wafika entlahleni yezidlele;
waphuma amabele, bahluma uboya bakho; waye ke wena uze kanye.

<span id="an_16:8">16:8</span> Ke kaloku ndagqitha kuwe, ndakubona, nalo
ixesha lakho lilixesha lothando. Ndatwabulula isondo lengubo yam phezu
kwakho, ndabugubungela ubuze bakho; ndakufungela, ndanqophisana nawe,
itsho iNkosi uYehova; waba ngowam ke.

<span id="an_16:9">16:9</span> Ke ndakuhlamba ngamanzi, ndakuhlambulula
amagazi akho, ndakuthambisa ngeoli.

<span id="an_16:10">16:10</span> Ndakwambesa ngeengubo ezimfakamfele,
ndakunxiba izixathula zesikhumba sehlengezi; ndakujikelisa intloko
ngelinen ecikizekileyo, ndakugqubuthela ngesilika.

<span id="an_16:11">16:11</span> Ndakuvathisa ngesivatho, ndakufaka
izacholo ezihlahleni, nemixokelelwane emqaleni wakho.

<span id="an_16:12">16:12</span> Ndakunika ikhonkco lempumlo, namajikazi
ezindlebeni zakho, nesithsaba sokuhomba entloko.

<span id="an_16:13">16:13</span> Wavatha ke igolide nesilivere,
nezambatho zakho zaba zezelinen ecikizekileyo, nezesilika,
nezimfakamfele. Wadla umgubo ocoliweyo, nobusi, neoli; waba mhle kakhulu
kunene, waya uphumelela ebukumkanini.

<span id="an_16:14">16:14</span> Lwaphuma udumo lobuhle bakho lwagqiba
ilizwe lonke; ngokuba bapheleliseka bona ngobungangamela bam, endabubeka
phezu kwakho; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_16:15">16:15</span> Wesuka wena wakholosa ngobuhle bakho,
wahenyuza ngenxa yodumo lwakho; ubuhenyu bakho wabuthululela phezu kwabo
bonke abadlulayo, waba ngowabo.

<span id="an_16:16">16:16</span> Wathabatha ezingutyeni zakho; iziganga
wazenzela iintente ezirhwexu, wahenyuza phezu kwazo; into ebe ingafanele
kuza, ebe ingafanele kubakho.

<span id="an_16:17">16:17</span> Wathabatha iimpahla zakho zokuhomba
zegolide yam, nezesilivere yam endakunikayo, wazenzela imifanekiso
engamadoda, wahenyuza nayo.

<span id="an_16:18">16:18</span> Wathabatha iingubo zakho ezimfakamfele,
wayigubungela ngazo; neoli yam nesiqhumiso sam wasibeka phambi kwayo.

<span id="an_16:19">16:19</span> Isonka sam endakunikayo, nomgubo
ocoliweyo, neoli, nobusi, izinto endakudlisayo zona, wazibeka phambi
kwayo, ukuba zibe livumba elithozamisayo. Kwaba njalo; itsho iNkosi
uYehova.

<span id="an_16:20">16:20</span> Wathabatha oonyana bakho neentombi
zakho, owazizalela mna, wabingelela ngazo kuyo ukuba idle. Bebubuncinane
na ke ubuhenyu bakho,

<span id="an_16:21">16:21</span> ukuba nje ubasike oonyana bam,
ubanikele ngokubacandisa bona emlilweni ngenxa yayo?

<span id="an_16:22">16:22</span> Emasikizini akho onke, nasebuhenywini
bakho, akuyikhumbulanga imihla yobuncinane bakho, oko ubuze kanye,
ugqushagqusha egazini lakho.

<span id="an_16:23">16:23</span> Kwaza kwathi, emva kwezo nto zakho
zonke ezimbi (yeha! yeha ke wena! itsho iNkosi uYehova),

<span id="an_16:24">16:24</span> wazakhela amanqugwala, wazenzela
iindawo eziphakamileyo ezitratweni zonke.

<span id="an_16:25">16:25</span> Emantloko eendlela zonke wazakhela
iindawo zakho eziphakamileyo, wabenza ubuhle bakho balisikizi, wayithi
qheke imilenze yakho kubo bonke abadlula ngendlela, wabandisa ubuhenyu
bakho.

<span id="an_16:26">16:26</span> Wahenyuza noonyana bamaYiputa,
abamelwane bakho abakhulu ngenyama; wabandisa ke ubuhenyu bakho ukuze
undiqumbise.

<span id="an_16:27">16:27</span> Yabona, ndasolula phezu kwakho isandla
sam, ndawunciphisa umamkeliso owumiselweyo, ndakunikela elitheni
labakuthiyayo, kweleentombi zamaFilisti, ezibe ziyidanele indlela yakho
yamanyala.

<span id="an_16:28">16:28</span> Wahenyuza noonyana baseAsiriya, ngenxa
yokuba unganelanga; wahenyuza ke nabo, akwanela noko.

<span id="an_16:29">16:29</span> Wabandisela ezweni lamaKanan ubuhenyu
bakho kwelamaKaledi, akwanela nayiloo nto.

<span id="an_16:30">16:30</span> Hayi, ukuthamba kwentliziyo yakho!
itsho iNkosi uYehova; ukuba wenze zonke ezo zinto, imisebenzi yenkazana
ehenyuzayo, esileyo.

<span id="an_16:31">16:31</span> Ekwakheni kwakho amanqugwala emantloko
eendlela zonke, nasekwenzeni kwakho iindawo zakho eziphakamileyo
ezitratweni zonke, akubanga njengehenyukazi eli, ngokusuka uwucukuceze
umvuzo wobuhenyu.

<span id="an_16:32">16:32</span> Umfazi okrexezayo wamkela abasemzini,
noko angumkamntu.

<span id="an_16:33">16:33</span> Onke amahenyukazi bawanika izipho; ke
wena wazinika zonke izithandane zakho izipho zakho, wazicenga ukuze zize
kuwe ngeenxa zonke ekuhenyuzeni kwakho.

<span id="an_16:34">16:34</span> Wena okwakho ukuhenyuza kuthe
kwaphambana nokwamankazana, ngokuthi ingabi nguwe olandelwayo
ekuhenyuzeni; ngokuthi urhole wena umvuzo wobuhenyu, ungarholelwa umvuzo
wobuhenyu; waba ngophambileyo ke.

<span id="an_16:35">16:35</span> Ngako oko, henyukazi, live ilizwi
likaYehova.

<span id="an_16:36">16:36</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ngenxa
enokuba iphalele imali yakho, batyhileka ubuze bakho ngokuhenyuza kwakho
nezithandane zakho, nangenxa yezigodo zonke zamasikizi akho, nangenxa
yamagazi oonyana bakho, owabanikelayo kuzo:

<span id="an_16:37">16:37</span> ngako oko, yabona, ndiya kuzithabatha
zonke izithandane zakho owakholisana nazo, nabo bonke owabathandayo,
ndawonye nabo bonke owabathiyayo, ndibahlanganise, ndikuchase ngeenxa
zonke, ndibutyhile ubuze bakho kubo, babubone ubuze bakho bonke.

<span id="an_16:38">16:38</span> Ndokugweba ngokugwetywa
kwabakrexezikazi nabaphalazi begazi, ndikwenze wena ube ligazi
lobushushu nobukhwele.

<span id="an_16:39">16:39</span> Ndokunikela esandleni sabo,
bawagungxule amanqugwala akho, bazidilize iindawo zakho eziphakamileyo,
bakuhlube iingubo zakho bazithabathe iimpahla zakho zokuhomba, bakushiye
uze kanye.

<span id="an_16:40">16:40</span> Baya kukunyusela ibandla, bakuxulube
ngamatye, bakuxabele ngamakrele abo;

<span id="an_16:41">16:41</span> bazitshise izindlu zakho ngomlilo,
bazenze kuwe izigwebo emehlweni abafazi abaninzi, ndikunqumamise ungabi
saba lihenyu, ungabi, sarhola umvuzo wobuhenyu.

<span id="an_16:42">16:42</span> Ndobupholisela kuwe ubushushu bam,
limke ikhwele lam kuwe, ndizole, ndingabi saqumba.

<span id="an_16:43">16:43</span> Ngenxa enokuba ungayikhumbulanga imihla
yobuncinane bakho, wesuka wangqungisana nam kwezi zinto zonke: yabona,
nam ndikunika ngokwendlela yakho entlokweni yakho, itsho iNkosi uYehova,
ukuze ungenzi manyala angaphezu kwamasikizi akho onke.

<span id="an_16:44">16:44</span> Yabona, bonke abazekelisi baya
kuzekelisa ngawe, besithi, Ifuze unina intombi yakhe.

<span id="an_16:45">16:45</span> Wena uyintombi yonyoko, odimeleyo
yindoda yakhe nabantwana bakhe; wena ungudade woodade benu, abadimeleyo
ngamadoda abo nabantwana babo; unyoko ngumHetikazi, uyihlo ngumAmori.

<span id="an_16:46">16:46</span> Udade wenu omkhulu nguSamari
namagxamesi akhe, ehleli ngasekhohlo kwakho; nomsakwenu omncinane kuwe,
ehleli ngasekunene kwakho, yiSodom namagxamesi ayo.

<span id="an_16:47">16:47</span> Akuhambanga ke ngeendlela zabo, wenze
ngokwamasikizi abo; ukanti ngomzuzwana wonakalise ngaphezu kwabo
ngeendlela zakho zonke.

<span id="an_16:48">16:48</span> Ndihleli nje, itsho iNkosi uYehova,
iSodom umsakwenu, yona namagxamesi ayo, ayenzanga njengoko wenze ngako
wena namagxamesi akho.

<span id="an_16:49">16:49</span> Nabu ke ubugwenxa beSodom umsakwenu;
yabe ilikratshi, nokuhlutha sisonka, nokuchulumacha, yona namagxamesi
ayo; ayabamba ngesandla abaziintsizana nabangamahlwempu.

<span id="an_16:50">16:50</span> Babezidla, besenza amasikizi phambi
kwam; ndabasusa, ndakukubona oko.

<span id="an_16:51">16:51</span> NoSamari akonanga ngokwesiqingatha
sezono zakho; waye wena uwandisile amasikizi akho ngaphezu kwakhe,
wabenza amalungisa odade benu, ngamasikizi akho owenzileyo.

<span id="an_16:52">16:52</span> Nawe, thwala ke ihlazo lakho, olibalele
kodade benu. Ngezono zakho owazenza ngokumasikizi kunabo, ubenze baba
ngamalungisa kunawe; dana ke nawe, ulithwale ihlazo lakho; ekubeni
ubenze amalungisa oodade benu.

<span id="an_16:53">16:53</span> Ekukubuyiseni kwam ukuthinjwa kwabo,
ukuthinjwa kweSodom namagxamesi ayo, nokuthinjwa koSamari namagxamesi
akhe, ndokubuyisa ukuthinjwa okukuthinjwa kwakho phakathi kwabo;

<span id="an_16:54">16:54</span> ukuze ulithwale ihlazo lakho, uzidanele
izinto zonke ozenzileyo, ubathuthuzele.

<span id="an_16:55">16:55</span> Baya kuthi abasakwenu, iSodom
namagxamesi ayo, babuyele kwakwisimo sabo sangaphambili, noSamari
namagxamesi akhe babuyele kwakwisimo sabo sangaphambili, nawe
namagxamesi akho nibuyele kwakwisimo senu sangaphambili.

<span id="an_16:56">16:56</span> ISodom umsakwenu ayibanga sifundo
emlonyeni wakho ngemini yamakratshi akho;

<span id="an_16:57">16:57</span> zingekatyhilwa izinto zakho ezimbi,
njengasexesheni lesingcikivo samagxamesi akwa-Aram nesangeenxa zonke
kuye, samagxamesi amaFilisti, awakucukulayo ngeenxa zonke.

<span id="an_16:58">16:58</span> Amanyala akho namasikizi akho
uwathwele; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_16:59">16:59</span> Ngokuba itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ndenza ke kuwe njengoko wenze ngako wena, osidelileyo isifungo, ukuba
uwaphule umnqophiso.

<span id="an_16:60">16:60</span> Ndiya kuwukhumbula mna umnqophiso wam
nawe ngemihla yobuncinane bakho, ndikumisele umnqophiso ongunaphakade.

<span id="an_16:61">16:61</span> Wozikhumbula iindlela zakho, udane
ekubamkeleni kwakho oodade benu, abakhulu kunawe kunye nabancinane
kunawe; ndikunike babe ziintombi kuwe, noko bengengabomnqophiso wakho.

<span id="an_16:62">16:62</span> Ndowumisa mna umnqophiso wam nawe, wazi
ukuba ndinguYehova;

<span id="an_16:63">16:63</span> ukuze ukhumbule, udane, ungabi saba
nakuvula mlomo ngenxa yehlazo lakho, ekukuxoleleni kwam zonke izinto
ozenzileyo; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_17:1">17:1</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_17:2">17:2</span> Nyana womntu, jika iqhina, uzekelise
ngomzekeliso kwindlu kaSirayeli, uthi,

<span id="an_17:3">17:3</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi: Ixhalanga
elikhulu, elimaphiko makhulu, elintsiba zolukileyo, eliboya buqhamileyo,
buchokochoko, leza eLebhanon, lathabatha amantloko omsedare.

<span id="an_17:4">17:4</span> Laqhawula eliphezulu emahlamvini awo,
lalisa ezweni lakwaKanan, lalimisa emzini wabarhwebi.

<span id="an_17:5">17:5</span> Lacaphula embewini yelo zwe, layifaka
entsimini ehlwayelwayo, layithabatha layisa kumanzi amaninzi, layimisa
ngokomngculuba.

<span id="an_17:6">17:6</span> Yahluma, yaba ngumdiliya onabileyo,
omfuphi, ukuze amasebe awo asinge kulo, neengcambu zawo zibe phantsi
kwalo; waba ngumdiliya ke, wenza amasebe, waqhama amagqabi.

<span id="an_17:7">17:7</span> Kwabakho elinye ixhalanga elikhulu,
elimaphiko makhulu, linoboya obuninzi. Nango lo mdiliya unabela ngakulo
ngeengcambu zawo, ugobela ngakulo amasebe awo, ukuba liwanyele
ezindimeni otyewe kuzo.

<span id="an_17:8">17:8</span> Ubutyelwe entsimini elungileyo wona,
ngasemanzini amaninzi, ukuze wenze amasebe, uxakathe iziqhamo, ukuba ube
ngumdiliya onguwona unguwo.

<span id="an_17:9">17:9</span> Yithi, Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Womila na? Elaa xhalanga aliyi kuzinyothula na iingcambu zawo,
lizinqumle iziqhamo zawo, ubune, athi onke amagqabi amatsha okuhluma
kwawo abune, kungabi nangangalo inkulu nangabantu baninzi, ukuwususa
ezingcanjini zawo?

<span id="an_17:10">17:10</span> Yabona, khona utyelwe, womila na? Awuyi
kubuna ubune na, wakufikelwa lulophu lwasempumalanga? Uya kubunela
ezindimeni ohlume kuzo.

<span id="an_17:11">17:11</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_17:12">17:12</span> Khawuthi kwindlu eneenkani, Anikwazi na
ukuba kuyintoni na oko? Yithi, Yabonani, ukumkani waseBhabheli weza
eYerusalem, wamthabatha ukumkani wayo nabathetheli bayo, wabasa kuye
eBhabheli.

<span id="an_17:13">17:13</span> Wathabatha owasembeweni yokumkani,
wanqophisana naye, wamfungisa; wathabatha iinjengele zelizwe elo;

<span id="an_17:14">17:14</span> ukuze bube bubukumkani obuphantsi,
ukuze bungaziphakamisi, ukuze awugcine umnqophiso wakhe, ukuze ume wona.

<span id="an_17:15">17:15</span> Wasuka ke wagwilika kuye ngokuthuma
abathunywa bakhe eYiputa, ukuze anikwe amahashe nabantu abaninzi. Woba
nempumelelo na? Wosinda na owenze loo nto? Wowaphula umnqophiso, asinde
na ke?

<span id="an_17:16">17:16</span> Ndihleli nje, itsho iNkosi uYehova,
inyaniso, endaweni yokumkani owamenza ukumkani, osifungo asidelileyo,
omnqophiso awaphuleyo, uya kufela kuyo, esazulwini seBhabheli.

<span id="an_17:17">17:17</span> UFaro akayi kumnceda ngampi inkulu
nangasikhungu sikhulu emfazweni, kwakufunjwa udonga lokungqinga,
kwakhiwe inqaba zokubonisela; ukuze inqunyulwe imiphefumlo emininzi.

<span id="an_17:18">17:18</span> Ekubeni esidelile isifungo, ukuba
awaphule umnqophiso, yabona, unike isandla sakhe, waza noko wenza zonke
ezi zinto; akayi kusinda.

<span id="an_17:19">17:19</span> Ngako oko itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ndihleli nje, inyaniso, isifungo sam asidelileyo, nomnqophiso wam
awaphuleyo, ndiya kumnika entlokweni yakhe.

<span id="an_17:20">17:20</span> Ndowutwabulula phezu kwakhe umnatha
wam, abanjiswe ngumgibe wam, ndimse eBhabheli, ndimangalelane naye khona
ngenxa yomenezo lwakhe, andimenezele ngalo.

<span id="an_17:21">17:21</span> Baya kuwa likrele bonke abasabileyo
bakhe emahlelweni akhe onke, namasalela athiwe saa qhu kwimimoya yonke;
nazi ukuba mna Yehova ndithethile.

<span id="an_17:22">17:22</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Mna ndiya
kuthabatha ke ihlamvu emantloko omsedare omde, ndilimise; emahlamvini
awo aphezulu ndiya kuqhawula elithambileyo, ndilityale mna entabeni
ephakamileyo, ende.

<span id="an_17:23">17:23</span> Ndiya kulityala ke entabeni ende
yakwaSirayeli, linyuse amasebe, lixakathe iziqhamo, libe ngumsedare
ongowona unguwo, zihlale phantsi kwawo zonke iintaka zeentlobo
ngeentlobo; ziya kuhlala emthunzini wamasebe awo.

<span id="an_17:24">17:24</span> Iya kwazi yonke imithi yasendle, ukuba
mna Yehova ndiwuthobile umthi ophakamileyo, ndiwuphakamisile umthi
omfuphi; ndiwomisile umthi omanzi, ndiwuqhamisile umthi owomileyo. Mna
Yehova ndithethile, ndenza.

<span id="an_18:1">18:1</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_18:2">18:2</span> Uyintoni na kuni lo mzekeliso, nizekelisa
ngawo emhlabeni wakwaSirayeli, nisithi, ooyise badle iidiliya ezimuncu,
kwaba buthelezi amazinyo oonyana?

<span id="an_18:3">18:3</span> Ndihleli nje, itsho iNkosi uYehova
ukuthi, anisayi kuba sazekelisa ngalo mzekeliso kwaSirayeli.

<span id="an_18:4">18:4</span> Yabonani, yonke imiphefumlo yeyam;
umphefumlo woyise unjengomphefumlo wonyana, yeyam yomibini; umphefumlo
owonayo, kuya kufa wona.

<span id="an_18:5">18:5</span> Umntu xa athe waba lilungisa, wenza
ngokwesiko nangobulungisa;

<span id="an_18:6">18:6</span> akadlela ezintabeni, amehlo akhe
akawaphakamisela kwizigodo zendlu yakwaSirayeli; umfazi wommelwane wakhe
akamenza inqambi, akasondela kumfazi enomzi;

<span id="an_18:7">18:7</span> akamxinzelela phantsi umntu, wasibuyisa
isibambiso sokuboleka kwakhe, akaxhakamfula; wamnika olambileyo isonka
sakhe, wamgubungela oze ngengubo;

<span id="an_18:8">18:8</span> akanikela imali ukuba adle abanye ngayo,
akathabatha nzala yamboleko; wasibuyisa isandla sakhe ekugqwetheni,
wenza ngokwesiko nangenyaniso phakathi kobani nobani;

<span id="an_18:9">18:9</span> wahamba ngemimiselo yam, wagcina amasiko
am, ukuba enze ngenyaniso: ulilungisa, inene uya kuphila; itsho iNkosi
uYehova.

<span id="an_18:10">18:10</span> Ke ethe wazala unyana osisigwinta,
ophalaza igazi, owenza nokuba inye kwezo zinto,

<span id="an_18:11">18:11</span> ke yena ezo nto zonke engazenzanga,
unyana kananjalo odlela ezintabeni, omenza inqambi umfazi wommelwane
wakhe;

<span id="an_18:12">18:12</span> oluxinzelela phantsi usizana nehlwempu,
oxhakamfulayo, ongasibuyisiyo isibambiso; owaphakamisela kwizigodo
amehlo akhe, owenza amasikizi;

<span id="an_18:13">18:13</span> onikela imali ukuba adle abanye ngayo,
othabatha inzala yemboleko: wophila na ke loo nyana? Akayi kuphila;
wenze onke la masikizi; uya kubulawa afe; igazi lakhe liya kuba phezu
kwakhe.

<span id="an_18:14">18:14</span> Yabonani ke, ethe yena lo wazala
unyana, othe wazibona zonke izono zikayise azenzayo, abone ke,
angenjenjalo;

<span id="an_18:15">18:15</span> angadleli ezintabeni, amehlo akhe
angawaphakamiseli kwizigodo zendlu kaSirayeli, umfazi wommelwane wakhe
angamenzi inqambi;

<span id="an_18:16">18:16</span> angamxinzeleli phantsi umntu,
angabambisi ngesibambiso, angaxhakamfuli; isonka sakhe asinike
olambileyo, amgubungele oze ngengubo;

<span id="an_18:17">18:17</span> abuyise isandla sakhe kolusizana;
angadli abanye ngemali, angathabathi nzala yamboleko, wenza ngokwamasiko
am, uhamba ngemimiselo yam: lowo unyana akayi kufa ngobugwenxa bukayise;
inene uya kuphila.

<span id="an_18:18">18:18</span> Uyise yena, ngokokuba ecudisile kakubi,
exhakamfula umzalwana, wenza okungalungileyo phakathi kwabantu bakowabo,
yabonani, uya kufa ngobugwenxa bakhe.

<span id="an_18:19">18:19</span> Ukanti nithi ke, Kungathuba lini na
ukuba unyana angabuthwali ubugwenxa bukavise? Unyana kaloku wenze
ngokwesiko nangobulungisa; uyigcinile yonke imimiselo yam, wayenza;
inene, uya kuphila.

<span id="an_18:20">18:20</span> Umphefumlo owonayo, kuya kufa wona
wodwa. Unyana akayi kuthwala ubugwenxa bukayise, noyise akayi kubuthwala
ubugwenxa bonyana; ubulungisa belungisa buya kuba phezu kwalo,
nokungendawo kongendawo kuya kuba phezu kwakhe.

<span id="an_18:21">18:21</span> Ongendawo ke, xa athe wabuya ezonweni
zakhe zonke azenzileyo, wayigcina yonke imimiselo yam, wenza ngokwesiko
nangobulungisa, inene, uya kuphila; akayi kufa.

<span id="an_18:22">18:22</span> Zonke izikreqo zakhe azenzileyo aziyi
kukhunjulelwa kuye; ngobulungisa bakhe abenzileyo, uya kuphila.

<span id="an_18:23">18:23</span> Kumnandi na kanene kum ukufa
kongendawo? Itsho iNkosi uYehova. Okumnandi kum asikuko na ukuthi abuye
ezindleleni zakhe, aphile?

<span id="an_18:24">18:24</span> Khona ekubuyeni kwelungisa ebulungiseni
balo, lenza ngobugqwetha, ngokwamasikizi awenzileyo ongendawo, lophila
na lona? Yonke imisebenzi yalo yobulungisa elayenzayo ayiyi kukhunjulwa;
ngenxa yobumenemene balo elimeneze ngabo, nangenxa yezono zalo elone
ngazo: ngenxa yezo zinto liya kufa.

<span id="an_18:25">18:25</span> Ukanti nithi ke, Indlela yeNkosi
ayilungelelene. Khanive, ndlu kaSirayeli; indlela yam ayilungelelene,
yini na? Asizezenu na iindlela ezingalungeleleneyo?

<span id="an_18:26">18:26</span> Xa lithe ilungisa labuya ebulungiseni
balo, lenza ngobugqwetha, lofa ngezo zinto; lofa ngobugqwetha balo
elibenzileyo.

<span id="an_18:27">18:27</span> Xa athe ongendawo wabuya kokungendawo
kwakhe akwenzileyo, wenza ngokwesiko nangobulungisa, yena uya
kuwusindisa umphefumlo wakhe.

<span id="an_18:28">18:28</span> Ekubeni ebonile, wabuya ezikreqweni
zakhe zonke azenzileyo, uya kuphila; akayi kufa.

<span id="an_18:29">18:29</span> Ukanti ithi ke indlu kaSirayeli,
Indlela yeNkosi ayilungelelene. Iindlela zam azilungelelene na, ndlu
kaSirayeli? Asizezenu na iindlela ezingalungeleleneyo?

<span id="an_18:30">18:30</span> Ngako oko ndiya kunigweba elowo
ngokwendlela yakhe, ndlu kaSirayeli; itsho iNkosi uYehova. Buyani,
nizibuyise ezikreqweni zenu zonke, bungabi sisikhubekiso ubugwenxa kuni.

<span id="an_18:31">18:31</span> Lahlani zonke izikreqo zenu enikreqe
ngazo, nizenzele intliziyo entsha nomoya omtsha. Yini na ukuba nife,
ndlu kaSirayeli?

<span id="an_18:32">18:32</span> Ngokuba akumnandi kum ukufa kofayo;
itsho iNkosi uYehova. Zibuyiseni ke niphile.

<span id="an_19:1">19:1</span> Wena ke, yenza isijwili ngezikhulu
zakwaSirayeli, uthi,

<span id="an_19:2">19:2</span> Uyintoni na unyoko? Ingonyamakazi,
ebuthume phakathi kweengonyamakazi, ewondlela amathole ayo phakathi
kweengonyama ezintsha.

<span id="an_19:3">19:3</span> Yakhulisa elinye ematholeni ayo, laba
yingonyama entsha, lafunda ukuqwenga iinyamakazi; ladla abantu.

<span id="an_19:4">19:4</span> Iintlanga zahlaba umkhosi ngalo,
labanjiswa emhadini wazo; zalisa ezweni lamaYiputa, lifakwe amakhonkco.

<span id="an_19:5">19:5</span> Yakubona ingonyamakazi ukuba
aliphumeleli, lidakile ithemba layo, yathabatha elinye ematholeni ayo,
yalenza ingonyama entsha.

<span id="an_19:6">19:6</span> Lahambahamba phakathi kweengonyamakazi,
laba yingonyama entsha, lafunda ukuqwenga iinyamakazi; labadla abantu.

<span id="an_19:7">19:7</span> Labazi abahlolokazi babo, layenza
amanxuwa imizi yabo, kwaba senkangala kwilizwe nakwinzaliseko yalo,
ngezwi lokubharhula kwalo.

<span id="an_19:8">19:8</span> Iintlanga zaba ngeenxa zonke emazweni,
zamisa kulo, zawutwabulula phezu kwalo umnatha wazo, labanjiswa emhadini
wazo.

<span id="an_19:9">19:9</span> Zalifaka endlwaneni linamakhonkco zalisa
kukumkani waseBhabheli, zalisa ezimboniselweni, ukuze ilizwi lalo
lingabi savakala ezintabeni zakwaSirayeli.

<span id="an_19:10">19:10</span> Unyoko ubenjengomdiliya, otyelwe
ngasemanzini, ekuphumleni kwakho, waqhama, wanamasebe amaninzi ngenxa
yamanzi amaninzi.

<span id="an_19:11">19:11</span> Waba namasebe aqinileyo okuba ziintonga
zabalawuli. Ubude bawo baphakama baphezulu, phakathi kweengqimba zamafu;
wabonakala ekuphakameni kwawo ngobuninzi bamasebe awo.

<span id="an_19:12">19:12</span> Wanyothulwa ke ngobushushu, wakhahlelwa
emhlabeni, ulophu lwasempumalanga lwazomisa iziqhamo zawo; axhuzulwa oma
amasebe awo aqinileyo, atsha ngumlilo.

<span id="an_19:13">19:13</span> Ngoku ke utyelwe entlango, ezweni
elingumqwebedu, elomileyo.

<span id="an_19:14">19:14</span> Kuphume ke umlilo emahlamvini amasebe
awo, wazitshisa iziqhamo zawo, akwabakho sebe liqinileyo kuwo, lokuba
yintonga yokulawula. Sisijwili ke, saye siya kuba sisijwili.

<span id="an_20:1">20:1</span> Ke kaloku kwathi ngomnyaka wesixhenxe,
ngenyanga yesihlanu, ngolweshumi enyangeni leyo, kwafika amadoda, evela
kumadoda amakhulu akwaSirayeli, ukuba abuzise kuYehova. Ahlala phantsi
phambi kwam.

<span id="an_20:2">20:2</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_20:3">20:3</span> Nyana womntu, thetha namadoda amakhulu
akwaSirayeli, uthi kuwo, Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Nize kubuzisa kum
na? Ndihleli nje, unakanye ukuba ndibuzwe nini; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_20:4">20:4</span> Uza kubagweba na, uza kugweba na, nyana
womntu? Bazise ke amasikizi ooyise.

<span id="an_20:5">20:5</span> Yithi kubo, Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ngemini endamnyulayo uSirayeli, endayiphakamiselayo isandla sam imbewu
yendlu kaYakobi, endazazisayo kubo ezweni laseYiputa, endabapha kamisela
isandla sam, ndisithi, NdinguYehova uThixo wenu:

<span id="an_20:6">20:6</span> ngaloo mini kanye, ndabaphakamisela
isandla sam, ukuze ndibakhuphe ezweni laseYiputa, ndibase ezweni
endabahlolelayo lona, elibaleka amasi nobusi, liligugu kunamazwe onke.

<span id="an_20:7">20:7</span> Ndathi kubo, Lahlani elowo izinto
ezinezothe zamehlo akhe, ningazenzi iinqambi ngezigodo zaseYiputa;
ndinguYehova uThixo wenu.

<span id="an_20:8">20:8</span> Basuka baba neenkani kum, abavuma
ukundiphulaphula, abazilahla elowo izinto ezinezothe zamehlo akhe,
abazishiya izigodo zaseYiputa. Ndathi ke, ndiya kuthulula ubushushu bam
phezu kwabo, ndiwuphelelisele kubo umsindo wam phakathi kwelizwe
laseYiputa.

<span id="an_20:9">20:9</span> Koko ndenzayo ngenxa yegama lam; ukuze
lingahlanjelwa emehlweni eentlanga, ababephakathi kwazo, endazazisa kubo
emehlweni azo, ekubakhupheni kwam ezweni laseYiputa.

<span id="an_20:10">20:10</span> Ndabakhupha ke ezweni laseYiputa,
ndabasa entlango;

<span id="an_20:11">20:11</span> ndabanika imimiselo yam, ndabazisa
namasiko am, awothi umntu ewenzile, aphile ngawo.

<span id="an_20:12">20:12</span> Kananjalo ndabanika iisabatha zam,
ukuba zibe ngumqondiso phakathi kwam nabo, ukuze bazi ukuba mna Yehova
ndiya bangcwalisa.

<span id="an_20:13">20:13</span> Indlu kaSirayeli yesuka yaba neenkani
kum entlango; abahamba ngemimiselo yam; bawacekisa amasiko am, awothi
umntu ewenzile, aphile ngawo; bazihlambela kakhulu iisabatha zam. Ndathi
ke, ndiya kuthulula ubushushu bam phezu kwabo entlango, ukuze
ndibagqibele.

<span id="an_20:14">20:14</span> Koko ndenzayo ngenxa yegama lam; ukuze
lingahlanjelwa emehlweni eentlanga, endabakhuphayo emehlweni azo.

<span id="an_20:15">20:15</span> Kananjalo mna ndabaphakamisela isandla
entlango, ukuba ndingabasi ezweni endandibanikile, elibaleka amasi
nobusi, liligugu kunamazwe onke;

<span id="an_20:16">20:16</span> ngenxa yokuba bawacekisayo amasiko am,
abahamba ngemimiselo yam, bazihlambela iisabatha zam; ngokuba intliziyo
yabo yazilandela izigodo zabo.

<span id="an_20:17">20:17</span> Koko laba nenceba iliso lam kubo, ukuba
ndingabatshabalalisi, ndingabagqibeli entlango.

<span id="an_20:18">20:18</span> Ndathi ke koonyana babo entlango,
Musani ukuhamba ngemimiselo yooyihlo, ningawagcini amasiko abo,
ningazenzi iinqambi ngezigodo zabo.

<span id="an_20:19">20:19</span> Mna Yehova ndinguThixo wenu; hambani
ngemimiselo yam, niwagcine amasiko am, niwenze;

<span id="an_20:20">20:20</span> nizingcwalise iisabatha zam, zibe
ngumqondiso phakathi kwam nani, ukuze nazi ukuba ndinguYehova uThixo
wenu.

<span id="an_20:21">20:21</span> Basuka oonyana baba neenkani kum;
abahamba ngemimiselo yam, abawagcina amasiko am ukuba bawenze, awothi
umntu ewenzile aphile ngawo; bazihlambela iisabatha zam. Ndathi ke,
ndiya kuthulula ubushushu bam phezu kwabo, ndiphelelisele umsindo wam
kubo entlango.

<span id="an_20:22">20:22</span> Koko ndasibuyisayo isandla sam, ndenza
ngenxa yegama lam, ukuba lingahlanjelwa emehlweni eentlanga,
endabakhuphayo emehlweni azo.

<span id="an_20:23">20:23</span> Kananjalo ndabaphakamisela isandla sam
entlango, ukuba ndibachithachithe ezintlangeni, ndibaphangalalisele
emazweni;

<span id="an_20:24">20:24</span> ngenxa enokuba bengawenzanga amasiko
am, bayicekisayo imimiselo yam, bazihlambela iisabatha zam, amehlo abo
alandela izigodo zooyise.

<span id="an_20:25">20:25</span> Nam ndabamisela imimiselo
engabalungeleyo, namasiko abangenakuphila ngawo.

<span id="an_20:26">20:26</span> Ndabenza iinqambi ngezipho zabo,
ekucandiseni kwabo emlilweni yonke into evula isizalo, ukuze
ndibaphanzise; ukuze bazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_20:27">20:27</span> Ngako oko, thetha kwindlu kaSirayeli,
nyana womntu, uthi kubo, Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ooyihlo babuye
bandinyelisa nangale nto, ekumenezeni kwabo ababemeneza ngako kum.

<span id="an_20:28">20:28</span> Kuba xenikweni ndabasayo ezweni
endasiphakamiselayo isandla sam sokuba ndibanike lona, basuka bakhangela
zonke iinduli ezinde, nemithi yonke ethe shinyi; bayibingelela khona
imibingelelo yabo, banikela khona imisondezo yabo equmbisayo, babeka
khona ivumba lamadini abo elithozamisayo, bathululela khona iminikelo
yabo ethululwayo.

<span id="an_20:29">20:29</span> Ndathi ke kubo, Esi siganga niya kuso
siyintoni na? Igama laso ke kuthiwa, siSiganga, unanamhla.

<span id="an_20:30">20:30</span> Ngako oko yithi kwindlu kaSirayeli,
Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Nizenze iinqambi ngendlela yooyihlo,
nihenyuze ngokulandela izinto zabo ezinezothe nje;

<span id="an_20:31">20:31</span> nizenze iinqambi ezigodweni zenu
ngokunikela izipho zenu, nangokuba candisa emlilweni oonyana benu
nanamhlanje; mna ndingabuzwa nini na, ndlu kaSirayeli? Ndihleli nje,
