itsho iNkosi uYehova, andiyi kubuzwa nini, nakanye.

<span id="an_20:32">20:32</span> Loo nto ithe qatha emoyeni wenu, ayiyi
kubakho nokubakho: leyo nithi, Siya kuba njengeentlanga, njengemizalwane
yamazwe, silungiselele kwimithi namatye.

<span id="an_20:33">20:33</span> Ndihleli nje, inyaniso, itsho iNkosi
uYehova, ngesandla esithe nkqi, nangengalo eyolukileyo, nangobushushu
obuthululwayo, ndiya kuba ngukumkani phezu kwenu.

<span id="an_20:34">20:34</span> Ndonikhupha ezizweni, ndinibuthe
emazweni enaphangalaliswa kuwo, ngesandla esithe nkqi, nangengalo
eyolukileyo, nangobushushu obuthululwayo,

<span id="an_20:35">20:35</span> Ndiya kunisa kwintlango yezizwe,
ndimangalelane nani, sikhangelane ebusweni;

<span id="an_20:36">20:36</span> njengoko ndamangalelana nooyihlo
kwintlango yelizwe laseYiputa, ndiya kwenjenjalo ukumangalelana nani;
itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_20:37">20:37</span> Ndoniphumelisa phantsi kwentonga,
ndinibophelele ngomnqophiso;

<span id="an_20:38">20:38</span> ndibakhethe kuni abagwilikayo
nabakreqayo kum. Ndiya kubakhupha ezweni lokuphambukela kwabo; ke akuyi
kungena namnye emhlabeni wakwaSirayeli, ukuze nazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_20:39">20:39</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Nina ke,
ndlu kaSirayeli, hambani, nikhonze elowo isigodo sakhe; kodwa emveni
koko, inyaniso, niya kundiphulaphula, ningabi salihlambela igama lam
elingcwele ngezipho zenu nangezigodo zenu.

<span id="an_20:40">20:40</span> Ngokuba itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Entabeni yam engcwele, entabeni ende yakwaSirayeli, khona apho iya
kundikhonza yonke indlu yakwaSirayeli, yonke iphela ezweni; khona apho
baya kuba likholo kum; khona apho ndiya kubiza imirhumo yenu
neentlahlela yezipho zenu, entweni yenu yonke eniyingcwalisayo.

<span id="an_20:41">20:41</span> Niya kuba likholo kum ninevumba
elithozamisayo, ekunikhupheni kwam ezizweni; ndinibuthe emazweni
enaphangalaliswa kuwo, ndizingcwalisele kuni emehlweni eentlanga;

<span id="an_20:42">20:42</span> nazi ukuba ndinguYehova, ekuniseni kwam
emhlabeni wakwaSirayeli, ezweni endasiphakamisela isandla sam sokuba
ndilinike ooyihlo,

<span id="an_20:43">20:43</span> Niya kuzikhumbula khona iindlela zenu
neentlondi zenu zonke, enazenza iinqambi ngazo; nizikruqukele ngokwenu
ngenxa yazo zonke izinto ezimbi enizenzileyo;

<span id="an_20:44">20:44</span> nazi ukuba ndinguYehova, ekuniphatheni
kwam ngenxa yegama lam, kungekhona ngokweendlela zenu ezimbi,
nangokweentlondi zenu ezibolileyo, ndlu kaSirayeli; itsho iNkosi
uYehova.

<span id="an_20:45">20:45</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_20:46">20:46</span> Nyana womntu, bhekisa ubuso bakho
kwelasezantsi, uwise intetho usingise ezantsi, uprofete ngehlathi
lelizwe lasezantsi;

<span id="an_20:47">20:47</span> uthi kwihlathi lelizwe lasezantsi, Live
ilizwi likaYehova; itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Yabona, ndifaka umlilo
kuwe, utshise kuwe wonke umthi omanzi, nawo wonke umthi owomileyo. Akuyi
kucima dangatye lamadangatye; borhawuka ubuso babantu bonke,
kuthabathele ezantsi kuse entla,

<span id="an_20:48">20:48</span> Yobona yonke inyama, ukuba mna Yehova
ndiwubasile; awuyi kucinywa.

<span id="an_20:49">20:49</span> Ndathi, Awu! Nkosi Yehova, bathi ngam
lo, Akenzi ngemizekeliso kodwa na?

<span id="an_21:1">21:1</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_21:2">21:2</span> Nyana womntu, bhekisa ubuso kwiYerusalem,
uwise intetho ezingcweleni, uprofete ngomhlaba wakwaSirayeli.

<span id="an_21:3">21:3</span> Yithi kumhlaba wakwaSirayeli, Utsho
uYehova ukuthi, Yabona, ndikuchasile; ndirhola ikrele lam esingxotyeni
salo, ndinqumle kuwe ilungisa nongendawo.

<span id="an_21:4">21:4</span> Ngenxa ke enokuba ndiya kunqumla kuwe
ilungisa nongendawo, ngako oko liya kuphuma ikrele lam esingxotyeni
salo, liye enyameni yonke, lithabathele ezantsi lise entla;

<span id="an_21:5">21:5</span> yazi yonke inyama, ukuba mna Yehova
ndilirholile ikrele lam esingxotyeni salo; alisayi kuba sabuya libuye.

<span id="an_21:6">21:6</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, ncwina; uqhekeke
amanqe, uncwine nangobukrakra, emehlweni abo.

<span id="an_21:7">21:7</span> Kothi, xa bathe kuwe, Uncwinelani na?
uthi, Kungenxa yeendaba, ngokuba zisiza; kuya kunyibilika zonke
iintliziyo, ziwe zonke izandla, incame yonke imimoya, amadolo onke
angabi namandla. Yabona, ziyeza, ziya kubakho; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_21:8">21:8</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_21:9">21:9</span> Nyana womntu, profeta uthi, Utsho uYehova
ukuthi, Ikrele, ikrele liloliwe, likhazimlisiwe nokukhazimliswa.

<span id="an_21:10">21:10</span> Liloliwe ukuze lixhele libulale;
likhazimlisiwe ukuze limenyezele njengombane. Ngesiba nemihlali sithi,
Intonga yonyana wam le icekisa imithi yonke na?

<span id="an_21:11">21:11</span> Linikelwe ukuba likhazimliswe,
liphathwe ngesandla; liloliwe ikrele elo, likhazimlisiwe elo, ukuba
linikelwe esandleni sombulali.

<span id="an_21:12">21:12</span> Khala ubhomboloze, nyana womntu;
ngokuba lithene mbende nabantu bam, lithene mbende nezikhulu zonke
zakwaSirayeli; zizisulu zekrele kunye nabantu bam; ngako oko tywakraza
ethangeni.

<span id="an_21:13">21:13</span> Ngokuba sekucikidiwe; hi, kothini na
ukuba nentonga ecekisayo? Akuyi kuba njalo; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_21:14">21:14</span> Wena ke nyana womntu, profeta,
utywakraze izandla; liphindwe okwesithathu ikrele, ikrele lababuleweyo;
likrele lobuleweyo, lalowo mkhulu, elibarawulayo.

<span id="an_21:15">21:15</span> Ukuze intliziyo ithe amandla, zande
izikhubekiso, ndiwamisele amasango abo onke ikrele elijikajikayo. Awu!
Lenzelwe ukuba libe njengombane, lithiwe rhuthu ukuba libulale.

<span id="an_21:16">21:16</span> Tyekela ngasekunene, guqukela ekhohlo,
apho lubhekisa khona uhlangothi lwakho.

<span id="an_21:17">21:17</span> Nam ndiya kuzitywakraza izandla zam,
ndibupholise ubushushu bam, mna Yehova ndithethile.

<span id="an_21:18">21:18</span> Kwafika kum ilizwi likaYehova, lisithi,

<span id="an_21:19">21:19</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, zimisele
iindlela ezimbini, ukuze lizengazo ikrele lokumkani waseBhabheli;
maziphume zweni-nye zombini, ukrole umalathiso, uwukrole emantloko
endlela yomzi.

<span id="an_21:20">21:20</span> Misa indlela, ukuze ikrele lifike
eRabha yoonyana baka-Amon, nakwelakwaYuda, eYerusalem enqatyisiweyo.

<span id="an_21:21">21:21</span> Kuba ukumkani waseBhabheli umise
ekwahlukaneni kweendlela, emantloko eendlela zombini, ukuze ahlabe
isihlabo; uhlukuhla iintolo, ubuza kwimilondekhaya, ukhangela
esibindini.

<span id="an_21:22">21:22</span> Esandleni sakhe sokunene isihlabo
sihlabe iYerusalem, ukuze kumiswe izinto zokutyhomfa, uhlatywe umkhosi
wokubulala, kuphakanyiswe izwi lokuduma, kumiswe izinto zokutyhomfa
emasangweni, kufunjwe udonga lokungqinga, kwakhiwe iinqaba zokubonisela.

<span id="an_21:23">21:23</span> Soba njengesihlabo esikhohlakeleyo kubo
emehlweni abo, bafungelwe izifungo bona; ke yena wokhumbuza ubugwenxa,
ukuze baxhakamfulwe.

<span id="an_21:24">21:24</span> Ngako oko itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ngenxa yokukhumbuza kwenu ubugwenxa benu, ekutyhilekeni kwezikreqo zenu,
ukuze zibonakale izono zenu ezintlondini zenu zonke; ngenxa
yokukhunjulwa kwenu, niya kuxhakamfulwa ngesandla.

<span id="an_21:25">21:25</span> Wena ke, mbulawa ungendawo, sikhulu
sakwaSirayeli, umini yakho ifikileyo ngexesha lobugwenxa bokuphela,
itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,

<span id="an_21:26">21:26</span> Luya kususwa unkontsho, sithulwe
nesithsaba; oko koko, namhla kunamhla; okuthobekileyo kuya
kuphakanyiswa, okuphakamileyo kuya kuthotywa.

<span id="an_21:27">21:27</span> Ndiya kukuphenula ndikuphenule,
ndikuphenule; kwanako oko akuyi kuba kuko, koda kufike lowo kukokwakhe
ukugweba; ndikunike yena.

<span id="an_21:28">21:28</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, profeta uthi,
Itsho iNkosi uYehova ngokusingisele koonyana baka-Amon, ngokusingisele
kungcikivo lwabo, ukuthi, Ikrele, ikrele lirholelwe ukuba libulale;
likhazimlisiwe ukuba lidle, ukuba libe njengombane.

<span id="an_21:29">21:29</span> Bekubonela inkohlakalo nje, bekuhlabela
amanga nje, liya kukubeka ke ezintanyeni zabangendawo ababuleweyo,
abamini iya kufika ngexesha lobugwenxa bokuphela.

<span id="an_21:30">21:30</span> Libuyisele esingxotyeni salo. Endaweni
odalelwe kuyo, ezweni lemvelo yakho, ndiya kukugweba.

<span id="an_21:31">21:31</span> Ndiya kuthulula phezu kwakho ubhavumo
lwam. Ndiya kukubasela ngomlilo wokuphuphuma komsindo wam, ndikunikele
esandleni samadoda azizityhakala, iingcibi ezonakalisayo.

<span id="an_21:32">21:32</span> Uya kuba kukudla komlilo; igazi lakho
liya kuba phakathi kwelizwe; akuyi kukhunjulwa; kuba mna Yehova
ndithethile.

<span id="an_22:1">22:1</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_22:2">22:2</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, uza kuwugweba na?
Uza kuwugweba na umzi wamagazi? Wazise ke onke amasikizi awo.

<span id="an_22:3">22:3</span> Uze uthi, Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Mzindini, uphalaza igazi esazulwini sawo, ukuze lifike ixesha lawo,
wenze izigodo kuwo ukuze ube yinqambi!

<span id="an_22:4">22:4</span> Ngegazi lakho olithululeyo uzeke ityala,
nangezigodo zakho ozenzileyo uzenze inqambi, wazisondeza iimini zakho,
wafika eminyakeni yakho. Ngenxa yoko ndikwenza into yengcikivo
ezintlangeni, nento yokucukucezwa kuwo onke amazwe.

<span id="an_22:5">22:5</span> Abakufuphi nabakude kuwe baya
kukucukuceza; unegama lobunqambi, unesaqunge esikhulu.

<span id="an_22:6">22:6</span> Yabona, izikhulu zakwaSirayeli, saseso
ngokwengalo yaso, zibe zikuwe, ukuze ziphalaze igazi.

<span id="an_22:7">22:7</span> Uyise nonina babacukucezela kuwe;
owasemzini bamcudisela esazulwini sakho; iinkedama nabahlolokazi
babaxinzelela phantsi kuwe.

<span id="an_22:8">22:8</span> Iingcwele zam uzidelile, neesabatha zam
uzihlambele.

<span id="an_22:9">22:9</span> Amadoda anentlebendwane abekuwe, ukuze
aphalaze igazi; adlela ezintabeni kuwe, enza amanyala esazulwini sakho.

<span id="an_22:10">22:10</span> Ubuze booyise butyhilelwe kuwe;
oyinqambi ngokuba nomzi bamdlwengulela kuwe.

<span id="an_22:11">22:11</span> Omnye wenza amasikizi nomfazi
wommelwane wakhe; omnye umenza inqambi umolokazana wakhe ngobugqwirha;
omnye udlwengula udade wabo, intombi kayise, kuwe.

<span id="an_22:12">22:12</span> Bamkela izicengo bekuwe, ukuze
baphalaze igazi; wena udle abantu ngemali, wathabatha inzala yemboleko:
uyamdla ummelwane wakho ngokucudisa; undilibele; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_22:13">22:13</span> Yabona, nditywakraza izandla zam ngenxa
yenzuzo yakho embi oyizuzileyo, nangenxa yamagazi akho asesazulwini
sakho.

<span id="an_22:14">22:14</span> Intliziyo yakho iya kuma na? Izandla
zakho ziya kuthi nkqi na, ngemihla endiya kukuphatha ngayo? Mna Yehova
ndithethile, ndiya kwenza ke.

<span id="an_22:15">22:15</span> Ndiya kukuphangalalisela ezintlangeni,
ndikuchithachithe emazweni, ndibugqibele ubunqambi bakho kuwe.

<span id="an_22:16">22:16</span> Wozihlambela emehlweni eentlanga, wazi
ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_22:17">22:17</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_22:18">22:18</span> Nyana womntu, indlu kaSirayeli isuke
yaba ligwebu lentsimbi kum; bonke bephela baba lubhedu nebhekile
nesinyithi nelothe, phakathi eziko; baba ligwebu lesilivere.

<span id="an_22:19">22:19</span> Ngako oko itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ngenxa yokuba naba ligwebu lentsimbi nonke niphela, ngako oko, yabonani,
ndiya kunibutha esazulwini seYerusalem.

<span id="an_22:20">22:20</span> Njengokuhlanganiselwa kwesilivere
nobhedu nesinyithi nelothe nebhekile phakathi eziko, ukuba umlilo
uzifuthe, ukuze zinyibilike: ndiya kwenjenjalo ukunibutha ngomsindo wam,
nangobushushu bam, ndinifake, ndininyibilikise.

<span id="an_22:21">22:21</span> Ndonifumba, ndifuthe umlilo
wokuphuphuma komsindo wam kuni, ninyibilike phakathi kwawo.

<span id="an_22:22">22:22</span> Njengokuba isilivere inyibilikiswa
phakathi eziko, niya kwenjenjalo ukunyibilikiswa phakathi kwayo; nazi
ukuba mna Yehova ndibuthulule ubushushu bam phezu kwenu.

<span id="an_22:23">22:23</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_22:24">22:24</span> Nyana womntu, yithi kulo, Ulilizwe
elizulu lingasiyo, elinganelwayo ngomhla wobhavumo.

<span id="an_22:25">22:25</span> Lucebo lwabaprofeti balo esazulwini
salo. Njengengonyama ebharhulayo, eqwenga inyamakazi, badla imiphefumlo;
bahlutha into eqwetyiweyo nenqabileyo; bandisa abahlolokazi balo
esazulwini salo.

<span id="an_22:26">22:26</span> Ababingeleli balo bayawugonyamela
umyalelo wam, bazihlambele iingcwele zam; abacaluli phakathi kokungcwele
nokuhlambelayo, ababonisi mahluko kokuyinqambi nokuhlambulukileyo;
bayawafihla amelulo abo kwiisabatha zam, ndihlanjelwe esazulwini sabo.

<span id="an_22:27">22:27</span> Abathetheli balo esazulwini salo
banjengeengcuka eziqwenga ixhoba, ukuba baphalaze igazi, batshabalalise
imiphefumlo, ukuze bazuze inzuzo embi.

<span id="an_22:28">22:28</span> Abaprofeti babatyabeka ngodaka
olulephukayo, bebona imibono yenkohlakalo, bebahlabela izihlabo
ezingamanga, besithi, Itsho iNkosi uYehova; kanti uYehova akathethanga.

<span id="an_22:29">22:29</span> Abantu belizwe elo bayacudisa,
bayaphanga, baxinzelela phantsi usizana nehlwempu, bacudise owasemzini
ngokungesesikweni.

<span id="an_22:30">22:30</span> Ndafuna kubo indoda engaba luthango
phakathi, ime ethutyeni phambi kwam, ikhusele ilizwe elo, ukuze
ndingalitshabalalisi; ke andiyifumani.

<span id="an_22:31">22:31</span> Ngoko ke ndithulula ubhavumo lwam phezu
kwabo, ndibagqibele ngomlilo wokuphuphuma komsindo wam, ndibanike
ngokwendlela yabo entlokweni yabo; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_23:1">23:1</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_23:2">23:2</span> Nyana womntu, kwakukho abafazi ababini,
iintombi zamfazi mnye.

<span id="an_23:3">23:3</span> Bahenyuza eYiputa, bahenyuza
besebancinane; acofelwa khona amabele abo; zaphathwa khona iingono
zamabele zobuntombi babo.

<span id="an_23:4">23:4</span> Amagama abo ke nguNtente-yakhe omkhulu
kubo, noNtente-yam-kuye umsakwabo; baba ngabam, bazala oonyana
neentombi. Amagama abo nguSamari uNtente-yakhe, yiYerusalem
uNtente-yam-kuye.

<span id="an_23:5">23:5</span> UNtente-yakhe wahenyuza engumkam,
watshiswa kukukhanuka izithandane zakhe, ama-Asiriya, umelwane lwakhe:

<span id="an_23:6">23:6</span> abavethe iingubo ezimsi, amabamba
neerhuluneli, amadodana aluluhle onke ephela, abamahashe bekhwele
emahasheni.

<span id="an_23:7">23:7</span> Wakubhekisela kubo ukuhenyuza kwakhe,
koonyana baseAsiriya abaluluhle bonke bephela; wathi abo bonke
abetshiseka kukubakhanuka, wazenza inqambi ngezigodo zabo.

<span id="an_23:8">23:8</span> Akakuyeka nokuhenyuza kwakhe kwaseYiputa;
ngokuba ebuncinaneni bakhe babelala naye, baziphathe iingono zamabele
zobuntombi bakhe bona; bathululele ubufebe babo phezu kwakhe.

<span id="an_23:9">23:9</span> Ngako oko ndamnikela esandleni
sezithandane zakhe, esandleni soonyana baseAsiriya, abo abetshiseka
kukubakhanuka.

<span id="an_23:10">23:10</span> Bona babutyhila ubuze bakhe, bathabatha
oonyana bakhe neentombi zakhe, bambulala ngekrele; waba
ngundaba-mlonyeni kubafazi, bamgweba.

<span id="an_23:11">23:11</span> Wakubona oko umsakwabo,
uNtente-yam-kuye, waba mandundu kunaye ukutshiseka kwakhe kukukhanuka,
kwaba mandundu ukuhenyuza kwakhe kunokuhenyuza kodade wabo.

<span id="an_23:12">23:12</span> Watshiseka kukubakhanuka oonyana
baseAsiriya, amabamba, neerhuluneli, umelwane lwakhe, abavethe
ezimbejembeje; abamahashe bekhwele emahasheni, amadodana aluluhle onke
ephela.

<span id="an_23:13">23:13</span> Ndabona ukuba uzenze inqambi,
bandlela-nye bobabini.

<span id="an_23:14">23:14</span> Wongeza ekuhenyuzeni kwakhe; wabona
amadoda ezotywe eludongeni, imifanekiso yamaKaledi ezotywe ngeqabo
elibomvu,

<span id="an_23:15">23:15</span> enxibe iinqwemesha ezinqeni,
eneenkontsho ezimfakamfele ezintloko, ebonakala engabaphathi-mikhosi
onke ephela, efana noonyana baseBhabheli, belamaKaledi, izwe lokuzalwa
kwabo.

<span id="an_23:16">23:16</span> Watshiseka kukuwakhanuka, amehlo akhe
akuwabona; wathuma abathunywa kwelamaKaledi.

<span id="an_23:17">23:17</span> Beza ke kuye oonyana baseBhabheli
esililini sokuncokolisa, bamenza inqambi ngobufebe babo; wazenza inqambi
ngabo; wancothuka kubo umphefumlo wakhe.

<span id="an_23:18">23:18</span> Wakutyhila ukuhenyuza kwakhe,
wabutyhila ubuze bakhe, wancothuka ke umphefumlo wam kuye, njengoko
umphefumlo wam wancothukayo kumsakwabo.

<span id="an_23:19">23:19</span> Wongeza ke ukuhenyuza kwakhe,
ngokukhumbula imihla yobuncinane bakhe, awahenyuza ngayo ezweni
leYiputa.

<span id="an_23:20">23:20</span> Watshiseka kukuwakhanuka amakrexe akhe,
anyama ziziinyama zamaesile, amakhanuko awo angamakhanuko amahashe.

<span id="an_23:21">23:21</span> Wamana ukhumbula amanyala obuncinane
bakho, oko amaYiputa abephathe iingono zamabele akho, ngenxa yamabele
obuncinane bakho.

<span id="an_23:22">23:22</span> Ngako oko, Ntente-yam-kuye, itsho
iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Yabona, ndikuxhokonxela izithandane zakho, ezo
uncothukileyo kuzo umphefumlo wakho; ndizizise phezu kwakho, zivela
ngeenxa zonke:

<span id="an_23:23">23:23</span> oonyana baseBhabheli namaKaledi onke,
abaveleli, izikhulu, iinduna, benoonyana bonke baseAsiriya, amadodana
aluluhle, amabamba neerhuluneli, bonke bephela, nabaphathi-mikhosi,
namaphakathi, bengabakhweli bamahashe bonke bephela.

<span id="an_23:24">23:24</span> Baya kukufikela benezikhali, neenqwelo
zokulwa, neevili, benesikhungu sezizwe; babhekise kuwe iingweletshetshe
namakhaka nezigcina-ntloko ngeenxa zonke. Ndolunikela kubo ugwebo, ukuba
bakugwebe ngokwamasiko abo,

<span id="an_23:25">23:25</span> ndikunikele ebukhweleni bam, bakuphathe
ngobushushu. Baya kususa impumlo yakho neendlebe zakho, nento yakho
eseleyo iwe likrele. Bona baya kuthabatha oonyana bakho neentombi zakho;
nento yakho eseleyo itshiswe ngumlilo;

<span id="an_23:26">23:26</span> bakuhlube iingubo zakho, bazithabathe
iimpahla zakho zokuhomba.

<span id="an_23:27">23:27</span> Ndowaphelisa amanyala akho nokuhenyuza
kwakho kwasezweni laseYiputa, ungabi sawaphakamisela amehlo akho kuwo,
ungabi salikhumbula elaseYiputa.

<span id="an_23:28">23:28</span> Ngokuba itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Yabona, ndiya kukunikela esandleni sabo ubathiyileyo, esandleni sabo
uncothukileyo kubo umphefumlo wakho.

<span id="an_23:29">23:29</span> Baya kukuphatha ngentiyo, bathabathe
konke ukuxelenga kwakho, bakushiye uze kanye, butyhileke ubuze
bokuhenyuza kwakho, namanyala akho, nokuhenyuza kwakho.

<span id="an_23:30">23:30</span> Kuya kwenzeka oko kuwe, ngenxa
yokuhenyuza kwakho ekulandeleni iintlanga, ngenxa enokuba uzenze inqambi
ngezigodo zazo.

<span id="an_23:31">23:31</span> Uhambe ngendlela yomsakwenu;
ndoyinikela ke indebe yakhe esandleni sakho.

<span id="an_23:32">23:32</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Uya
kuyisela indebe yomsakwenu, yona leyo inzulu, ibanzi; iya kuba
yintlekisa nesigculelo, ngokuba inombilini omkhulu.

<span id="an_23:33">23:33</span> Uya kuzala kukunxila nasisingqala;
yindebe yakwankangala kankangala indebe yodade wenu uSamari.

<span id="an_23:34">23:34</span> Uya kuyisela ke, uyifince, uwaqobe
amagophe ayo, uzijece ngawo amabele; ngokuba ndithethile, itsho iNkosi
uYehova.

<span id="an_23:35">23:35</span> Ngako oko itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ngenxa enokuba undilibele, wandiphosa emva komhlana wakho, uya
kuwathwala nokuwathwala amanyala akho nokuhenyuza kwakho.

<span id="an_23:36">23:36</span> Wathi uYehova kum, Nyana womntu, uza
kubagweba na ooNtente-yakhe noNtente-yam-kuye? Baxelele ke amasikizi
abo.

<span id="an_23:37">23:37</span> Ngokuba bakrexezile, izandla zabo
zinegazi; bakrexezene nezigodo zabo; kananjalo oonyana babo, ababazalela
mna, babacandisele kuzo, ukuba batshiswe ngumlilo.

<span id="an_23:38">23:38</span> Babuye benza noku kum: bayenze inqambi
ingcwele yam kwangayo loo mini, bazihlambela iisabatha zam;

<span id="an_23:39">23:39</span> bakuzisikela izigodo zabo oonyana babo,
bangena ke engcweleni yam kwangayo loo mini, ukuze bayihlambele; yabona
benjenjalo endlwini yam phakathi.

<span id="an_23:40">23:40</span> Phezu koko bathumele kumadoda avela
kude, kwathunyelwa kuwo umthunywa; yabona, afika; wona lawo wazihlambayo
umzimba ngenxa yawo, waziqaba amehlo ngomsizi, wavathela wona izivatho
zakho;

<span id="an_23:41">23:41</span> wahlala esingqengqelweni
esinobuqaqawuli, alungiselwa isithebe phambi kwaso, wabeka ke kuso
isiqhumiso sam neoli yam.

<span id="an_23:42">23:42</span> Izwi lengxokolo latyondyoloza khona.
Kumadoda aseluninzini loluntu kwaziswa abaseli basentlango, babafaka
izacholo ezihlahleni zabo, nezithsaba zokuhomba ezintlokweni zabo.

<span id="an_23:43">23:43</span> Ndathi ke kulowo oselehagele
ekukrexezeni, Ngokunje uhenyuzo lwakhe luya kukrexeza, lona ngokwalo.

<span id="an_23:44">23:44</span> Bamngena ke njengoko kungenwa ngako
kumfazi olihenyukazi: benjenjalo ukumngena uNtente-yakhe,
noNtente-yam-kuye, abo bafazi banamanyala.

<span id="an_23:45">23:45</span> Ke amadoda angamalungisa, wona ke aya
kubagweba ngokwesiko labakrexezikazi, nangokwesiko labaphalazi begazi;
ngokuba bengabakrexezikazi, zinegazi izandla zabo.

<span id="an_23:46">23:46</span> Ngokuba itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ndiya kubanyusela ibandla, ndibanikele ekunqakulweni nasekuphangweni;

<span id="an_23:47">23:47</span> ibandla libaxulube ngamatye, libasike
ngamakrele alo. Liya kubabulala oonyana babo neentombi zabo, lizitshise
izindlu zabo;

<span id="an_23:48">23:48</span> ndiwaphelise amanyala ezweni,
bathethiseke abafazi bonke, bangenzi ngokwamanyala enu.

<span id="an_23:49">23:49</span> Baya kuwabeka ke amanyala enu phezu
kwenu, nizithwale izono zezigodo zenu; nazi ukuba ndiyiNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_24:1">24:1</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum ngomnyaka
wesithoba, ngenyanga yeshumi, ngolweshumi enyangeni leyo, lisithi,

<span id="an_24:2">24:2</span> Nyana womntu, Zibhalele igama lale mini,
layo yona le mini; ukumkani waseBhabheli uyishicilele iYerusalem ngayo
yona le mini.

<span id="an_24:3">24:3</span> Uze uyizekelisele ngomzekeliso indlu
eneenkani, uthi kubo, Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Beka imbiza eziko,
yibeke, kananjalo ugalele amanzi kuyo.

<span id="an_24:4">24:4</span> Hlanganisela kuyo iinyama zayo; zonke
iinyama ezilungileyo, umlenze negxalaba; yizalise ngamathambo
akhethiweyo.

<span id="an_24:5">24:5</span> Thabatha ezikhethiweyo zempahla
emfutshane, kananjalo amathambo uwafumbele iinkuni ngaphantsi kwayo.
Yibilise kakuhle; kananjalo amathambo ayo makaphekwe phakathi kwayo.

<span id="an_24:6">24:6</span> Ngako oko, itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Yeha, mzindini unamagazi! Mbizandini inomhlwa, emhlwa ungasukiyo!
Yirhole inyama ngeenyama zayo; aliphumi nayo iqashiso.

<span id="an_24:7">24:7</span> Ngokuba igazi lawo liphakathi kwawo;
ulibeke engxondorheni ebalelelwe lilanga; awuliphalazanga emhlabeni,
ukuba liselelwe luthuli.

<span id="an_24:8">24:8</span> Ukuze kunyuke ubushushu, ukuze
iphindezelwe impindezelo, igazi lawo ndilibeke engxondorheni ebalelelwe
lilanga, ukuze lingaselelwa.

<span id="an_24:9">24:9</span> Ngako oko, itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Yeha, mzindini unamagazi! Nam ndiya kuyenza ibe nkulu imfumba yeenkuni.

<span id="an_24:10">24:10</span> Fumba iinkuni, khwezela umlilo, vuthisa
inyama, ujiye umhluzi, atshe amathambo;

<span id="an_24:11">24:11</span> uyibeke phezu kwamalahle ayo,
ingasenanto phakathi, ukuze lufudumale lutshe ubhedu lwayo, bunyibilike
ubunqambi bayo phakathi kwayo, umhlwa wayo ugqibele.

<span id="an_24:12">24:12</span> Izidinisile ngemigushanxa; awuphumi
kuyo umhlwa wayo omninzi; mawube semlilweni umhlwa wayo.

<span id="an_24:13">24:13</span> Ebunqambini bakho ngamanyala; ngenxa
enokuba ndikuhlambulule, akwahlambuluka, akusayi kuhlambuluka
ebunqambini bakho, ndide ndibupholisele kuwe ubushushu bam.

<span id="an_24:14">24:14</span> Mna Yehova ndithethile; iyeza le nto,
ndiya kuyenza; andiyi kuyeka, andiyi kuba nanceba, andiyi kuzohlwaya.
Baya kukugweba ngokweendlela zakho nangokweentlondi zakho; itsho iNkosi
uYehova.

<span id="an_24:15">24:15</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_24:16">24:16</span> Nyana womntu, yabona, ndithabatha kuwe
intanda yamehlo akho ngesibetho; uze ungambambazeli, ungalili;
makungaphumi zinyembezi kuwe.

<span id="an_24:17">24:17</span> Gcuma uthe cwaka; uze ungenzi sijwili
ngabafileyo. Jikela unkontsho lwakho, unxibe iimbadada zakho ezinyaweni
zakho, ungazigqubutheli iindevu zakho eziphezu komlomo, ungasidli isonka
sabantu.

<span id="an_24:18">24:18</span> Ndathetha ke nabantu kusasa; ngokuhlwa
wafa umkam; ndenza ke ngengomso njengoko wayendiwisele umthetho ngako.

<span id="an_24:19">24:19</span> Bathi abantu kum, Akusixeleli na, ukuba
ezi zintozithini na kuthi, ukuba wenjenje?

<span id="an_24:20">24:20</span> Ndathi kubo, Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova
kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_24:21">24:21</span> Yithi kwindlu kaSirayeli, Itsho iNkosi
uYehova ukuthi, Yabonani, ndiya kuyingcolisa ingcwele yam, iqhayiya
lamandla enu, intanda yamehlo enu, isizondelelo somphefumlo wenu, bawe
likrele oonyana benu neentombi zenu enibashiyileyo.

<span id="an_24:22">24:22</span> Niya kwenza ke njengoko ndenze ngako:
iindevu eziphezu komlomo aniyi kuzigqubuthela, ningasidli isonka
sabantu;

<span id="an_24:23">24:23</span> iinkontsho zenu ziya kuba sentloko
kuni, neembadada zenu zibe sezinyaweni zenu; aniyi kumbambazela, nilile;
ke niya kungcungcutheka ebugwenxeni benu, nigcume, omnye ekhangele
komnye.

<span id="an_24:24">24:24</span> UHezekile woba sisimanga kuni; niya
kwenza njengako konke akwenzileyo; ekuzeni kwako oko, niya kwazi ukuba
ndiyiNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_24:25">24:25</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, inyaniso, mini
ndithabatha kubo inqaba yabo, imihlali yesihombo sabo, intanda yamehlo
abo, into abaphakamisela kuyo umphefumlo wabo, oonyana babo neentombi
zabo:

<span id="an_24:26">24:26</span> ngayo loo mini kuya kufika osindileyo
kuwe, avakalise oko ezindlebeni zakho.

<span id="an_24:27">24:27</span> Ngayo loo mini uya kuvuleka umlomo
wakho, kunye nosindileyo lowo; uthethe, ungabi saba sisidenge; ube
sisimanga kubo; bazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_25:1">25:1</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_25:2">25:2</span> Nyana womntu, bhekisa ubuso bakho
koonyana baka-Amon, uprofete ngabo,

<span id="an_25:3">25:3</span> uthi koonyana baka-Amon, Liveni ilizwi
leNkosi uYehova. Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ngenxa enokuba usithi
kwingcwele yam, Tshotsho! ngokuba ihlanjelwe; nakumhlaba wakwaSirayeli,
Tshotsho! ngokuba wenziwe kwaba senkangala; nakwindlu yakwaYuda,
Tshotsho! ngokuba bathinjiwe:

<span id="an_25:4">25:4</span> ngako oko, yabona, ndikunikela koonyana
basempumalanga, ukuba bamele kuwe, bamise iingqili zabo kuwe, benze
neendawo zokuhlala kwabo kuwe. Bona baya kudla iziqhamo zakho, basele
amasi akho.

<span id="an_25:5">25:5</span> Ndiya kuyenza iRabha ibe likriwa
leenkamela, eloonyana baka-Amon ndilenze libe yindawo yokubutha
kwemihlambi; nazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_25:6">25:6</span> Ngokuba itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ngenxa enokuba ubethe esandleni sakho, wangqisha ngonyawo, wawuvuyela
umhlaba wakwaSirayeli ngokucekisa komphefumlo:

<span id="an_25:7">25:7</span> ngako oko, yabona, ndisolula phezu kwakho
isandla sam, ndikunikele ezintlangeni, ukuba ube lixhoba, ndikunqumle
ezizweni, ndikwenze udake, ungabikho emazweni. Ndiya kukutshabalalisa;
wazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_25:8">25:8</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ngenxa
enokuba besithi ooMowabhi, noSehire, Yabonani, injengeentlanga zonke
indlu yakwaYuda:

<span id="an_25:9">25:9</span> ngako oko, yabonani, ndivula icala
likaMowabhi, ndithabathela emizini yakhe, kwesekupheleni kwakhe, eligugu
lelizwe, iBhete-yeshimoti, neBhahali-mehon, ndise eKiriyatayim.

<span id="an_25:10">25:10</span> Ndolivulela oonyana basempumalanga,
kunye neloonyana baka-Amon, ndibanike limiwe, ukuze bangabi sakhunjulwa
ezintlangeni oonyana baka-Amon;

<span id="an_25:11">25:11</span> ndenze izigwebo kwaMowabhi; bazi ukuba
ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_25:12">25:12</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ngenxa
enokuba uEdom esebenze ngokuphindezela impindezelo kwindlu yakwaYuda,
wazeka ityala elikhulu ngokuphindezela kubo:

<span id="an_25:13">25:13</span> ngako oko itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ndiya kusolula isandla sam naphezu kwelakwaEdom, ndinqumle kulo umntu
nenkomo; ndilibharhise, kuthabathele kwaTeman; bawe likrele, kuse
nakwaDedan.

<span id="an_25:14">25:14</span> Ndiya kuphindezela kwaEdom ngesandla
sabantu bam amaSirayeli, benze kwaEdom ngokomsindo wam nangokobushushu
bam; bakwazi ke ukuphindezela kwam; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_25:15">25:15</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ngenxa
yokwenza kwamaFilisti ngempindezelo, ephindezela ngempindezelo, ecekisa
emphefumlweni, esonakalisa, enobutshaba obungunaphakade:

<span id="an_25:16">25:16</span> ngako oko itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Yabona, ndiya kusolula isandla sam phezu kwamaFilisti, ndiwanqumle
amaKreti, ndiwatshabalalise amasalela aselunxwemeni lolwandle.

<span id="an_25:17">25:17</span> Ndiya kwenza kuwo iimpindezelo
ezinkulu, ezishushu; bazi ukuba ndinguYehova, ekwenzeni kwam impindezelo
kuwo.

<span id="an_26:1">26:1</span> Kwathi ngomnyaka weshumi elinamnye,
ngolokuqala enyangeni leyo, kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_26:2">26:2</span> Nyana womntu, ngenxa enokuba iTire isithi
ngeYerusalem, Tshotsho! lwaphukile ucango lwezizwe; luvulekele kum;
ndiya kuchuma mna, ibe linxuwa yona!

<span id="an_26:3">26:3</span> ngako oko, itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Yabona, ndikuchasile, Tire. Ndiya kukunyusela iintlanga ezininzi,
njengokuba ulwandle lunyusa amaza alo;

<span id="an_26:4">26:4</span> ziziqhuqhe iindonga zaseTire,
zizigungxule iinqaba zakho ezinde. Ndolutshayela uthuli lwayo kuyo,
ndiyenze ibe yingxondorha ebalelelwe lilanga.

<span id="an_26:5">26:5</span> Iya kuba yindawo yokwanekela iminatha
phakathi kolwandle; ngokuba ndithethile, itsho iNkosi uYehova; ibe
lixhoba leentlanga.

<span id="an_26:6">26:6</span> Namagxamesi ayo asemaphandleni aya
kubulawa ngekrele; bazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_26:7">26:7</span> Ngokuba itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Yabona, iTire ndiya kuyizisela uNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli,
evela entla, ukumkani wookumkani, enamahashe neenqwelo zokulwa,
nabakhweli, nesikhungu sabantu, nabantu abaninzi.

<span id="an_26:8">26:8</span> Amagxamesi akho asemaphandleni uya
kuwabulala ngekrele, akumisele inqaba yokubonisela, afumbe kuwe udonga
lokungqinga, akumisele ikhusi lamakhaka;

<span id="an_26:9">26:9</span> abhekise ezindongeni zakho iimpahla zakhe
zokutyhomfa, azidilize iinqaba zakho ezinde ngeentsimbi zakhe.

<span id="an_26:10">26:10</span> Ngenxa yoninzi lwamahashe akhe, uthuli
lwawo luya kukugubungela; iindonga zakho ziya kunyikima ngenxa yesandi
sabakhweli, neseevili, neseenqwelo zokulwa, ekungeneni kwakhe ngamasango
akho, njengabangena emzini oqhekezwayo.

<span id="an_26:11">26:11</span> Ngamanqina amahashe akhe uya kuzigqusha
izitrato zakho zonke; uya kubabulala abantu bakho ngekrele, iintsika
zakho ezinamandla aziwise emhlabeni.

<span id="an_26:12">26:12</span> Baya kubuthimba ubutyebi bakho,
bayiphange into orhweba ngayo, bazigunguxule iindonga zakho, bazidilize
izindlu zakho ezinqwenelekayo, bawatshonise emanzini amatye akho,
nemithi yakho, nothuli lwakho.

<span id="an_26:13">26:13</span> Ndoluphelisa ulwandile lweengoma zakho,
singabi saviwa isandi seehadi zakho.

<span id="an_26:14">26:14</span> Ndokwenza ube yingxondorha ebalelelwe
lilanga; uya kuba yindawo yokwaneka iminatha. Akusayi kuba sakhiwa;
ngokuba mna Yehova ndithethile; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_26:15">26:15</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova kwiTire, ukuthi,
Aziyi kunyikima na iziqithi ngenxa yesithonga sokuwa kwakho, ekuncwineni
kwabangxwelerhiweyo, ekubulaweni kwabaphakathi kwakho?

<span id="an_26:16">26:16</span> Ziya kuhla ezitroneni zabo bonke
abazizikhulu zolwandle, bazisuse iingubo zabo zokwaleka, bazihlube
iingubo zabo ezimfakamfele; bambathe ukugubha, bahlale phantsi
emhlabeni, bagubhe ngamaphanyazo onke, bamangaliswe nguwe.

<span id="an_26:17">26:17</span> Baya kukuphakamisela isijwili, bathi
kuwe, Yoo! Utheni na ukudaka, wena ubumiwe ngabeelwandle, wena mzindini
udumileyo, owawomelele elwandle, wona nabemi bawo, obe ubaqhiphukisa
umbilini abemi bawo bonke!

<span id="an_26:18">26:18</span> Ngoku ziyagubha iziqithi ngomhla wokuwa
kwakho, zikhwankqiswe iziqithi eziselwandle ngenxa yokuphela kwakho.

<span id="an_26:19">26:19</span> Ngokuba itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ekukwenzeni kwam ube ngumzi olinxuwa, njengemizi engasamiweyo;
ekuwanyuseni kwam phezu kwakho amanzi anzongonzongo, akugubungele amanzi
amaninzi:

<span id="an_26:20">26:20</span> ndiya kukuhlisela kwabahle baya
emhadini, ndikuse ebantwini basendaleni, ndikuhlalise ezweni
langaphantsi, emanxuweni asendaleni nabahle baya emhadini, ukuze
ungamiwa; ndenze ubukhazikhazi ezweni labahleliyo.

<span id="an_26:21">26:21</span> Ndokwenza ube sisikhwankqiso,
ungabikho; bakufune, bangabi sakufumana naphakade; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_27:1">27:1</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_27:2">27:2</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, yiphakamisele
isimbonono iTire.

<span id="an_27:3">27:3</span> Yithi kwiTire, Wena uhleliyo ezingenweni
zolwandle, mrhwebelikazi wezizwe eziqithini ezininzi, itsho iNkosi
uYehova ukuthi, Tire, uthi wena, Ndimhle kwaphela.

<span id="an_27:4">27:4</span> Isembilinini yeelwandle imida yakho,
abakhi bakho bakwenze wamhle kwaphela.

<span id="an_27:5">27:5</span> Ngemisipres yaseSenire bakwakhele zonke
iideke zakho, bathabatha imisedare yaseLebhanon ukwenza imasti kuwe.

<span id="an_27:6">27:6</span> Bawenza ngemioki yaseBhashan amaphini
akho okubheqa; izihlalo zakho bazenza ngeempondo zeendlovu, ezifakelwe
emigalagaleni yaseziqithini zamaKiti.

<span id="an_27:7">27:7</span> Ilinen ecikizekileyo emfakamfele
yaseYiputa yaba iyiseyile yakho, ukuba ibe yibhanile kuwe; ingubo emsi
nemfusa yaseziqhithini zakwaElisha yaba ngumthunzi wakho.

<span id="an_27:8">27:8</span> Abemi baseTsidon neArvadi baye
bengababheqi bakho; izilumko zakho, Tire, zaba phakathi kwakho, zaba
ngabaqhubi bakho.

<span id="an_27:9">27:9</span> Amadoda amakhulu aseGebhali nezilumko
zakhona ebe zikuwe, zaba ngabalungisi beentanda zakho. Yonke imikhombe
yolwandle ibe ikuwe, noomateloshe bayo, ukuba yanane urhwebo lwakho.

<span id="an_27:10">27:10</span> AmaPersi namaLudi namaPuti
ebesemkhosini wakho, engamadoda akho okulwa; abezixhoma kuwe
iingweletshetshe nezigcina-ntloko; akunika ubungangamela wona.

<span id="an_27:11">27:11</span> Oonyana baseArvadi babenomkhosi wakho
phezu kweendonga zakho ngeenxa zonke, namakroti abesezinqabeni zakho
ezinde; axhoma iingweletshetshe zawo ezindongeni zakho ngeenxa zonke;
wona akwenza wamhle kwaphela.

<span id="an_27:12">27:12</span> ITarshishe yarhwebelana nawe ngenxa
yobuninzi bobuncwane bonke, bakurholela isilivere, nesinyithi,
nebhekile, nelothe, ngeempahla zakho.

<span id="an_27:13">27:13</span> OoYavan noTubhali noMesheki
babengabarhwebeli bakho barhwebisana nawe ngeziqu zabantu nangeempahla
zobhedu.

<span id="an_27:14">27:14</span> Abendlu kaTogarma bakurholela amahashe
eenqwelo zokulwa, nawokukhwela, noondlebende, ngeempahla zakho.

<span id="an_27:15">27:15</span> Oonyana bakaDedan babengabarhwebeli
bakho; iziqithi ezininzi bezirhwebisana nawe, zakubuyisela iimpondo
zeendlovu nemisimbithi, yaba sisithabathaba.

<span id="an_27:16">27:16</span> UAram warhwebelana nawe ngenxa
yobuninzi bezinto ozenzayo, bakurholela iikarbhunkolo, neengubo
ezimfusa, nezimfakamfele, nelinen ecikizekileyo, nekorale, neerubhi,
ngeempahla zakho.

<span id="an_27:17">27:17</span> ElakwaYuda nelizwe lakwaSirayeli
belingabarhwebeli bakho; barhwebisana nawe ngengqolowa yaseMiniti
nangemiqhathane, nangobusi, nangeoli, nangamafutha aqholiweyo.

<span id="an_27:18">27:18</span> IDamasko yarhwebelana nawe, ngenxa
yobuninzi bezinto ozenzayo, ngenxa yobuninzi bobuncwane bonke, ngewayini
yaseHelebhon nangoboya begusha obuqaqambileyo.

<span id="an_27:19">27:19</span> OoVedan noYavan waseUzali baye
bekurholela intsimbi ekhandiweyo; ikasiya nekalamo bezisekurhwebeni
kwakho.

<span id="an_27:20">27:20</span> UDedan ubengumrhwebeli wakho wezidwashu
zokukhwela.

<span id="an_27:21">27:21</span> Elakwa-Arabhi nezikhulu zonke
zakwaKedare bezirhwebisana nawe, zarhwebisana nawe ngamatakane,
nangeenkunzi zeegusha, nangeenkunzi zeebhokhwe.

<span id="an_27:22">27:22</span> Abarhwebi bakwaShebha nabakwaRama baye
bengabarhwebeli bakho, bakurholela ubulawu bonke obuyintloko, namatye
onke anqabileyo, negolide, ngeempahla zakho.

<span id="an_27:23">27:23</span> OoHaran noKane noEden, abarhwebi
bakwaShebha, nabaseAsiriya, nabaseKilemadi, baye bengabarhwebeli bakho;

<span id="an_27:24">27:24</span> babengabarhwebeli bakho ngeengubo
ezintle kwaphela, nangeengubo zokwaleka ezimsi nezimfakamfele,
nangemichako emabalabala. Ezo zinto zithandelwe zaqiniswa ngamaqamesi,
ukuba ziye emarikeni yakho.

<span id="an_27:25">27:25</span> Iinqanawa zaseTarshishe bezingabathuthi
bakho nabolwananiso lwakho. Wachuma ke, wazuka kakhulu embilinini
yeelwandle.

<span id="an_27:26">27:26</span> Bakusa emanzini amakhulu ababheqi
bakho; umoya wasempumalanga wakwaphula embilinini yeelwandle.

<span id="an_27:27">27:27</span> Ubuncwane bakho neempahla zakho
othengise ngazo, nezinto zakho ozananileyo, noomateloshe bakho,
nabaqhubi bakho, nabalungisi beentanda zakho, nabananisi beento zakho
zokwananwa, namadoda akho onke okulwa aphakathi kwakho, kunye nesikhungu
sakho sonke esiphakathi kwakho, baphalala embilinini yeelwandle ngemini
yokuwa kwakho.

<span id="an_27:28">27:28</span> Ngenxa yezwi lokukhala labaqhubi bakho,
ayanyikima amadlelo.

<span id="an_27:29">27:29</span> Bayehla emikhombeni yabo bonke ababheqi
noomateloshe, bonke abaqhubi baselwandle, beze kuma emhlabeni.

<span id="an_27:30">27:30</span> Baya kulivakalisa ilizwi labo phezu
kwakho, bakhale kakrakra, bazigalele ngothuli ezintloko, bazigalele
ngothuthu.

<span id="an_27:31">27:31</span> Bozicheba iintloko ngenxa yakho,
babhinqe ezirhwexayo, bakulilele ngobukrakra bomphefumlo wabo,
bembambazela kakrakra.

<span id="an_27:32">27:32</span> Bokuphakamisela isimbonono esimemeni
sabo, bakwenzele isimbonono, besithi, Ngubani na onjengeTire,
onjengobethwe wathi cwaka embilinini yeelwandle?

<span id="an_27:33">27:33</span> Ekuphumeni kweempahla zakho othengise
ngazo ezilwandle, wahluthisa izizwe ezininzi; ngobuninzi bobuncwane
bakho nobolwananiso lwakho wabatyebisa ookumkani behlabathi.

<span id="an_27:34">27:34</span> Kungoku, waphukile nje, umkile
ezilwandle, ezinzulwini zamanzi; luwile nawe ulwananiso lwakho,
nesikhungu sakho sonke.

<span id="an_27:35">27:35</span> Bonke abemi beziqithi baya kumangaliswa
nguwe, ookumkani bazo babe namanwele benamanwele, buthe ntshwa ubuso
babo.

<span id="an_27:36">27:36</span> Abarhwebi abasezizweni baya kwenza
umsondlo; usuke wena ube sisikhwankqiso, ungabi sabakho naphakade.

<span id="an_28:1">28:1</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_28:2">28:2</span> Nyana womntu, Yithi kwinganga yeTire,
Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ngenxa enokuba intliziyo yakho iphakamile,
usithi, NdinguThixo, ndihleli esihlalweni soThixo embilinini yeelwandle;
phofu ungumntu, ungeThixo, nakuba uyenze intliziyo yakho
yanjengentliziyo yoThixo:

<span id="an_28:3">28:3</span> yabona, ulumke kambe nangaphezu
koDaniyeli; zonke izinto ezisitheleyo azisithelisiwe kuwe.

<span id="an_28:4">28:4</span> Ngobulumko bakho nangengqondo yakho
uzenzele ubuhandiba, wangenisa igolide nesilivere ebuncwaneni bakho.

<span id="an_28:5">28:5</span> Ngobuninzi bobulumko bakho ubandisile
ubuhandiba bakho, ngorhwebo lwakho, yaphakama intliziyo yakho
ngobuhandiba bakho.

<span id="an_28:6">28:6</span> Ngako oko, itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ngenxa enokuba wayenza intliziyo yakho yanjengentliziyo yoThixo,

<span id="an_28:7">28:7</span> ngako oko, uyabona, ndiya kukuzisela
abasemzini, abangcangcazelisi basezintlangeni; baburholele ubuhle
bobulumko bakho amakrele abo, bakuhlambele ukubengezela kwakho.

<span id="an_28:8">28:8</span> Baya kukuhlisela emhadini, ufe ngokufa
kwababuleweyo, embilinini yeelwandle.

<span id="an_28:9">28:9</span> Wotsho ubuye utsho na ukuthi,
NdinguThixo, phambi kombulali wakho? ungumntu nje, ungeThixo, esandleni
sokuhlabayo.

<span id="an_28:10">28:10</span> Uya kufa ukufa kwabangalukileyo
ngesandla sabasemzini, ngokuba ndithethile; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_28:11">28:11</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_28:12">28:12</span> Nyana womntu, mphakamisele isimbonono
ukumkani waseTire, uthi kuye, Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Wena lutywino
lwesakhiwo esilinganiselweyo kakuhle, uzeleyo bubulumko, umhle kwaphela.

<span id="an_28:13">28:13</span> Ubuse-Eden emyezweni kaThixo; onke
amatye anqabileyo abe esisigubungelo sakho: isardiyo, netopazi,
nedayimani, nekrizolite, nebherilo, neyaspisi, nesafire, nekarbhunkolo,
nesmarado, negolide; umsebenzi weengqondi zakho nowamankazana akho waye
ukuwe; ngemini yokudalwa kwakho ezo zinto zalungiswa.

<span id="an_28:14">28:14</span> Waye uyikerubhi ethanjisiweyo,
egqubuthelayo; ndakwenza ke, waba sentabeni engcwele kaThixo,
wahambahamba phakathi kwamatye anomlilo.

<span id="an_28:15">28:15</span> Wagqibelela ngeendlela zakho, kususela
kwimini yokudalwa kwakho, kwada kwafumaneka ubugqwetha kuwe.

<span id="an_28:16">28:16</span> Ngobuninzi borhwebo lwakho umbilini
wakho wazala kukugonyamela, wona ke. Ndiya kulahla wena, ngokwento
engcolileyo, umke entabeni kaThixo; ndikutshabalalise, kerubhi
igqubuthelayo, usuke phakathi kwamatye anomlilo.

<span id="an_28:17">28:17</span> Intliziyo yakho iphakamile ngenxa
yobuhle bakho, ubonakalisile ubulumko bakho kunye nokubengezela kwakho.
Ndikukhahlela emhlabeni ndikwenze ube ngumbonelo phambi kokumkani.

<span id="an_28:18">28:18</span> Ngobuninzi bobugwenxa bakho,
ebugqwetheni borhwebo lwakho, uzihlambele iingcwele zakho; ndivelisa ke
umlilo kwaphakathi kwakho; uya kukutshisa wona, ndikwenze ube luthuthu
emhlabeni, emehlweni abo bonke abakubonayo.

<span id="an_28:19">28:19</span> Bonke abakwaziyo ezizweni baya
kumangaliswa nguwe, usuke ube sisikhwankqiso, ungabuyi ubekho naphakade.

<span id="an_28:20">28:20</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaThixo kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_28:21">28:21</span> Nyana womntu, bhekisa ubuso bakho
eTsidon, uprofete ngayo.

<span id="an_28:22">28:22</span> Yithi, Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Uyabona, ndikuchasile, Tsidon; ndiya kuzizukisa phakathi kwakho; bazi
ukuba ndinguYehova, ekwenzeni kwam izigwebo kuyo, ndizingcwalisele kuyo.

<span id="an_28:23">28:23</span> Ndiya kuthumela kuyo indyikitya yokufa
negazi ezitratweni zayo; bawe abangxwelerhiweyo phakathi kwayo likrele,
eliyifikelayo ngeenxa zonke; bazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_28:24">28:24</span> Akuyi kuba sabakho meva anobuhlungu,
naluviko lwenza buhlungu, kwindlu kaSirayeli, luphuma kubo bonke
abangeenxa zonke kuyo, abayicukuleyo; bazi ke ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_28:25">28:25</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ekuyibutheni kwam indlu kaSirayeli, ezizweni abaphangalaliswe kuzo,
ndiya kuzingcwalisela kubo emehlweni eentlanga, bahlale emhlabeni wabo,
endawunika umkhonzi wam uYakobi.

<span id="an_28:26">28:26</span> Baya kuhlala kuwo bekholosile, bakhe
izindlu, batyale izidiliya, bahlale bekholosile ekwenzeni kwam izigwebo
kubo bonke ababacukulayo, abangeenxa zonke kubo; bazi ukuba ndinguYehova
uThixo wabo.

<span id="an_29:1">29:1</span> Ngomnyaka weshumi, ngenyanga yeshumi,
ngolweshumi elinesibini enyangeni leyo, kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum
lisithi,

<span id="an_29:2">29:2</span> Nyana womntu, bhekisa ubuso bakho kuFaro
ukumkani waseYiputa, uprofete ngaye, nangeYiputa yonke iphela.

<span id="an_29:3">29:3</span> Thetha uthi, Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Uyabona, ndikuchasile, Faro kumkani waseYiputa, ngwenya inkulu
ibuthumileyo emijelweni yayo yoMnayile, itsho ukuthi, Ngowam umlambo,
ndizenzele mna.

<span id="an_29:4">29:4</span> Ndiya kufaka amakhonkco emihlathini
yakho, ndizinamathisele emaxolweni akho iintlanzi zemijelo yakho,
ndikurhole emijelweni yakho, neentlanzi zonke zemijelo yakho,
ezinamathele emaxolweni akho.

<span id="an_29:5">29:5</span> Ndiya kukulahlela entlango, wena
neentlanzi zonke zemijelo yakho. Uya kuwa endle, akuyi kuhlanganiswa
ubuthwe; ndikunikele ukuba ube kukudla kwamarhamncwa elizwe nokweentaka
zezulu.

<span id="an_29:6">29:6</span> Baya kwazi bonke abemi baseYiputa ukuba
ndinguYehova. Ngokokuba ibe ingumsimelelo wengcongolo kwindlu
kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_29:7">29:7</span> Bakubambelela kuwe ngamahlamvu akho,
usuka uvikiveke, ukrazule lonke igxalaba labo; uthi bakusimelela ngawe,
waphuke, ugxadazelise zonke izinqe zabo.

<span id="an_29:8">29:8</span> Ngako oko, itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Uyabona, ndikuzisela ikrele, ndinqumle kuwe umntu nenkomo;

<span id="an_29:9">29:9</span> ilizwe laseYiputa kube senkangala,
libharhe; bazi ukuba ndinguYehova, ngenxa enokuba usithi, Umlambo
ngowam, ndizenzele mna.

<span id="an_29:10">29:10</span> Ngako oko uyabona, ndikuchasile
nemijelo yakho; ndiya kulibharhisa ilizwe laseYiputa libharhe, kube
senkangala, lithabathele eMigidoli, lise eSevene, lise emdeni
wakwaKushi.

<span id="an_29:11">29:11</span> Akuyi kucanda lunyawo lwamntu kulo,
akuyi kucanda nqina lankomo kulo, lingemiwa, iminyaka engamashumi amane.

<span id="an_29:12">29:12</span> Ndiya kulenza kube senkangala ilizwe
laseYiputa phakathi kwamazwe abharhileyo, ibe ngamanxuwa imizi yalo
phakathi kwemizi engamanxuwa, iminyaka engamashumi amane;
ndiwaphangalalisele amaYiputa ezintlangeni, ndiwachithachithe emazweni.

<span id="an_29:13">29:13</span> Ngokuba itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ekupheleni kweminyaka engamashumi amane, ndiya kuwabutha amaYiputa
ezizweni, abephangalaliselwe kuzo;

<span id="an_29:14">29:14</span> ndibuyise ukuthinjwa kweYiputa,
ndiwabuyise elizweni lasePatrosi, ezweni lokuvela kwawo, abe sisikumkani
esiphantsi khona.

<span id="an_29:15">29:15</span> Ezikumkanini aya kuba sesiphantsi,
angabi saziphakamisa ngokwawo phezu kweentlanga; ndiwanciphise, ukuze
angazinyatheleli phantsi iintlanga.

<span id="an_29:16">29:16</span> Akayi kuba saba yinkoloseko yendlu
kaSirayeli, ekhumbuza ubugwenxa ngokubheka kwayo kuwo; azi ukuba
ndiyiNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_29:17">29:17</span> Kwathi ngomnyaka wamashumi omabini
anesixhenxe, ngenyanga yokuqala, ngolokuqala enyangeni leyo, kwafika
ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_29:18">29:18</span> Nyana womntu, uNebhukadenetsare
ukumkani waseBhabheli, impi yakhe uyisebenzise umsebenzi omkhulu eTire.
Zonke iintloko zikhuthukile, onke amagxalaba atyabukile; ukanti akabanga
namvuzo ke, yena nempi yakhe, eTire, ngenxa yomsebenzi awusebenzileyo
kuyo.

<span id="an_29:19">29:19</span> Ngako oko, itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Uyabona, uNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli ndimnika ilizwe
laseYiputa, ukuba athuthe intabalala yalo, athimbe intimbo yalo, aphange
ixhoba lalo, ezo zinto zibe ngumvuzo wempi yakhe.

<span id="an_29:20">29:20</span> Umvuzo wakhe awusebenzeleyo ndimnika
ilizwe laseYiputa, ngokuba baye besebenzele mna; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_29:21">29:21</span> Ngayo loo mini ndiya kuyihlumisela
uphondo indlu kaSirayeli, ndikunike ukuvulwa komlomo phakathi kwabo;
bazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_30:1">30:1</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_30:2">30:2</span> Nyana womntu, profeta uthi, Itsho iNkosi
uYehova ukuthi, Bhombolozani, nithi, Hayi ke, le mini!

<span id="an_30:3">30:3</span> Ngokuba ikufuphi le mini, ikufuphi imini
kaYehova, imini yamafu; iya kuba lixesha leentlanga.

<span id="an_30:4">30:4</span> Ikrele liya kuyifikela iYiputa; kuya
kubakho ukuzibhijabhija kwaKushi, ekuweni kwababuleweyo eYiputa,
ithatyathwe intabalala yayo, zichithwe iziseko zayo.

<span id="an_30:5">30:5</span> AmaKushi, namaPuti, namaLudi, nomxukuxela
wonke, namaKubhi, noonyana belizwe lomnqophiso, baya kuwa likrele
ndawonye nayo.

<span id="an_30:6">30:6</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Baya kuwa abaxhasi
beYiputa, lihle iqhayiya lamandla ayo. Baya kuthabathela iMigidoli, base
eSevene, besiwa likrele kuyo; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_30:7">30:7</span> KwelamaYiputa koba senkangala phakathi
kwamazwe abharhileyo, nemizi yalo ibe phakathi kwemizi engamanxuwa;

<span id="an_30:8">30:8</span> bazi ukuba ndinguYehova, ekufakeni kwam
umlilo eYiputa, baphuke bonke abancedi balo.

<span id="an_30:9">30:9</span> Ngayo loo mini kuya kuphuma kum
abathunywa ngeenqanawa, ukuze bothuse amaKushi akholosileyo,
azibhijabhije ngokwawo njengasemini yeYiputa; ngokuba, uyabona, iyeza le
nto.

<span id="an_30:10">30:10</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ndiya
kuyiphelisa ingxokolo yeYiputa ngesandla sikaNebhukadenetsare, ukumkani
waseBhabheli.

<span id="an_30:11">30:11</span> Yena enabantu bakhe, abangcangcazelisi
basezintlangeni, baya kuziswa ukuba balitshabalalise ilizwe, bayirholele
amakrele abo iYiputa, balizalise ilizwe ngababuleweyo.

<span id="an_30:12">30:12</span> Ndoyomisa imijelo yoMnayile,
ndithengise ngelizwe ezandleni zabanobubi, ndilenze kube senkangala
ilizwe nenzaliseko yalo, ngezandla zabasemzini; mna Yehova ndithethile.

<span id="an_30:13">30:13</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ndiya
kuzidakisa izigodo, ndiziphelise izithixo ezingento eNofu, kungabi
sabakho sikhulu sasezweni laseYiputa, ndingenise ukoyika ezweni
laseYiputa.

<span id="an_30:14">30:14</span> Ndiya kuyenza kube senkangala iPatrosi,
ndifake umlilo eTsohan, ndenze izigwebo kwiNo;

<span id="an_30:15">30:15</span> ndobuthulula ubushushu bam phezu
kweSin, inqaba yaseYiputa; ndiyinqumle ingxokolo yaseNo;

<span id="an_30:16">30:16</span> ndifake umlilo eYiputa. ISin iya
kuzibhijabhija izibhijabhije, neNo inqikwe, neNofu ibe nababandezeli
emini.

<span id="an_30:17">30:17</span> Amadodana aseAven nasePibhesete aya
kuwa likrele, yona ke loo mizi ithinjwe.

<span id="an_30:18">30:18</span> ETapanesi iya kuba mnyama imini,
ekuzaphuleni kwam khona iidyokhwe zaseYiputa, liphele kuyo iqhayiya
lamandla ayo. Amafu aya kuyisibekela, namagxamesi ayo athinjwe;

<span id="an_30:19">30:19</span> ndenze izigwebo eYiputa; bazi ukuba
ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_30:20">30:20</span> Kwathi ngomnyaka weshumi elinamnye,
ngenyanga yokuqala, ngolwesixhenxe enyangeni leyo, kwafika ilizwi
likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_30:21">30:21</span> Nyana womntu, ingalo kaFaro ukumkani
waseYiputa ndiyaphule; uyabona, ayiyi kubotshwa ukuba ifakwe umhlabelo,
ukuba ibotshwe ngezithandelo, ukuba yomelele, ukuba iphathe ikrele.

<span id="an_30:22">30:22</span> Ngako oko, itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Yabona, ndimchasile uFaro ukumkani waseYiputa. Ndiya kuzaphula iingalo
zakhe, eyomeleleyo kwaneyaphukileyo, ndilivuthulule ikrele esandleni
sakhe.

<span id="an_30:23">30:23</span> Ndowaphangalalisela amaYiputa
ezintlangeni, ndiwachithachithe emazweni;

<span id="an_30:24">30:24</span> ndiya kuzomeleza ke iingalo zokumkani
waseBhabheli, ndibeke ikrele lam esandleni sakhe, ndizaphule iingalo
zikaFaro, ancwine phambi kwakhe ngoncwino longxwelerhiweyo.

<span id="an_30:25">30:25</span> Ndiya kuzomeleza iingalo zokumkani
waseBhabheli, ziwe iingalo zikaFaro; bazi ukuba ndinguYehova,
ekulibekeni kwam ikrele esandleni sokumkani waseBhabheli, alolulele
phezu kwelizwe laseYiputa.

<span id="an_30:26">30:26</span> Ndowaphangalalisela amaYiputa
ezintlangeni, ndiwachithachithe emazweni; bazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_31:1">31:1</span> Ke kaloku kwathi, ngomnyaka weshumi
elinamnye, ngenyanga yesithathu, ngolokuqala enyangeni leyo, kwafika
ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_31:2">31:2</span> Nyana womntu, yithi kuFaro ukumkani
waseYiputa, nakwingxokolo yakhe, Ufana nabani na ngobukhulu bakho?

<span id="an_31:3">31:3</span> Uyabona, uAsiriya ebengumsedare
waseLebhanon, omasebe mahle, eyintshinyela yemithi enomthunzi,
ephakamile ngobude; aba phakathi kweengqimba zamafu amantloko akhe.

<span id="an_31:4">31:4</span> Amanzi amkhulisa, amanzi enzonzobila
amphakamisa, imilambo yawo yahamba ngeenxa zonke elutyalweni lwawo,
athumela imijelo yawo kuyo yonke imithi yasendle.

<span id="an_31:5">31:5</span> Ngako oko, ubude bakhe baphakama, baba
ngaphezu kwayo yonke imithi yasendle; iimbaxa zakhe zanda, namahlamvu
akhe aba made, ngenxa yamanzi amaninzi ekunabeni kwakhe.

<span id="an_31:6">31:6</span> Zonke iintaka zezulu zakha ezimbaxeni
zakhe, zonke izinto eziphilileyo zasendle zazakhela phantsi kwamahlamvu
akhe; zonke iintlanga ezinkulu zahlala emthunzini wakhe.

<span id="an_31:7">31:7</span> Wamhle ngobukhulu bakhe, ngobude bamasebe
akhe; ngokuba ingcambu yakhe yabe isemanzini amaninzi.

<span id="an_31:8">31:8</span> Imisedare esemyezweni kaThixo
ayimsithanga; imisipres ayifananga neembaxa zakhe, nemipleyini ayibanga
njengamahlamvu akhe; yonke imithi emyezweni kaThixo ayifananga naye
ngobuhle bayo.

<span id="an_31:9">31:9</span> Ndamenza mhle ngobuninzi bamasebe akhe,
yaba nomona ngaye yonke imithi yase-Eden, esemyezweni kaThixo.

<span id="an_31:10">31:10</span> Ngako oko yatsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ngenxa enokuba eziphakamisile ngobude, wawanyusela amantloko akhe
phakathi kweengqimba zamafu, yazinyusa intliziyo yakhe ngokuphakama
kwakhe:

<span id="an_31:11">31:11</span> ndiya kumnikela esandleni senjengele
yeentlanga; inene, iya kumphatha ngesiko layo; ndamgxotha ngenxa
yokungendawo kwakhe.

<span id="an_31:12">31:12</span> Bamnqumla abasemzini, abangcangcazelisi
basezintlangeni bamlahla. Ezintabeni nasemifuleni yonke awa amasebe
akhe; amahlamvu akhe aphukela ezihlanjeni zehlabathi lonke; zehla zemka
emthunzini wakhe zonke izizwe zehlabathi, zamlahla.

<span id="an_31:13">31:13</span> Phezu kwesibili sakhe esiwileyo kuhlala
zonke iintaka zezulu, zifike emahlamvini akhe zonke izinto eziphilileyo
zasendle;

<span id="an_31:14">31:14</span> ukuze ingaziphakamisi ngenxa yobude
bayo yonke imithi yasemanzini, ingawanyuseli phakathi kweengqimba zamafu
amantloko ayo, ingazimeli ngokwayo ekuziphakamiseni kwayo, yonke esela
amanzi. Ngokuba bonke bephela banikelwe ekufeni, ezweni langaphantsi,
phakathi koonyana baka-Adam, kwabahle baya embadini.

<span id="an_31:15">31:15</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ngemini
yokuhla kwakhe ukuya kwelabafileyo, ndabanga isijwili; ndawagqubuthela
ngenxa yakhe amanzi anzongonzongo, ndathintela imilambo yawo, avingcelwa
amanzi amakhulu. Ndayambathisa iLebhanon ngezimnyama zokuzila ngenxa
yakhe, yonke imithi yasendle yetha amandla ngenxa yakhe.

<span id="an_31:16">31:16</span> Ngesithonga sokuwa kwakhe
ndazinyikimisa iintlanga, ekumhliseleni kwam ukuba aye kwelabafileyo,
nabahle baya emhadini; yathuthuzeleka ezweni langaphantsi yonke imithi
yase-Eden, enyuliweyo emihle yaseLebhanon, yonke esela amanzi.

<span id="an_31:17">31:17</span> Nabo njengaye behla baya kwelabafileyo,
kwababuleweyo ngekrele; ababeyingalo yakhe, behleli emthunzini wakhe
phakathi kweentlanga.

<span id="an_31:18">31:18</span> Kunjalonje, ufana nabani na
ngobuqaqawuli nangobukhulu emithini yase-Eden? Uya kuhliselwa nemithi
yase-Eden ezweni langaphantsi; uya kulala phakathi kwabangalukileyo,
kwanababuleweyo ngekrele. NguFaro ke lowo, nengxokolo yakhe yonke; itsho
iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_32:1">32:1</span> Ke kaloku kwathi ngomnyaka weshumi
elinesibini, ngenyanga yeshumi elinesibini, ngolokuqala enyangeni leyo,
kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_32:2">32:2</span> Nyana womntu, menzele isimbonono uFaro
ukumkani waseYiputa, uthi kuye, Wafanekiswa nengonyama entsha
yeentlanga, nakuba ube unjengengwenya elwandle; waxhuma emilanjeni
yakho, wawagxobha amanzi ngamathupha akho, wayinyathela imilambo yawo.

<span id="an_32:3">32:3</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ndiya
kuwutwabulula phezu kwakho umnatha wam, kunye nesikhungu sezizwe
ezininzi, zikunyuse ngomnatha wam.

<span id="an_32:4">32:4</span> Ndiya kukulahlela emhlabeni, ndikujulele
ebusweni belizwe, ndizihlalise phezu kwakho zonke iintaka zezulu,
ndizihluthise ngawe izinto eziphilileyo zehlabathi lonke.

<span id="an_32:5">32:5</span> Ndoyibeka phezu kweentaba inyama yakho,
ndiyizalise imifula ngezidumbu zakho;

<span id="an_32:6">32:6</span> ndiliseze ihlabathi ngokuphalala kwegazi
lakho, lise ezintabeni; zizale izihlambo nguwe.

<span id="an_32:7">32:7</span> Ndiya kulisibekelisa izulu ekukucimeni
kwam, ndizambathise iinkwenkwezi zalo ngezimnyama zokuzila. Ndiya
kulisibekela ilanga ngamafu, nenyanga ingakhanyisi ngokukhanya kwayo.

<span id="an_32:8">32:8</span> Zonke izikhanyiso ezikhanyisayo ezulwini
ndiya kuzambathisa ngezimnyama zokuzila ngenxa yakho, ndenze ubumnyama
phezu kwelizwe lakho; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_32:9">32:9</span> Ndoyenza ibe buhlungu intliziyo
yeentlanga ezininzi, ekukuseni kwam ukwaphulwa kwakho ezintlangeni,
emazweni ongawazanga.

<span id="an_32:10">32:10</span> Ndiya kuzimangalisisa ngawe izizwe
ezininzi, babe namanwele nokuba namanwele ngawe ookumkani bazo,
ekulilingiseni ikrele lam ebusweni babo, bagubhe ngamaphanyazo onke,
elowo ngenxa yomphefumlo wakhe, ngemini yokuwa kwakho.

<span id="an_32:11">32:11</span> Ngokuba itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Ikrele lokumkani waseBhabheli liya kukufikela.

<span id="an_32:12">32:12</span> Ndiya kuyiwisa ingxokolo yakho
ngamakrele amagorha; ngabangcangcazelisi basezintlangeni bonke bephala;
balibhuqe ikratshi leYiputa, itshabalale yonke ingxokolo yayo.

<span id="an_32:13">32:13</span> Ndiya kuzitshabalalisa zonke iinkomo
zayo, zimke emanzini amakhulu, lungabi sawagxobha unyawo lomntu,
namanqina eenkomo angawagxobhi.

<span id="an_32:14">32:14</span> Oko ndiya kuwawuthisa amanzi ayo,
nemilambo yayo, ndiyihambise ngokweoli; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_32:15">32:15</span> Ndakulenza kube senkangala ilizwe
laseYiputa, lenziwe ke kube senkangala ilizwe, lingabi nayo inzaliseko
yalo, ekubaxabeleni kwam bonke abemi balo: baya kwazi ukuba
ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_32:16">32:16</span> Siso esi isimbonono; siya kuvunywa
ngokwesimbonono; iintombi zeentlanga ziya kuyivuma ngokwesimbonono;
ngeYiputa nangengxokolo yayo yonke, ziya kuyivuma ngokwesimbonono; itsho
iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_32:17">32:17</span> Ke kaloku kwathi ngomnyaka weshumi
elinesibini, ngolweshumi elinesihlanu enyangeni leyo, kwafika ilizwi
likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_32:18">32:18</span> Nyana womntu, yenza isimema ngengxokolo
yaseYiputa, uyihlisele, yona nentombi yeentlanga eziziingangamsha,
ezweni langaphandle, nabahle baya emhadini.

<span id="an_32:19">32:19</span> Udlule bani na ngobuhle bakho? Yihla,
ulale kwabangalukileyo.

<span id="an_32:20">32:20</span> Baya kuwa phakathi kwababuleweyo
ngekrele; ikrele linikelwe esandleni; yiqweqwediseni, nengxokolo yayo
yonke.

<span id="an_32:21">32:21</span> Ziya kuthetha ngaye iinjengele
zamagorha phakathi kwelabafileyo, nabancedi bakhe, zithi, Behlile,
balele khona abangalukileyo, bebulewe ngekrele.

<span id="an_32:22">32:22</span> Ukhona uAsiriya nebandla lakhe lonke;
ngeenxa zonke kuye ngamangcwaba abo, bonke bephela bebulewe, bewe
likrele; abamangcwaba abo enziwe emhadini phakathi,

<span id="an_32:23">32:23</span> ibandla lakhe lingeenxa zonke
engcwabeni lakhe; bonke bephela bebulewe, bewe likrele, abaye besothusa
ilizwe labahleliyo.

<span id="an_32:24">32:24</span> Ukhona uElam, nengxokolo yakhe yonke
engeenxa zonke engcwabeni lakhe; bonke bephela bebulewe, bewe likrele,
ababehle baya ezweni langaphantsi bengalukile; abaye besothusa ilizwe
labahleliyo, bathwala ihlazo labo nabehle baya emhadini.

<span id="an_32:25">32:25</span> Bamenzela isilili phakathi
kwababuleweyo, enengxokolo yakhe yonke; aba ngeenxa zonke kuye
amangcwaba ayo; bonke bephela bengalukile, bebulewe ngekrele; ngokuba
bothusa abasezweni labahleliyo, bathwala ihlazo nabehle baya emhadini;
ubekwe phakathi kwababuleweyo.

<span id="an_32:26">32:26</span> Ukhona uMesheki-Tubhali, nengxokolo
yakhe yonke, engeenxa zonke kuye amangcwaba ayo; bonke bephela
bengalukile, bebulewe ngekrele; ngokuba besothuse ilizwe labahleliyo.

<span id="an_32:27">32:27</span> Ke abayi kulala namagorha awileyo
angawabangalukileyo, abehlayo baya kwelabafileyo beneempahla zokulwa,
ebekwe amakrele abo phantsi kweentloko zabo; ubugwenxa babo buwafikele
amathambo abo; ngokuba baye besothusa amagorha ezweni labahleliyo.

<span id="an_32:28">32:28</span> Nawe ke uya kwaphulwa phakathi
kwabangalukileyo, ulale nababuleweyo ngekrele.

<span id="an_32:29">32:29</span> Ukhona uEdom, ookumkani bakhe nezikhulu
zakhe zonke, abathi benobugorha babekwa kwababuleweyo ngekrele; balala
nabangalukileyo, nabehle baya emhadini.

<span id="an_32:30">32:30</span> Zikhona iinkosi zasentla, zonke
ziphela, namaTsidon onke, ezehlayo nababuleweyo; zidanile, noko
beziqhiphukisa umbilini ngobugorha bazo; zilele zingabangalukileyo
kwanababuleweyo ngekrele, zithwele ihlazo lazo nabehle baya emhadini.

<span id="an_32:31">32:31</span> UFaro uya kubabona, athuthuzeleke
ngenxa yengxokolo yakhe yonke; uFaro ubulewe ngekrele nempi yakhe yonke;
itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_32:32">32:32</span> Ngokuba ndamnika ukuba othuse ilizwe
labahleliyo; ulalisiwe ke phakathi kwabangalukileyo, kwanababuleweyo
ngekrele, uFaro nengxokolo yakhe yonke; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_33:1">33:1</span> Ke kaloku kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum,
lisithi,

<span id="an_33:2">33:2</span> Nyana womntu, thetha koonyana babantu
bakowenu, uthi kubo, Xa ndithe ilizwe ndalizisela ikrele, abantu belizwe
elo bathabatha indoda yaseziphelweni zabo, bayimisa ukuba ibe
ngumboniseli wabo;

<span id="an_33:3">33:3</span> yabona ikrele lilifikela ilizwe elo,
yavuthela isigodlo, yabavusa abantu;

<span id="an_33:4">33:4</span> ke umntu othe waliva izwi lesigodlo,
akavuswa, lafika ikrele elo, lamthabatha: loba sentlokweni yakhe igazi
lakhe.

<span id="an_33:5">33:5</span> Izwi lesigodlo ulivile, akavuswa, igazi
lakhe loba phezu kwakhe; evusiwe, ange ewusizile umphefumlo wakhe.

<span id="an_33:6">33:6</span> Umboniseli lowo, xa athe walibona ikrele
lisiza, akavuthela isigodlo, akabavusa abantu; lafika ikrele, lathabatha
kubo umphefumlo: lowo uthatyathwe ngobugwenxa bakhe, ke igazi lakhe
ndolibiza esandleni somboniseli lowo.

<span id="an_33:7">33:7</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, ndikwenze waba
ngumboniseli kwindlu kaSirayeli; woliva emlonyeni wam ilizwi,
ubavuselele ngokuphuma kum.

<span id="an_33:8">33:8</span> Ndakuthi kongendawo, Wena ungendawo, uya
kufa, inene; usuke ungathethi wena, ukuba umvuselele ongendawo, emke
endleleni yakhe: wofa yena ongendawo ngobugwenxa bakhe, ke igazi lakhe
ndolifuna esandleni sakho.

<span id="an_33:9">33:9</span> Wena ke, xa uthe wamvuselela ongendawo
endleleni yakhe, ukuba abuye kuyo, akabuya endleleni yakhe: wofa yena
ngobugwenxa bakhe, ke wena uwuhlangule umphefumlo wakho.

<span id="an_33:10">33:10</span> Ke kaloku wena, nyana womntu, yithi
kwindlu kaSirayeli, Niyalungisa ukuthi, Izikreqo zethu nezono zethu
ziphezu kwethu; siyangcungcutheka kuzo; singathini na ukuphila?

<span id="an_33:11">33:11</span> Yithi kubo, Ndihleli nje, itsho iNkosi
uYehova, unakanye ukuba kube mnandi kum ukufa kongendawo; kumnandi kum
ukubuya kongendawo endleleni yakhe, aphile. Buyani, buyani ezindleleni
zenu ezimbi! Yini na ukuba nide nife, ndlu kaSirayeli?

<span id="an_33:12">33:12</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, yithi koonyana
babantu bakowenu, Ubulungisa belungisa abuyi kulihlangula ngemini
yokreqo lwalo; ongendawo akayi kukhubeka ngokungendawo kwakhe, ngemini
yokubuya kwakhe kokungendawo kwakhe; nelungisa aliyi kuphila ngabo
ngemini yokona kwalo.

<span id="an_33:13">33:13</span> Ndakuthi kwilungisa, inene, lophila;
lize ke likholose ngobulungisa balo, lenze ngobugqwetha: bonke
ubulungisa balo abuyi kukhunjulwa; lofa ngobugqwetha balo elibenzileyo.

<span id="an_33:14">33:14</span> Ndakuthi kongendawo, Inene, uya kufa;
abuye ekoneni kwakhe, enze ngokusesikweni nangobulungisa;

<span id="an_33:15">33:15</span> ongendawo asibuyise isibambiso,
ayimisele into ehluthwe nguye, ahambe ngemimiselo yobomi, angenzi
ngobugqwetha: inene, wophila, akayi kufa.

<span id="an_33:16">33:16</span> Zonke izono zakhe awona ngazo aziyi
kukhunjulelwa kuye; wenze ngokusesikweni nangobulungisa; inene, wophila.

<span id="an_33:17">33:17</span> Bathi ke oonyana bakowenu, Indlela
kaYehova ayilungelelene; kanti ngabo, abandlela ingalungeleleneyo.

<span id="an_33:18">33:18</span> Lakubuya ilungisa ebulungiseni balo,
lenze ngobugqwetha, lofa ngabo.

<span id="an_33:19">33:19</span> Akubuya ongendawo kokungendawo kwakhe,
enze ngokusesikweni nangobulungisa, inene, wophila ngenxa yoko.

<span id="an_33:20">33:20</span> Nithi ke, Indlela yeNkosi
ayilungelelene. Ndiya kunigweba, elowo ngokweendlela zakhe, ndlu
kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_33:21">33:21</span> Ke kaloku kwathi ngomnyaka weshumi
elinesibini emva kokuthinjwa kwethu, ngenyanga yeshumi, ngolwesihlanu
enyangeni leyo, kwafika kum osindileyo eYerusalem, wathi, Umzi ubulewe.

<span id="an_33:22">33:22</span> Isandla sikaYehova saba phezu kwam
ngokuhlwa, ngaphambi kokufika kosindileyo. Wawuvula ke umlomo wam, wada
wafika kum kusasa; wavuleka umlomo wam, andaba saba sisidenge.

<span id="an_33:23">33:23</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_33:24">33:24</span> Nyana womntu, abahleli emanxuweni
emhlabeni wakwaSirayeli batsho ukuthi, uAbraham wayemnye, walidla ilifa
ilizwe; ke thina sibaninzi, silinikiwe ilizwe ukuba silidle ilifa.

<span id="an_33:25">33:25</span> Ngako oko yithi kubo, Itsho iNkosi
uYehova ukuthi, Nidla into enegazi, amehlo enu niwaphakamisele
ezigodweni zenu, niphalaze igazi; nolidla ilifa na ke ilizwe?

<span id="an_33:26">33:26</span> Nimi ngekrele lenu, nenza amasikizi,
nithi elowo nimenze inqambi umfazi wommelwane wakhe; nolidla ilifa na ke
izilwe?

<span id="an_33:27">33:27</span> Yitsho kubo ukuthi, Itsho iNkosi
uYehova ukuthi, Ndihleli nje, abo basemanxuweni baya kuwa likrele; lo
usendle ndimnikele emarhamncweni, ukuba amdle; bafe yindyikitya yokufa
abasezimboniselweni nasemiqolombeni.

<span id="an_33:28">33:28</span> Ndiya kulenza kube senkangala
yakwankangala ilizwe, liphele iqhayiya lamandla alo, zibe senkangala
iintaba zakwaSirayeli, kungacandi bani kuzo;

<span id="an_33:29">33:29</span> bazi ukuba ndinguYehova, ndakulenza
kube senkangala yakwankangala ilizwe, ngenxa yamasikizi onke
ababewenzile.

<span id="an_33:30">33:30</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, oonyana babantu
bakowenu bancokola ngawe ngasezindongeni naseminyango yezindlu, elowo
ethetha nomnye, elowo nomzalwana wakhe, esithi, Khanize, sive ukuba
lilizwi eliyini na eliphuma kuYehova.

<span id="an_33:31">33:31</span> Beza kuwe njengokuza kwabantu, bahlale
phambi kwakho ngokwabantu bam, baweve amazwi akho, bangawenzi; kuba
benza okukhanukwa ngumlomo wabo; intliziyo yabo ilandela inzuzo yabo
embi.

<span id="an_33:32">33:32</span> Yabona, kubo unjengovuma ingoma
emnandi, ozwi liyolileyo, olungisayo ukubetha uhadi; baweve amazwi akho,
bangawenzi noko.

<span id="an_33:33">33:33</span> Kothi ke kwakufika oko—nanko
kusiza—bazi, ukuba bekukho umprofeti phakathi kwabo.

<span id="an_34:1">34:1</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_34:2">34:2</span> Nyana womntu, profeta ngabalusi
bakwaSirayeli; profeta, uthi kubo, ngabalusi abo, Itsho iNkosi uYehova
ukuthi, Yeha ke abalusi bakwaSirayeli, abaye bezalusa ngokwabo! Abalusi
babengafanele ukwalusa umhlambi wabo, yini na?

<span id="an_34:3">34:3</span> Amanqatha niyawadla, uboya nizambathise
ngabo; ezityetyisiweyo izimvu niyazixhela, umhlambi aniwalusi.

<span id="an_34:4">34:4</span> Ezityhafileyo anizomelezi, ezifayo
aniziphilisi, ezaphukileyo anizibophi, eziziintsali anizibuyisi,
ezidakileyo anizifuni; nizinyathela ngamandla kalukhuni.

<span id="an_34:5">34:5</span> Zaba lusali ngokungabi namalusi; zaba
kukudla kwamarhamncwa onke asendle, zaba lusali.

<span id="an_34:6">34:6</span> Umhlambi wam wadungudela ezintabeni
zonke, nasezindulini zonke ezinde, waba lusali umhlambi wam ebusweni
bonke belizwe. Akubangakho namnye uwukhathalelayo, akwabakho namnye
uwufunayo.

<span id="an_34:7">34:7</span> Ngako oko, balusindini, liveni ilizwi
likaYehova, lisithi,

<span id="an_34:8">34:8</span> Ndihleli nje, itsho iNkosi uYehova,
inyaniso, ngenxa enokuba umhlambi wam ulixhoba, umhlambi wam udliwa
ngamarhamncwa onke asendle, ngokungabi namalusi; abalusi bam
bengawukhathaleli umhlambi wam, abalusi bezalusa ngokwabo, bengawalusi
umhlambi wam:

<span id="an_34:9">34:9</span> ngako oko, balusindini, liveni ilizwi
likaYehova, lisithi,

<span id="an_34:10">34:10</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Yabonani,
ndibachasile ibalusi. Ndiya kuwubiza umhlambi wam ezandleni zabo,
ndibanqumamise ekwaluseni umhlambi wam, bangabi sazalusa ngokwabo
abalusi; ndiwuhlangule umhlambi wam emlonyeni wabo, ungabi saba kukudla
kubo.

<span id="an_34:11">34:11</span> Ngokuba itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Yabonani, mna ngokwam ndiya kuwukhathalela umhlambi wam, ndiwuvelele.

<span id="an_34:12">34:12</span> Njengoko umalusi awuvelelayo umhlambi
wakhe, ngemini yokubakho kwakhe phakathi komhlambi wakhe othiwe saa qhu,
ndiya kwenjenjalo ukuwuvelela umhlambi wam; ndiwuhlangule ezindaweni
zonke, owaba lusali kuzo ngemini enamafu, enamafu amnyama.

<span id="an_34:13">34:13</span> Ndiya kuwukhupha ezizweni, ndiwubuthe
emazweni, ndiwuse emhlabeni wawo, ndiwalusele ezintabeni zakwaSirayeli,
ezihlanjeni nasezindaweni zonke ezimiweyo zelizwe.

<span id="an_34:14">34:14</span> Ndiya kuwalusela ebutyanini
obulungileyo, libe sezintabeni ezinde zakwaSirayeli idlelo lawo;
edlelweni elilungileyo, uya kubutha khona, udle utyani obutyebileyo
ezintabeni zakwaSirayeli.

<span id="an_34:15">34:15</span> Mna ndiya kuwalusa umhlambi wam,
ndiwenze ubuthe mna; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_34:16">34:16</span> Ezilahlekileyo ndiya kuzifuna,
ndibuyise eziziintsali, ndibophe ezaphukileyo, ndizomeleze ezifayo; ke
ezityebileyo ndozitshabalalisa, nezomeleleyo ndizaluse ngokusesikweni.

<span id="an_34:17">34:17</span> Nina ke, mhlambi wam, itsho iNkosi
uYehova ukuthi, Yabonani, ndiya kugweba phakathi kweegusha neegusha,
naphakathi kweenkunzi zeegusha neenkunzi zeebhokhwe.

<span id="an_34:18">34:18</span> Yinto encinane na kuni, ukuthi nibudle
utyani obulungileyo, nize okuseleyo kotyani nikunyhashe ngamanqina enu?
nisele amanzi angcwengekileyo, niwagxobhe aseleyo ngamanqina enu?

<span id="an_34:19">34:19</span> Umhlambi wam udla obunyhashiweyo
ngamanquna enu; usela agxojiweyo ngamanqina enu.

<span id="an_34:20">34:20</span> Ngako oko itsho iNkosi uYehova kuzo
ukuthi, Yabonani, mna ndiya kugweba phakathi kweegusha ezityebileyo
neegusha ezinqinileyo.

<span id="an_34:21">34:21</span> Ngenxa enokuba nityhala ngehleza
nangegxalaba, nizihlabe ngeempondo zenu ezityhafileyo zonke, nide
nizenze zibe lusali, zigqibe ilizwe:

<span id="an_34:22">34:22</span> ndowusindisa umhlambi wam, ungabi saba
lixhoba, ndigwebe phakathi kweegusha neegusha.

<span id="an_34:23">34:23</span> Ndomisa phezu kwawo umalusi abe mnye,
awaluse, umkhonzi wam uDavide; yena uya kuwalusa, abe ngumalusi wawo
yena;

<span id="an_34:24">34:24</span> mna Yehova ndibe nguThixo wawo,
umkhonzi wam uDavide abe sisikhulu phakathi kwawo; mna Yehova
ndithethile.

<span id="an_34:25">34:25</span> Ndiya kuwenzela umnqophiso woxolo,
ndiwaphelise amarhamncwa amabi elizweni, uhlale entlango ukholosile,
ulale emahlathini.

<span id="an_34:26">34:26</span> Ndowenza wona, kwaneendawo ezingeenxa
zonke endulini yam, ube yintsikelelo; ndihlise imvula ngexesha elililo;
iya kuba yimvula yentsikelelo.

<span id="an_34:27">34:27</span> Umthi wasendle wonika isiqhamo sawo,
ilizwe linike indyebo yalo, banqabe emhlabeni wabo; bazi ukuba
ndinguYehova, ekuzaphuleni kwam izikeyi zedyokhwe, ndibahlangule
esandleni sabo babebakhonzisa.

<span id="an_34:28">34:28</span> Abayi kuba saba lixhoba leentlanga,
angabadli amarhamncwa elizwe; bahlale bekholosile, kungabikho
ubothusayo.

<span id="an_34:29">34:29</span> Ndobavelisela isityalo sokuba ludumo,
bangabi sasuswa yindlala ezweni, bangabi sathwala hlazo leentlanga.

<span id="an_34:30">34:30</span> Baya kwazi ukuba mna Yehova Thixo wabo
ndinabo, bangabantu bam bona, indlu kaSirayeli; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_34:31">34:31</span> Nina ke ningumhlambi wam, umhlambi
wedlelo lam; nisisintu, ndinguThixo wenu; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_35:1">35:1</span> Ke kaloku kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum,
lisithi,

<span id="an_35:2">35:2</span> Nyana womntu, bhekisa ubuso bakho
entabeni yakwaSehire, uprofete ngayo,

<span id="an_35:3">35:3</span> uthi kuyo, Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Yabona, ndikuchasile, ntaba yakwaSehire. Ndosolulela isandla sam phezu
kwakho, ndikwenze kube senkangala yakwankangala.

<span id="an_35:4">35:4</span> Imizi yakho ndiya kuyenza amanxuwa, ube
senkangala; wazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_35:5">35:5</span> Ngenxa enokuba waba nobutshaba
obungunaphakade, wabanikela esandleni sekrele oonyana bakaSirayeli
ngexesha lokusindeka kwabo, ngexesha lobugwenxa bokuphela:

<span id="an_35:6">35:6</span> ngako oko, ndihleli nje, itsho iNkosi
uYehova, ndiya kukwenza igazi; lokusukela ke igazi; ngokokuba
ungalithiyanga igazi, lokusukela igazi.

<span id="an_35:7">35:7</span> Ndoyenza kube senkangala yakwankangala
intaba yakwaSehire, ndinqumle kuyo odlulayo nobuyayo.

<span id="an_35:8">35:8</span> Ndiya kuzizalisa iintaba zakhe
ngababuleweyo bakhe; ezindulini zakho, nasemifuleni yakho,
nasezihlanjeni zakho zonke, ababuleweyo ngekrele bawe kuzo.

<span id="an_35:9">35:9</span> Ndiya kukwenza kube senkangala kuwe
ngonaphakade, imizi yakho ingemiwa mntu; nazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_35:10">35:10</span> Ngenxa enokuba usithi, Iintlanga ezi
zombini namazwe la omabini ngawam, sowahlutha; ukanti uYehova ukhona;

<span id="an_35:11">35:11</span> ngako oko ndihleli nje, itsho iNkosi
uYehova, ndiya kwenza kuwe ngokomsindo wakho, nangokobukhwele bakho,
obenzileyo kubo ngentiyo yakho; ndizazise kubo, xenikweni ndithe
ndakugweba.

<span id="an_35:12">35:12</span> Uya kwazi ukuba mna Yehova ndikuvile
konke ukugiba kwakho, owakuthethayo ngeentaba zakwaSirayeli, usithi,
Kusenkangala kuzo, sizinikiwe ukuba zibe kukudla.

<span id="an_35:13">35:13</span> Nizikhulisele ngam ngemilomo yenu,
nawafumba phezu kwam amazwi enu; ndivile ke mna.

<span id="an_35:14">35:14</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Lakuvuya
ihlabathi lonke, ndokwenza kube senkangala kuwe.

<span id="an_35:15">35:15</span> Njengoko walivuyelayo ilifa lendlu
kaSirayeli, ngenxa yokuba bekusenkangala kulo, ndiya kwenjenjalo kuwe;
kuya kuba senkangala kuwe, ntaba yakwaSehire, nelakwaEdom lonke liphela;
bazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_36:1">36:1</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, profeta ngazo
iintaba zakwaSirayeli, uthi, Zintaba zakwaSirayeli, liveni ilizwi
likaYehova!

<span id="an_36:2">36:2</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ngenxa
enokuba utshaba lusithi ngani, Tshotsho, imimango engunaphakade
ibililifa lethu!

<span id="an_36:3">36:3</span> ngako oko profeta uthi, Itsho iNkosi
uYehova ukuthi, Ngenxa enokuba, ewe, ngenxa enokuba benenze kwaba
senkangala, baniginya ngeenxa zonke, ukuze nibe lilifa lamasalela
eentlanga, naba semilonyeni yabanolwimi nasentlebendwaneni yabantu:

<span id="an_36:4">36:4</span> ngako oko, nina zintaba zakwaSirayeli,
liveni ilizwi leNkosi uYehova, lisithi, Itsho iNkosi uYehova kwiintaba
nakwiinduli, kwizihlambo nakwimifula, kwiindawo ezibharhileyo
ezingamanxuwa nakwimizi eshiyiweyo, eyaba lixhoba nesigculelo samasalela
eentlanga ezingeenxa zonke;

<span id="an_36:5">36:5</span> ngako oko, itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Inyaniso, ndithethe ngomlilo wobukhwele bam ngawo amasalela eentlanga,
nangamaEdom onke ephela, alenze ilifa lawo ilizwe lam, evuyile
ngentliziyo yonke, ecukuceza ngomphefumlo, ukuze alilahle libe lixhoba.

<span id="an_36:6">36:6</span> Ngako oko, profeta ngomhlaba
wakwaSirayeli, uthi kwiintaba nakwiinduli, kwizihlambo nakwimifula,
Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Yabonani, ndithethe ndinobukhwele,
ndinobushushu, ngenxa enokuba nilithwele ihlazo leentlanga.

<span id="an_36:7">36:7</span> Ngako oko, itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Mna ndisiphakamisile isandla sam; inyaniso, iintlanga ezingeenxa zonke
kuni, zona ziya kuthwala ihlazo lazo.

<span id="an_36:8">36:8</span> Ke nina, zintaba zakwaSirayeli, niya
kuvelisa amasebe, iziqhamo zenu nizixakathele abantu bam amaSirayeli;
ngokuba sekukufuphi ukuvela kwazo.

<span id="an_36:9">36:9</span> Ngokuba, niyabona, ndingakuni; ndobuyela
kuni, nilinywe, nihlwayelwe.

<span id="an_36:10">36:10</span> Ndiya kwandisela abantu phezu kwenu,
yonke indlu kaSirayeli, yonke iphela, imiwe imizi, akhiwe amanxuwa.

<span id="an_36:11">36:11</span> Ndiya kwandisela abantu ke neenkomo
phezu kwenu, bande, baqhame; ndinenze nimiwe ngokwangaphambili ke,
ndinenzele okulungileyo ngaphezu kokwasekuqaleni kwenu; nazi ukuba
ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_36:12">36:12</span> Ndohambisa abantu phezu kwenu, abantu
bam amaSirayeli, bakuzuze ube lilifa labo, ungasabuyi ubahluthe
abantwana.

<span id="an_36:13">36:13</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ngenxa
enokuba bathi kuwe, Usisidlabantu, uluhluthe abantwana uhlanga lwakho:

<span id="an_36:14">36:14</span> ngako oko akuyi kubuya ube
sisidlabantu, ungabuyi ulukhubekise uhlanga lwakho; itsho iNkosi
uYehova.

<span id="an_36:15">36:15</span> Andiyi kubuya ndikuvise ihlazo
leentlanga, ungabuyi usithwale isingcikivo sezizwe, ungabuyi
ulukhubekise uhlanga lwakho; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_36:16">36:16</span> Kwafika ke ilizwi likaYehova kum,
lisithi,

<span id="an_36:17">36:17</span> Nyana womntu, xa indlu kaSirayeli yabe
ihleli emhlabeni wayo, bawenza inqambi ngeendlela zabo nangeentlondi
zabo; iindlela zabo phambi kwam zaba njengobunqambi bomfazi onomzi.

<span id="an_36:18">36:18</span> Ndaphalaza ubushushu bam phezu kwabo
ngenxa yegazi, ababeliphalaze ezweni elo, nangenxa yokulenza inqambi
kwabo ngezigodo zabo.

<span id="an_36:19">36:19</span> Ndabenza baba lusali ezintlangeni,
bachithwachithwa emazweni; ndabagweba ngokweendlela zabo,
nangokweentlondi zabo.

<span id="an_36:20">36:20</span> Bafika ezintlangeni ezo babesiya kuzo,
balihlambela igama lam elingcwele; ekubeni bekusithiwa ngabo, Ngabantu
bakaYehova aba, baphume ezweni lakhe.

<span id="an_36:21">36:21</span> Ndaba nofefe ngenxa yegama lam
elingcwele, ebeyilihlambele indlu kaSirayeli ezintlangeni abaya kuzo.

<span id="an_36:22">36:22</span> Ngako oko yithi kwindlu kaSirayeli,
Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Andenzi ngenxa yenu, ndlu kaSirayeli;
ndenza ngenxa yegama lam elingcwele, enilihlambeleyo ezintlangeni ebe
niye kuzo.

<span id="an_36:23">36:23</span> Ndiya kulingcwalisa igama lam elikhulu,
elihlanjelweyo ezintlangeni, enilihlambeleyo phakathi kwazo; ukuze zazi
iintlanga ukuba ndinguYehova, itsho iNkosi uYehova, ndakuzingcwalisa
ngokwam kuni emehlweni azo.

<span id="an_36:24">36:24</span> Ndonithabatha ke ezintlangeni,
ndinibuthe emazweni onke, ndinise emhlabeni wenu.

<span id="an_36:25">36:25</span> Ndiya kunitshiza ngamanzi amhlophe,
nihlambuluke; ndinihlambulule kubunqambi benu bonke, nakwizigodo zenu
zonke.

<span id="an_36:26">36:26</span> Ndoninika intliziyo entsha, ndininike
umoya omtsha ngaphakathi kwenu; ndiyisuse intliziyo elilitye enyameni
yenu, ndininike intliziyo eyinyama.

<span id="an_36:27">36:27</span> Ndofaka uMoya wam ngaphakathi kwenu,
ndinenze nihambe ngemimiselo yam, niwagcine amasiko am, niwenze;

<span id="an_36:28">36:28</span> niya kuhlala ezweni endalinika ooyihlo;
nibe ngabantu bam, mna ndibe nguThixo wenu.

<span id="an_36:29">36:29</span> Ndiya kunisindisa ebunqambini benu
bonke, ndibize ingqolowa, ndiyandise, ndinganiziseli indlala.

<span id="an_36:30">36:30</span> Ndosandisa isiqhamo somthi nokuphuma
emasimini, ukuze ningabuyi namkeliswe isingcikivo sendlala ezintlangeni.
