<span id="an_36:31">36:31</span> Niya kuzikhumbula ke iindlela zenu
ezimbi, neentlondi zenu ezingalungileyo, nizikruqukele ngokwenu, ngenxa
yobugwenxa benu nangenxa yamasikizi enu.

<span id="an_36:32">36:32</span> Andiyi kukwenza oku ngenxa yenu, itsho
iNkosi uYehova; makwazeke oko kuni. Danani, nibe nehlazo ngenxa
yeendlela zenu, ndlu kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_36:33">36:33</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ngemini
endiya kunihlambulula ngayo ebugwenxeni benu bonke, ndiya kuyenza imizi
ukuba imiwe, akhiwe amanxuwa.

<span id="an_36:34">36:34</span> Ilizwe ebe kusenkangala kulo liya
kulinywa, endaweni yokuba bekusenkangala kulo emehlweni abo bonke
abadlulayo.

<span id="an_36:35">36:35</span> Baya kuthi, Eli lizwe, bekusenkangala
kulo, lisuke laba njengomyezo wase-Eden; nemizi ebeyibharhile,
ebingamanxuwa, ebigungxulwe, imiwe, inqatyisiwe.

<span id="an_36:36">36:36</span> Ziya kwazi ke iintlanga eziseleyo
ngeenxa zonke kuni, ukuba mna Yehova ndakha into egungxulweyo,
ndiyityale indawo ebe kusenkangala kuyo. Mna Yehova ndithethile, ndiya
kwenza.

<span id="an_36:37">36:37</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ngale nto
ndisaya kuquqelwa yindlu kaSirayeli, ukuba ndibenzele; ndiya kubandisa
babe sisintu njengomhlambi;

<span id="an_36:38">36:38</span> njengomhlambi ongamadini angcwele,
njengomhlambi waseYerusalem ngamaxesha ayo amisiweyo; ukuzala yimihlambi
yabantu, iya kuba njalo imizi engamanxuwa; bazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_37:1">37:1</span> Saba phezu kwam isandla sikaYehova;
waphuma nam uYehova, ndikuMoya, wandibeka entilini phakathi; yona ke
izele ngamathambo.

<span id="an_37:2">37:2</span> Wandidlulisa kuwo, wandijikelezisa
ngeenxa zonke; yabona, ebemaninzi kakhulu entilini leyo; yabona,
ebeselomile kakhulu.

<span id="an_37:3">37:3</span> Wathi ke kum, Nyana womntu, aya kuphila
na ke la mathambo? Ndathi, Nkosi Yehova, kwazi wena.

<span id="an_37:4">37:4</span> Wathi kum, Profeta phezu kwala mathambo,
uthi kuwo, Mathambondini, liveni ilizwi likaYehova.

<span id="an_37:5">37:5</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova kula mathambo,
ukuthi, Niyabona, ndingenisa umoya kuni; niya kuphila ke.

<span id="an_37:6">37:6</span> Ndiya kunifaka imisipha, ndimilise kuni
inyama, ndinaleke ngolusu, ndifake umoya ngaphakathi kwenu, niphile;
nazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_37:7">37:7</span> Ndaprofeta ngoko bendiwiselwe umthetho
ngako; kwabakho isandi ndakuprofeta; nanko kurhashaza, asondelelana
amathambo, ithambo lasondela kwithambo lalo.

<span id="an_37:8">37:8</span> Ndakhangela, nanko kukho imisipha kuwo,
yamila inyama, kwaleka ulusu luthabathela phezulu; umoya ke awabakho.

<span id="an_37:9">37:9</span> Wathi kum, Profeta kuwo umoya, profeta,
nyana womntu, uthi kuwo umoya, Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Vela, moya
kwimimoya yomine, uphefumlele kwaba babuleweyo, baphile.

<span id="an_37:10">37:10</span> Ndaprofeta ke ngoko bendiwiselwe
umthetho ngako. Wangena umoya kuwo; baphila, bema ngeenyawo, umkhosi
omkhulu kakhulu kunene.

<span id="an_37:11">37:11</span> Wathi ke kum, Nyana womntu, la mathambo
yindlu kaSirayeli yonke; yabona, bathi, Amathambo ethu omile, nethemba
lethu lidakile, sinqanyulwe.

<span id="an_37:12">37:12</span> Ngako oko profeta, uthi kubo, Itsho
iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Yabonani, ndiya kuwavula amangcwaba enu,
ndininyuse niphume emangcwabeni enu, bantu bam, ndinise emhlabeni
wakwaSirayeli.

<span id="an_37:13">37:13</span> Niya kwazi ukuba ndinguYehova,
ekuwavuleni kwam amangcwaba enu, nasekuninyuseni kwam, niphume
emangcwabeni enu, bantu bam.

<span id="an_37:14">37:14</span> Ndofaka uMoya wam kuni, niphile,
ndinibeke emhlabeni wenu; nazi ukuba mna Yehova ndithethile, ndiya
kwenza; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_37:15">37:15</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_37:16">37:16</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, thabathela kuwe
intonga ibe nye, ubhale kuyo uthi, EkaYuda, neyoonyana bakaSirayeli,
amadlelane akhe; uthabathe enye intonga ubhale kuyo uthi, EkaYosefu
(intonga kaEfrayim), nendlu yonke kaSirayeli, amadlelane akhe;

<span id="an_37:17">37:17</span> uzisondeze ke, enye kwenye, zibe
ntonga-nye, zibe nto-nye esandleni sakho.

<span id="an_37:18">37:18</span> Bothi bakuthetha nawe oonyana babantu
bakowenu, besithi, Akasixeleli na, ziyintoni na ezi ntonga kuwe?

<span id="an_37:19">37:19</span> uthi wena kubo, Itsho iNkosi uYehova
ukuthi, Yabonani, ndiya kuyithabatha intonga kaYosefu, esesandleni
sikaEfrayim nezizwe zikaSirayeli, amadlelane akhe endiwabeke kuyo
ndawonye nentonga kaYuda, ndibenze babe ntonga-nye, babe nto-nye
esandleni sam.

<span id="an_37:20">37:20</span> Iintonga obhale kuzo zize zibe
sesandleni sakho emehlweni abo.

<span id="an_37:21">37:21</span> Uze uthi kubo, Itsho iNkosi uYehova
ukuthi, Yabonani, ndiya kubathabatha oonyana bakaSirayeli phakathi
kweentlanga abahamba kuzo, ndibabuthe, bavele ngeenxa zonke, ndibase
emhlabeni wabo.

<span id="an_37:22">37:22</span> Ndobenza luhlanga lunye elizweni elo,
ezintabeni zakwaSirayeli, abe mnye ukumkani, engukumkani wabo bonke
bephela; bangabuyi babe ziintlanga ezimbini, bangabuyi bahluke babe
zizikumkani ezibini.

<span id="an_37:23">37:23</span> Abayi kubuya bazenze iinqambi ngezigodo
zabo, nangezinto zabo ezinezothe, nangezikreqo zabo zonke; ke
ndobasindisa emakhayeni abo onke, ababesona kuwo, ndibahlambulule, babe
ngabantu bam, ndibe nguThixo wabo.

<span id="an_37:24">37:24</span> Umkhonzi wam uDavide woba ngukumkani
kubo, abe ngumalusi omnye kubo bonke bephela; bahambe ngamasiko am,
bagcine imimiselo yam, bayenze.

<span id="an_37:25">37:25</span> Bohlala ezweni elo, ndalinika umkhonzi
wam uYakobi, ababehleli kulo ooyise; bahlale ke khona, bona nabantwana
babantwana babo kude kuse ephakadeni; uDavide, umkhonzi wam, abe
sisikhulu sabo ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_37:26">37:26</span> Ndobenzela umnqophiso woxolo; uya kuba
ngumnqophiso ongunaphakade kubo; ndibamise, ndibandise, ndibeke ingcwele
yam phakathi kwabo ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_37:27">37:27</span> Umnquba wam uya kuba phezu kwabo, ndibe
nguThixo wabo, babe ngabantu bam:

<span id="an_37:28">37:28</span> zazi iintlanga ukuba ndinguYehova
ongcwalise amaSirayeli, xa ingcwele yam iya kubakho phakathi kwabo
ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_38:1">38:1</span> Ke kaloku, kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum,
lisithi,

<span id="an_38:2">38:2</span> Nyana womntu, bubhekise ubuso bakho
kuGogi wasezweni lakwaMagogi, isikhulu sakwaRoshe noMesheki noTubhali,
uprofete ngaye.

<span id="an_38:3">38:3</span> Yithi, Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Yabona, ndikuchasile, Gogi, sikhulu sakwaRoshe noMesheki noTubhali.

<span id="an_38:4">38:4</span> Ndiya kukuphambanisa, ndikufake
amakhonkco emihlathini, ndikurhole nempi yakho yonke, amahashe
nabamahashe, abaxhobe baphelelisela bonke bephela, ibandla elikhulu,
benamakhaka neengweletshetshe, bephethe amakrele bonke bephela:

<span id="an_38:5">38:5</span> benamaPersi namaKushi namaPuti, onke
ephela eneengweletshetshe nezigcina-ntloko;

<span id="an_38:6">38:6</span> uGomere namahlelo akhe onke, nendlu
kaTogarma ezingontsini zasentla, inamahlelo akhe onke; izizwe ezininzi
zinawe.

<span id="an_38:7">38:7</span> Lunga, uzilungisele iinto zonke, wena
nebandla lakho lonke, elibizelwe ndawonye kuwe, ube ngumgcini walo.

<span id="an_38:8">38:8</span> Emva kwemihla emininzi uya kuvelelwa;
ekupheleni kweminyaka leyo uya kufika elizweni elibuyisiweyo ekreleni,
libuthiwe ezizweni ezininzi; ufike ezintabeni zakwaSirayeli ezahlala
zibharhile. Lona likhutshwe ezizweni, baza bahlala bekholosile bonke
bephela.

<span id="an_38:9">38:9</span> Uya kunyuka uze njengesiphango,
njengelifu ukulisibekela ilizwe, wena namahlelo akho onke, nezizwe
ezininzi ezinawe.

<span id="an_38:10">38:10</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ngaloo
mini, kuya kuthi qatha izinto entliziyweni yakho, ucinge ingcinga embi.

<span id="an_38:11">38:11</span> Uya kuthi, Ndiya kunyuka ndiye ezweni
lamaphandle; ndiya kubafikela abazolileyo, abahleli bekholosile bonke
bephela, abahleli bengenazindonga, bengenamivalo nazingcango;

<span id="an_38:12">38:12</span> ukuba uthimbe, uhlasele amaxhoba,
usibuyisele isandla sakho kumanxuwa amiweyo, nakubantu abahlanganisiweyo
ezintlangeni, bezuze imfuyo nempahla, abahleli esazulwini somhlaba.

<span id="an_38:13">38:13</span> OoShebha noDedan, nabarhwebi
baseTarshishe, neengonyama ezintsha zabo zonke, baya kuthi kuwe, Uze
kuthimba na, ukuba lihlasele amaxhoba na ibandla lakho olibizele
ndawonye? ukuba limke negolide nesilivere, lithabathe imfuyo nempahla,
lithimbe kakhulu na?

<span id="an_38:14">38:14</span> Ngako oko profeta, nyana womntu, uthi
kuGogi, Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Akuyi kuba njalo na ngaloo mini,
ekuhlaleni kwabantu bam amaSirayeli bekholosile, uya kuyazi loo nto?

<span id="an_38:15">38:15</span> Uya kuphuma endaweni yakho,
ezingontsini zasentla, wena nezizwe ezininzi ezinawe, bekhwele
emahasheni bonke bephela, ibandla elikhulu, impi eninzi;

<span id="an_38:16">38:16</span> unyuke ubafikele bantu bam amaSirayeli
njengelifu, ukuba ulisibekele ilizwe. Ekupheleni kwemihla kuya kubakho
oko, ndikuse, ulifikele ilizwe lam, ukuze iintlanga zindazi,
ekuzingcwaliseni kwam kuwe emehlweni azo, Gogi.

<span id="an_38:17">38:17</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Nguwe na
lowa, ndandithetha yena ngeemini zamandulo ngomlomo wabakhonzi bam,
abaprofeti bakwaSirayeli, ababeprofeta iminyaka kwezo mini ngelithi,
ndokuzisa phezu kwabo?

<span id="an_38:18">38:18</span> Kuya kuthi ngaloo mini, ngemini
yokuwufikela kukaGogi umhlaba wakwaSirayeli, itsho iNkosi uYehova,
bunyuke ubushushu bam emathatheni am.

<span id="an_38:19">38:19</span> Ke ndithethe ndinobukhwele, ndinomlilo
wokuphuphuma komsindo wam. Inyaniso, ngaloo mini kuya kubakho ukunyikima
okukhulu emhlabeni wakwaSirayeli.

<span id="an_38:20">38:20</span> Ziya kunyikima phambi kwam iintlanzi
zolwandle, neentaka zezulu, namarhamncwa asendle, nezinambuzane zonke
ezinambuzelayo emhlabeni, nabantu bonke abasebusweni bomhlaba,
zigungxulwe iintaba, iwe imixawuka, zonke iindonga ziwe emhlabeni.

<span id="an_38:21">38:21</span> Ndombizela ikrele ezintabeni zam zonke,
itsho iNkosi uYehova; ikrele lomntu liya kuma kumzalwana wakhe.

<span id="an_38:22">38:22</span> Ndiya kumgweba ngendyikitya yokufa
nangegazi; nangesiphango esikhukulayo, nangamatye esichotho, umlilo
nesulfure ndiwunise phezu kwakhe, naphezu kwamahlelo akhe, naphezu
kwezizwe ezininzi ezinaye.

<span id="an_38:23">38:23</span> Ndiya kuzikhulisa, ndizingcwalise,
ndizazise ngokwam emehlweni eentlanga ezininzi; zazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_39:1">39:1</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, profeta ngoGogi,
uthi, Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Yabona, ndikuchasile, Gogi, sikhulu
sakwaRoshe noMesheki noTubhali.

<span id="an_39:2">39:2</span> Ndiya kukuphambanisa, ndikurhole,
ndikunyuse uphume ezingontsini zasentla, ndikuse ezintabeni
zakwaSirayeli.

<span id="an_39:3">39:3</span> Ndosithi qhwithi isaphetha sakho
esandleni sakho sokhohlo, ndiziwise iintolo zakho esandleni sakho
sokunene.

<span id="an_39:4">39:4</span> Uya kuwa ezintabeni zakwaSirayeli, wena
namahlelo akho onke, nezizwe ezinawe. Ndiya kukunikela ezintakeni
ezixwilayo zeentlobo ngeentlobo, nasemarhamncweni asendle, ukuba ube
kukudla.

<span id="an_39:5">39:5</span> Uya kuwa ebusweni belizwe, ngokuba
ndithethile; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_39:6">39:6</span> Nothumela umlilo kwaMagogi, nakubemi
beziqithi abakholosileyo; bazi ukuba ndinguYehova.

<span id="an_39:7">39:7</span> Ndiya kulazisa igama lam elingcwele
phakathi kwabantu bam amaSirayeli, ndingabuyi ndilingcolise igama lam
elingcwele; zazi iintlanga ukuba ndinguYehova, oyiNgcwele kwaSirayeli.

<span id="an_39:8">39:8</span> Yabona, le nto iyeza, iya kubakho; itsho
iNkosi uYehova; yiloo mini ndandithetha yona.

<span id="an_39:9">39:9</span> Ke baya kuphuma abemi bemizi
yakwaSirayeli, baphembe babase umlilo ngezikrweqe, nangeengweletshetshe,
nangamakhaka, ngezaphetha, nangeentolo, nangeenduku, nangezikhali;
baphembe umlilo ngazo iminyaka esixhenxe.

<span id="an_39:10">39:10</span> Abayi kutheza ziinkuni endle,
bangagawuli nasemahlathini; ngokuba baya kuwuphemba ngezikrweqe umlilo;
bathimbe kwabo babethinjwe ngabo, baphange ababephangwe ngabo; itsho
iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_39:11">39:11</span> Kuya kuthi ngaloo mini, ndimnike uGogi
indawo, apho liya kuba khona ingcwaba lakhe kwaSirayeli, umfula
wabadluli ngasempumalanga elwandle; ubavalele abadluli; bamngcwabele
khona uGogi nengxokolo yakhe yonke, bathi ngumfula wengxokolo kaGogi.

<span id="an_39:12">39:12</span> Indlu kaSirayeli yoba neenyanga
ezisixhenxe ibangcwaba, ukuze balihlambulule ilizwe;

<span id="an_39:13">39:13</span> bonke abantu belizwe eli bangcwabe,
kube ludumo kubo mini ndizizukisayo; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_39:14">39:14</span> Baya kubalula amadoda anomonde
acandacanda elizweni, nahamba nalawo acandacandayo, angcwabe abaseleyo
ebusweni belizwe, ukuba alihlambulule. Ekupheleni kweenyanga ezisixhenxe
aya kuligocagoca.

<span id="an_39:15">39:15</span> Baya kucanda abacandacanda elizweni,
babone ithambo lomntu, bamise umthelekelelo ecaleni kwalo, bade
abangcwabi abo balingcwabe emfuleni wengxokolo kaGogi.

<span id="an_39:16">39:16</span> Igama lomzi okhona liya kuba
nguNgxokolo; balihlambulule ke ilizwe.

<span id="an_39:17">39:17</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, itsho iNkosi
uYehova ukuthi, Yithi, kwiintaka zeentlobo ngeentlobo, nakumarhamncwa
onke asendle, Buthanani nize; zihlanganiseni ngeenxa zonke
embingelelweni wam endinibingeleleyo, umbingelelo omkhulu ezintabeni
zakwaSirayeli; nidle inyama, nisele igazi.

<span id="an_39:18">39:18</span> Niya kudla inyama yamagorha, nisele
igazi lezikhulu zehlabathi, iinkunzi zeegusha, namatakane, neenkunzi
zeebhokhwe, neenkunzi zeenkomo ezintsha ezityetyisiweyo zaseBhashan,
zonke ziphela.

<span id="an_39:19">39:19</span> Nodla amanqatha nihluthe, nisele igazi
ninxile embingelelweni wam endinibingeleleyo;

<span id="an_39:20">39:20</span> nihluthe esithebeni sam ngamahashe
nangabamahashe, ngamagorha namadoda onke okulwa; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_39:21">39:21</span> Ndiya kubumisa ubuqaqawuli bam
ezintlangeni, ziwubone iintlanga zonke umgwebo wam endiya kuwenza,
nesandla sam endiya kusisa kuzo.

<span id="an_39:22">39:22</span> Iya kwazi indlu kaSirayeli ukuba
ndinguYehova uThixo wabo, ithabathela kuyo le mini ise naphi.

<span id="an_39:23">39:23</span> Neentlanga ziya kwazi ukuba indlu
kaSirayeli yathinjwa ngenxa yobugwenxa babo; ngenxa enokuba bamenezayo
kum, ndabusithelisa ubuso bam kubo, ndabanikela esandleni sababandezeli
babo, bawa likrele bonke bephela.

<span id="an_39:24">39:24</span> Ndabenza ngokobunqambi babo
nangokwezikreqo zabo, ndabusithelisa ubuso bam kubo.

<span id="an_39:25">39:25</span> Ngako oko, itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Kaloku ndiya kukubuyisa ukuthinjwa kukaYakobi, ndisikwe yimfesane ngenxa
yendlu yonke kaSirayeli, ndibe nobukhwele ngegama lam elingcwele.

<span id="an_39:26">39:26</span> Baya kulithwala ihlazo labo,
nobumenemene babo bonke ababemeneza ngabo kum, ekuhlaleni kwabo
emhlabeni wabo bekholosile, kungekho ubothusayo.

<span id="an_39:27">39:27</span> Ekubabuyiseni kwam ezizweni,
ekubabutheni kwam emazweni eentshaba zabo, ndozingcwalisa kubo emehlweni
eentlanga ezininzi.

<span id="an_39:28">39:28</span> Baya kwazi ukuba ndinguYehova uThixo
wabo, owenza ukuba bathinjelwe ezintlangeni, ndize ndibawomelisele
emhlabeni wabo, ndingabuyi ndishiye namnye kubo khona.

<span id="an_39:29">39:29</span> Andiyi kuba sabusithelisa ubuso bam
kubo, ngokokuba ndithulule uMoya wam phezu kwendlu kaSirayeli; itsho
iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_40:1">40:1</span> Ngomnyaka wamashumi omabini anamihlanu
wokuthinjwa kwethu, ekuqalekeni komnyaka, ngolweshumi enyangeni leyo,
ngomnyaka weshumi elinesine emva kokuxatyelwa komzi, ngayo kanye loo
mini, isandla sikaYehova saba phezu kwam, wandisa khona.

<span id="an_40:2">40:2</span> Ngemibono kaThixo wandisa ezweni
lakwaSirayeli elo, wandibeka entabeni ephakamileyo kakhulu; phezu kwayo
kwanga sisakhiwo somzi ngasezantsi.

<span id="an_40:3">40:3</span> Wandisa khona: nanko umntu, okubonakala
kunjengokubonakala kobhedu, ephethe intsontelo yeflakisi ngesandla,
nengcongolo yokulinganisa; waye ke emi esangweni.

<span id="an_40:4">40:4</span> Wathetha nam loo mntu, wathi, Nyana
womntu, khangela ngamehlo akho, uve ngeendlebe zakho, ugqale ngentliziyo
yakho zonke izinto endikubonisa zona; ngokuba uziswe apha ukuze
uboniswe. Xelela indlu kaSirayeli konke okubonayo.

<span id="an_40:5">40:5</span> Nanko ke, kukho udonga ngaphandle
kwendlu, olujikelezileyo ngeenxa zonke, isesandleni somntu lowo
ingcongolo yokulinganisa, iziikubhite ezintandathu, iyileyo iyikubhite
enobubanzi besandla. Wabulinganisa ububanzi besakhiwo; baba yingcongolo
enye, ukuphakama kwayingcongolo enye.

<span id="an_40:6">40:6</span> Waya esangweni elibheke empumalanga,
wenyuka ngezinyuko zalo, walinganisa omnye umbundu wesango; waba
yingcongolo enye ububanzi, omnye umbundu ke wokuqala wayingcongolo enye
ububanzi.

<span id="an_40:7">40:7</span> Negumbi lokulinda laba yingcongolo enye
ubude, layingcongolo enye ububanzi; phakathi kwamagumbi okulinda
zaziikubhite ezintlanu; umbundu wesango, ongasevarandeni yesango
enganeno kwayo indlu, wayingcongolo enye.

<span id="an_40:8">40:8</span> Walinganisa ivaranda yesango leyo
inganeno kwayo indlu, yayingcongolo enye.

<span id="an_40:9">40:9</span> Walinganisa ivaranda yesango ke,
yaziikubhite ezisibhozo, iintsika zayo zaziikubhite ezimbini; ke
ivaranda yesango yayinganeno kwayo indlu.

<span id="an_40:10">40:10</span> Ke amagumbi okulinda, esango elisingise
empumalanga, aba mathathu ngapha, aba mathathu nangapha, aba mlinganiso
mnye omathathu, zaba mlinganiso mnye iintsika ngapha nangapha.

<span id="an_40:11">40:11</span> Walinganisa ububanzi bokungena
kwesango, baziikubhite ezilishumi; ubude besango ngalinye baziikubhite
ezilishumi elinazithathu.

<span id="an_40:12">40:12</span> Ke umda phambi kwamagumbi okulinda
wawuyikubhite enye ngapha, wayikubhite enye nangapha umda; amagumbi
okulinda aba ziikubhite ezintandathu ngapha, aba ziikubhite ezintandathu
nangapha.

<span id="an_40:13">40:13</span> Walinganisa isango, ethabathela
eluphahleni lwamagumbi okulinda, esa eluphahleni lwamanye; laba
ziikubhite ezimashumi mabini anantlanu ububanzi; umnyango ulunge
nomnyango.

<span id="an_40:14">40:14</span> Iintsika wazenza zangamashumi
omathandathu eekubhite; yeza kuma ngentsika intendelezo ejikelezileyo
ngeenxa zonke esangweni.

<span id="an_40:15">40:15</span> Ke ukuthabathela phambi kwesango
lokungena, kuse phambi kwevaranda yesango eliphakathi, zabaziikubhite
ezimashumi mahlanu.

<span id="an_40:16">40:16</span> Bekukho iifestile ezi valiweyo
emagumbini okulinda nasezintsikeni zawo ngecala eliphakathi esangweni,
zijikelezile ngeenxa zonke; bekukwanjalo nasezingqamekweni. Bekukho
iifestile ngaphakathi, zijikelezile ngeenxa zonke; bekukho namasundu
ezintsikeni.

<span id="an_40:17">40:17</span> Wandisa entendelezweni ephandle; nanko,
kwenziwe amagumbi nombekelelo wamatye, kwajikeleza ngeenxa zonke
entendelezweni; yayingamagumbi angamashumi mathathu embekelelweni
wamatye.

<span id="an_40:18">40:18</span> Umbekelelo wamatye ubusemacaleni
amasango, ulungelelene nobude bamasango; umbekelelo lowo uphantsi.

<span id="an_40:19">40:19</span> Walinganisa ububanzi, ethabathela
phambi kwesango lentendelezo ephantsi, esa phambi kwelentendelezo
ephakathi nganeno kwalo; zalikhulu leekubhite ngasempumalanga
nangasentla.

<span id="an_40:20">40:20</span> Isango elibheke entla
ngasentendelezweni ephandle, wabulinganisa ubude balo nobubanzi balo;

<span id="an_40:21">40:21</span> namagumbi okulinda amathathu ngapha,
amathathu nangapha, neentsika zalo, neengqameko zalo. Laba
ngangomlinganiso wesango lokuqala; baziikubhite ezimashumi mahlanu ubude
balo, nobubanzi balo baziikubhite ezimashumi mabini anantlanu.

<span id="an_40:22">40:22</span> Iifestile zalo, neengqameko zalo,
namasundu alo, zaba ngangomlinganiso wesango elibheke empumalanga;
benyuka ngezinyuko ezisixhenxe ukuya kulo; neengqameko zalo zaba phambi
kwazo.

<span id="an_40:23">40:23</span> Amasango entendelezo ephakathi alunga
nesango langasentla nelangasempumalanga; walinganisa, wathabathela
esangweni, wesa esangweni; zalikhulu leekubhite.

<span id="an_40:24">40:24</span> Wandihambisa wandisingisa ezantsi; nali
isango, lisingise ezantsi; walinganisa iintsika zalo neengqameko zalo
kwangokwaloo milinganiso.

<span id="an_40:25">40:25</span> Bekukho iifestile kulo nakwiingqameko
zalo, zijikelezile ngeenxa zonke, njengeziya iifestile; zaba ziikubhite
ezimashumi mahlanu ubude, baziikubhite ezimashumi mabini anantlanu
ububanzi.

<span id="an_40:26">40:26</span> Ukunyuka ukuya kulo kwaba nezinyuko
ezisixhenxe, nezingqameko zalo zaziphambi kwazo; belinamasundu, elinye
lingapha, elinye lingapha, ezintsikeni zalo.

<span id="an_40:27">40:27</span> Bekukho isango elisa entendelezweni
ephakathi, elisingise ezantsi; walinganisa ethabathela esangweni elo,
esa esangweni elisingise ezantsi; zaba ziikubhite ezilikhulu.

<span id="an_40:28">40:28</span> Wandisa entendelezweni ephakathi
ngesango lasezantsi, walilinganisa isango lasezantsi kwangokwaloo
milinganiso;

<span id="an_40:29">40:29</span> namagumbi alo okulinda, neentsika zalo,
neengqameko zalo, kwangokwaloo milinganiso. Bekukho iifestile kulo
nakwiingqameko zalo, zijikelezile ngeenxa zonke; zaba ziikubhite
ezimashumi mahlanu ubude, zaba ziikubhite ezimashumi mabini anantlanu
ububanzi.

<span id="an_40:30">40:30</span> Iingqameko zajikeleza ngeenxa zonke:
zaba ziikubhite ezimashumi mabini anantlanu ubude, zaba ziikubhite
ezintlanu ububanzi.

<span id="an_40:31">40:31</span> Iingqameko zalo zabheka entendeezweni
ephandle; zibe zinamasundu iintsika zalo. Ukunyuka ukuya kulo kwaba
nezinyuko ezisibhozo.

<span id="an_40:32">40:32</span> Wandisa entendelezweni ephakathi,
esingise empumalanga, walilinganisa isango kwangokwaloo milinganiso;

<span id="an_40:33">40:33</span> namagumbi alo okulinda, neentsika zalo,
neengqameko zalo, kwangokwaloo milinganiso. Bekukho iifestile kulo,
nakwiingqameko zalo, zijikelezile ngeenxa zonke; aba ziikubhite
ezimashumi mahlanu ubude, zaba ziikubhite ezimashumi mabini anantlanu
ububanzi.

<span id="an_40:34">40:34</span> Iingqameko zalo zabheka entendelezweni
ephandle; zibe zinamasundu iintsika ngapha nangapha. Ukunyuka ukuya kulo
kwaba nezinyuko ezisibhozo.

<span id="an_40:35">40:35</span> Wandisa esangweni lasentla,
walilinganisa kwangokwaloo milinganiso;

<span id="an_40:36">40:36</span> namagumbi alo okulinda, neentsika zalo,
neengqameko zalo. Bekukho iifestile kulo, zijikelezile ngeenxa zonke;
zaba ziikubhite ezimashumi mahlanu ubude, zaba ziikubhite ezimashumi
mabini anantlanu ububanzi.

<span id="an_40:37">40:37</span> Iintsika zalo zakhangela entendelezweni
ephandle; zinamasundu iintsika zalo ngapha nangapha. Ukunyuka ukuya kulo
kwaba nezinyuko ezisibhozo.

<span id="an_40:38">40:38</span> Igumbi nomnyango walo
lalingasezintsikeni zamasango; bebewahlamba khona amadini anyukayo.

<span id="an_40:39">40:39</span> Evarandeni yesango bekukho iitafile
ezimbini ngapha, iitafile ezimbini nangapha, zokuxhelela amadini
anyukayo, nawesono, nawetyala.

<span id="an_40:40">40:40</span> Ecaleni elingaphandle, konyukayo esiya
ekungeneni kwesango ngasentla, bekukho iitafile ezimbini; nakwelinye
icala ngasevarandeni yesango bekukho iitafile ezimbini.

<span id="an_40:41">40:41</span> Kwabakho iitafile ezine ngapha,
iitafile ezine nangapha, ecaleni lesango; ziitafile ezisibhozo,
zokuxhelela kuzo.

<span id="an_40:42">40:42</span> Kananjalo bekukho neetafile ezine
ngasezinyukweni zamatye aqingqiweyo, aba yikubhite enye enesiqingatha
ubude, ikubhite enye enesiqingatha ububanzi, ikubhite enye ukuphakama,
ukuze babeke kuzo iimpahla zokuxhela amadini anyukayo nemibingelelo.

<span id="an_40:43">40:43</span> Amabhaxa angangobubanzi besandla, abe
eqiniselweendlwini, ajikeleza ngeenxa zonke; yaye isezitafileni inyama
yomsondezo.

<span id="an_40:44">40:44</span> Ngaphandle kwesango eliphakathi bekukho
amagumbi amabini entendelezweni ephakathi; elinye lingasecaleni lesango
lasentla, libheke ezantsi, elinye lingasecaleni lesango lasezantsi,
libheke entla.

<span id="an_40:45">40:45</span> Wathi kum, Eli gumbi, libheke ezantsi,
lelababingeleli abagcina isigxina sendlu le.

<span id="an_40:46">40:46</span> Igumbi elibheke entla lelababingeleli
abagcina isigcina sesibingelelo. Bona bangoonyana bakaTsadoki, koonyana
bakaLevi, abasondelayo kuYehova ukuba balungiselele kuye.

<span id="an_40:47">40:47</span> Wayilinganisa intendelezo; zaba
ziikubhite ezilikhulu ubude, zaba ziikubhite ezilikhulu nobubanzi;
imbombo-ne; isibingelelo ke besiphambi kwayo indlu.

<span id="an_40:48">40:48</span> Wandisa evarandeni yayo indlu,
walinganisa intsika yevaranda: iikubhite zontlanu ngapha, iikubhite
zontlanu ngapha; ububanzi besango baziikubhite ezintathu ngapha,
iikubhite ezintathu nangapha.

<span id="an_40:49">40:49</span> Ubude bevaranda baba ziikubhite
ezimashumi mabini, ububanzi baba ziikubhite ezilishumi elinanye
ngasezinyukweni, ebe kunyukwa ngazo kuyiwe kuyo. Bekukho iintsika
ngasezintsikeni zomnyango, enye ngapha, enye nangapha.

<span id="an_41:1">41:1</span> Wandisa etempileni, walinganisa iintsika;
zaba ziikubhite ezintandathu ububanzi ngapha, zaba ziikubhite
ezintandathu ububanzi nangapha; bububanzi ke bentente.

<span id="an_41:2">41:2</span> Ububanzi bomnyango bebuziikubhite
ezilishumi; amacala omnyango aba ziikubhite ezintlanu ngapha, iikubhite
ezintlanu nangapha. Wabulinganisa ubude bayo, baziikubhite ezimashumi
mane, ububanzi baziikubhite ezimashumi mabini.

<span id="an_41:3">41:3</span> Wangena ke ngaphakathi, walinganisa
intsika yomnyango; yaziikubhite ezimbini, nomnyango waziikubhite
ezintandathu ukuphakama, ububanzi bomnyango baziikubhite ezisixhenxe.

<span id="an_41:4">41:4</span> Wabulinganisa ubude bayo, baziikubhite
ezimashumi mabini, ububanzi baziikubhite ezimashumi mabini, wabhekisa
etempileni; wathi kum, Yingcwele kangcwele le.

<span id="an_41:5">41:5</span> Walulinganisa udonga lwendlu,
lwaziikubhite ezintandathu, ububanzi bendawo yokwayama baziikubhite
ezine; yajikeleza ngeenxa zonke endlwini leyo.

<span id="an_41:6">41:6</span> Amagumbi endawo yokwayama aba mathathu,
igumbi phezu kwegumbi, aba mashumi mathathu; aya kufika eludongeni
ebeyinalo indlu le, ngasemagumbini endawo yokwayama, eyajikeleza ngeenxa
zonke, ukuze abe nokubambeka khona; kodwa angabambeki eludongeni lwayo
indlu.

<span id="an_41:7">41:7</span> Kwaya kuba banzi ukujikeleza, okukhona
siya sinyuka isakhiwo ngokwamagumbi endawo yokwayama; ngokuba oko
kwayijikeleza indlu le, kwaya kusanda okukhona inyukayo, kuyijikeleza
indlu le ngeenxa zonke; ngenxa yoko indlu le yaya iba banzi okunyuka
inyukayo; lwaba kwanjalo olungaphantsi udidi, ukunyuka ukuya
kolungaphezulu ngokolo lungaphakathi.

<span id="an_41:8">41:8</span> Ndabona kwasendlwini le indawo
ephakamileyo, ejikelezileyo ngeenxa zonke; iziseko zamagumbi endawo
yokwayama zaziyingcongolo epheleyo, ziikubhite ezintandathu, ukuya
entlanganweni.

<span id="an_41:9">41:9</span> Ububanzi bodonga, ebe inabo indawo
yokwayama ngaphandle, bebuziikubhite ezintlanu; yaba kwanjalo indawo
eshiyekileyo endlwini enamagumbi endawo yokwayama ekule ndlu.

<span id="an_41:10">41:10</span> Phakathi kwamagumbi ibe ibububanzi
beekubhite ezimashumi mabini obujikelezileyo, bayijikeleza indlu ngeenxa
zonke.

<span id="an_41:11">41:11</span> Iminyango yendawo yokwayama
yayikhangele endaweni eshiyekileyo; omnye umnyango ukhangele ngentla,
omnye umnyango ukhangele ngezantsi; ububanzi bendawo eshiyekileyo
bebuziikubhite ezintlanu, bajikeleza ngeenxa zonke.

<span id="an_41:12">41:12</span> Isakhiwo esibe siphambi kwendawo
eqhiwukileyo, sasiziikubhite ezimashumi asixhenxe ububanzi baso ngecala
elisingise entshonalanga; udonga lwesakhiwo eso lwaluziikubhite
ezintlanu ububanzi balo; lwajikeleza ngeenxa zonke, nobude baso baba
ziikubhite ezimashumi asithoba.

<span id="an_41:13">41:13</span> Wayilinganisa ke indlu leyo, yaba
ziikubhite ezilikhulu ubude; indawo eqhiwukileyo, nesakhiwo sayo,
neendonga zaso, zaba ziikubhite ezilikhulu ubude.

<span id="an_41:14">41:14</span> Ububanzi bobuso bayo indlu, nobendawo
eqhiwukileyo ekhangele empumalanga baba ziikubhite ezilikhulu.

<span id="an_41:15">41:15</span> Wabulinganisa ke ubude besakhiwo esibe
siphambi kwendawo eqhiwukileyo, ebe singasemva kwayo, neegalari zaso
ngapha nangapha, iikubhite zaba likhulu; nendawo engcwele yangaphakathi,
neevaranda zentendelezo.

<span id="an_41:16">41:16</span> Imibundu leyo yeminyango, neefestile
ezo zivaliweyo, neegalari ezo zijikelezileyo ezindidini zazo zontathu
(malunga nemibundu yeminyango kukho amaceba emithi, ejikelezile ngeenxa
zonke; nomhlaba ude wema ngeefestile, iifestile ke zigutyungelwe),

<span id="an_41:17">41:17</span> naphezu kweminyango, kwada kwasendlwini
ngaphakathi nangaphandle, naseludongeni lonke, kwajikeleza ngeenxa
zonke, ngaphakathi nangaphandle, kwaba yimilinganiso.

<span id="an_41:18">41:18</span> Kwaye kwenziwe iikerubhi namasundu;
yalisundu phakathi kwekerubhi nekerubhi; ikerubhi yanobuso obubini;

<span id="an_41:19">41:19</span> yabubuso bomntu obubheke esundwini
ngapha, yabubuso bengonyama obubheke esundwini ngapha. Kwaye kwenjiwe
njalo endlwini yonke, kwajikeleza ngeenxa zonke.

<span id="an_41:20">41:20</span> Zenziwa zathabathela emhlabeni zesa
phezu kweminyango, iikerubhi namasundu, eludongeni ke lwetempile.

<span id="an_41:21">41:21</span> Itempile, imigubasi yayo ibe
imbombo-ne; nobuso bengcwele, imbonakalo yabo yabonakala ikwanjalo.

<span id="an_41:22">41:22</span> Isibingelelo sasingumthi,
ukubhite-ntathu ukuphakama, buziikubhite-mbini ubude baso; besineembombo
zaso nommiso waso, namacala aso engumthi. Wathi kum, Le yitafile ephambi
koYehova.

<span id="an_41:23">41:23</span> Bezimbini iingcango zetempile
nezengcwele.

<span id="an_41:24">41:24</span> Bezingambini iingcango kwiminyango
leyo, ziziingcango ezijingayo zombini, zimbini komnye umnyango, zimbini
iingcango nakomnye.

<span id="an_41:25">41:25</span> Kwaye kwenziwe kuzo, kwiingcango ezo
zetempile, iikerubhi namasundu, kunjengoko bekwenziwe ngako ezindongeni.
Kwaye kukho isinyuko somthi phambi kwevaranda ngaphandle.

<span id="an_41:26">41:26</span> Iifestile ezivaliweyo namasundu
zazingapha nangapha, emacaleni evaranda, nasemagumbini endawo yokwayama
kuyo indlu, nezinyuko.

<span id="an_42:1">42:1</span> Waphuma nam, waya entendelezweni
engaphandle ngendlela esinga ngentla, wandisa emagumbini amalunga
nendawo le iqhiwukileyo, amalunga nesakhiwo eso, akhangele entla.

<span id="an_42:2">42:2</span> Phambi kwecala elibude buziikubhite
ezilikhulu, elimnyango ungasentla, ububanzi baba ziikubhite ezimashumi
mahlanu.

<span id="an_42:3">42:3</span> Malunga neekubhite ezimashumi mabini
zentendelezo engaphakathi, malunga nombekelelo wamatye osentendelezweni
engaphandle, yaba yigalari isinge egalarini eludidini lwesithathu.

<span id="an_42:4">42:4</span> Phambi kwamagumbi kwakukho indawo
yokuhamba, ububanzi bayo buziikubhite ezilishumi; kukho indlela
eziikubhite zilikhulu, ebheka phakathi; iminyango yazo ke ibheka
ngentla.

<span id="an_42:5">42:5</span> Ke amagumbi aphezulu ebemafuphi
kunawaphantsi, kunaphakathi esakhiweni; ngokuba iigalari zawadlela.

<span id="an_42:6">42:6</span> Ngokuba ebendidi ntathu wona,
engenazintsika, njengokuba iintendelezo zineentsika: ngenxa yoko
kwarhoxiswa kwala angaphantsi kwanala aphakathi esikhundleni sawo.

<span id="an_42:7">42:7</span> Ke udonga olwalungaphandle, lulungelelene
namagumbi, lwasinga entendelezweni engaphandle phambi kwamagumbi la;
ubude balo babuziikubhite ezimashumi mahlanu.

<span id="an_42:8">42:8</span> Ngokuba ubude bamagumbi entendelezo
engaphandle baba ziikubhite ezimashumi mahlanu; kodwa ke phambi
kwetempile baba ziikubhite ezilikhulu.

<span id="an_42:9">42:9</span> Ngaphantsi kwala magumbi, ukungena
bekuvelwa ngasempumalanga ekuyiweni kuwo, kuvelwa entendelezweni
engaphandle.

<span id="an_42:10">42:10</span> Ebubanzini bodonga lwentendelezo,
kusingise empumalanga, phambi kwendawo eqhiwukileyo naphambi kwesakhiwo,
bekukho amagumbi.

<span id="an_42:11">42:11</span> Ayenendlela phambi kwawo, ebonakala
enjengamagumbi asingise entla; ngobude bawo, aba njalo nangobubanzi
bawo, aba njalo nangokuphuma kwawo konke, aba njalo nangamasiko awo.

<span id="an_42:12">42:12</span> Njengoko injalo iminyango yawo lawo,
injalo neminyango yamagumbi abe ekhangele ngezantsi; kwakukho umnyango
emantloko endlela, endlela emalunga nodonga olulungelelene namagumbi la,
endlela evela ngasempumalanga ekuyiweni kuwo.

<span id="an_42:13">42:13</span> Wathi kum, Amagumbi angasentla
namagumbi angasezantsi, aphambi kwendawo eqhiwukileyo, wona ngamagumbi
angcwele, apho ababingeleli abasondelayo kuYehova baya kudlela khona
ezona nto zingcwele; apho baya kuzibeka khona ezona nto zingcwele,
umnikelo wokudla, nedini lesono, neletyala; ngokuba le ndawo ingcwele.

<span id="an_42:14">42:14</span> Bakungena ababingeleli, mabangaphumi
engcweleni, baye entendelezweni engaphandle; bozibeka apho iingubo zabo,
abalungiselela benazo, ngokuba zingcwele; mabambathe ngubo zimbi,
basondele ke kokwabantu.

<span id="an_42:15">42:15</span> Wathi ke akugqiba ukuyilinganisa indlu
ephakathi, waphuma nam, wasingisa ngendlela yesango elibheke
empumalanga, walinganisa khona, wajikeleza ngeenxa zonke.

<span id="an_42:16">42:16</span> Walinganisa icala lasempumalanga
ngengcongolo yokulinganisa; yaziingcongolo ezimakhulu mahlanu
ngengcongolo yokulinganisa, ngeenxa zonke.

<span id="an_42:17">42:17</span> Walinganisa icala langasentla;
yaziingcongolo ezimakhulu mahlanu ngengcongolo yokulinganisa, ngeenxa
zonke.

<span id="an_42:18">42:18</span> Kwicala langasezantsi walinganisa
amakhulu amahlanu eengcongolo, ngengcongolo yokulinganisa.

<span id="an_42:19">42:19</span> Wajikela ecaleni langasentshonalanga,
walinganisa amakhulu amahlanu eengcongolo, ngengcongolo yokulinganisa.

<span id="an_42:20">42:20</span> Ngamacala omane wayilinganisa. Inodonga
olujikelezileyo ngeenxa zonke; ubude bangamakhulu amahlanu, nobubanzi
bangamakhulu amahlanu, ukuze kwahlulwe phakathi kokungcwele
nokuhlambeleyo.

<span id="an_43:1">43:1</span> Wandisa esangweni, esangweni elibheke
endleleni yangasempumalanga.

<span id="an_43:2">43:2</span> Nabo ke ubuqaqawuli boThixo kaSirayeli,
buvela ngendlela yangasempumalanga, isandi sabo sinjengesandi samanzi
amaninzi; ihlabathi lakhanya bubuqaqawuli bakhe.

<span id="an_43:3">43:3</span> Imbonakalo ke endayibonayo, ukubonakala
kwayo, yayinjengembonakalo leya, ndayibonayo ukuya kuwonakalisa kwam
umzi; kwakukho neembonakalo ezinjengeembonakalo endazibonayo emlanjeni
oyiKebhare; ndawa ke ngobuso.

<span id="an_43:4">43:4</span> Ubuqaqawuli bukaYehova beza endlwini
ngendlela yesango elibheke empumalanga.

<span id="an_43:5">43:5</span> UMoya wandifukula, wandisa entendelezweni
ephakathi; nabo ke ubuqaqawuli bukaYehova, buyizalisile indlu le.

<span id="an_43:6">43:6</span> Ndeva othetha kum esendlwini le; kwabakho
ke umntu omi ecaleni kwam.

<span id="an_43:7">43:7</span> Wathi kum, Nyana womntu, khangela indawo
yetrone yam, indawo yomphantsi weenyawo zam, apho ndiya kuhlala khona
phakathi koonyana bakaSirayeli ngonaphakade; ingabi salenza inqambi
igama lam elingcwele indlu kaSirayeli, bona nookumkani babo, ngobuhenyu
babo, nangezidumbu zookumkani babo ezigangeni zabo;

<span id="an_43:8">43:8</span> ekumiseni kwabo umbundu womnyango wabo
ngasembundwini womnyango wam, nemigubasi yabo ecaleni lemigubasi yam,
iludonga lodwa phakathi kwam nabo; belenze inqambi ke igama lam
elingcwele, ngamasikizi abo abawenzayo. Ndabagqibela ke ngomsindo wam.

<span id="an_43:9">43:9</span> Ngoku ke mabakhwelelise kum ubuhenyu
babo, nezidumbu zookumkani babo, ndihlale phakathi kwabo ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_43:10">43:10</span> Wena ke, nyana womntu, indlu kaSirayeli
yixelele le ndlu, beve ihlazo ngenxa yobugwenxa babo, basilinganise
isakhiwo esilinganiselweyo ngokuhle.

<span id="an_43:11">43:11</span> Ukuba bathe baliva ihlazo ngenxa
yezinto zonke abazenzileyo, bazise ukumeka kwendlu le nokuqulunqwa
kwayo, iziphumo zayo nezingeno zayo, iimeko zayo zonke nemimiselo yayo
yonke, iimeko zayo zonke nemiyalelo yayo yonke, uyibhale emehlweni abo;
bakugcine konke ukuma kwayo, nemimiselo yayo yonke, bayenze.

<span id="an_43:12">43:12</span> Nguwo lo umyalelo wayo indlu:
encotsheni yentaba, wonke umda wayo, ojikelezileyo ngeenxa zonke,
uyingcwele kangcwele. Yabona, nguwo lo umyalelo wayo indlu.

<span id="an_43:13">43:13</span> Yiyo le imilinganiso yesibingelelo
ngokweekubhite (ikubhite yikubhite nobubanzi besandla): umzantsi waso
woba yikubhite, ube yikubhite ububanzi; ulungqu lwawo eludinini lwawo
ngeenxa zonke lwalungangomoluko omnye weminwe. Lulo olo ufundo
lwesibingelelo esi.

<span id="an_43:14">43:14</span> Kuthabathela emzantsini osemhlabeni,
kude kuse emacaleni aphantsi, koba ziikubhite ezimbini ukuphakama,
nobubanzi bube yikubhite enye; kuthabathela emacaleni lawo amafutshane,
kude kuse emacaleni amade, koba ziikubhite ezine ukuphakama, nobubanzi
bube yikubhite enye.

<span id="an_43:15">43:15</span> Intaba kaThixo yoba ziikubhite ezine;
zothabathela ezikweni likaThixo, zinyuse iimpondo ezine.

<span id="an_43:16">43:16</span> Iziko likaThixo loba ziikubhite
ezilishumi elinambini ubude balo, ishumi elinambini ububanzi balo; loba
mbombo ne ngokwamacala alo omane.

<span id="an_43:17">43:17</span> Amacala oba ziikubhite ezilishumi
elinane ubude bawo, neshumi elinane ububanzi, ngokwamacala awo omane;
nolungqu ngeenxa zonke kuwo lube sisiqingatha sekubhite; umzantsi wawo
ube yikubhite enye ngeenxa zonke; nezinyuko zawo mazikhangele
empumalanga.

<span id="an_43:18">43:18</span> Wathi kum, Nyana womntu, itsho iNkosi
uYehova, ukuthi, Yiyo le imimiselo yesibingelelo ngemini yokwenziwa
kwaso, ukuba kunyuswe phezu kwaso amadini anyukayo, kutshizwe ngegazi
kuso.

<span id="an_43:19">43:19</span> Uya kubanika ababingeleli, abaLevi
abangabembewu kaTsadoki, abasondelayo kum, itsho iNkosi uYehova, ukuba
balungiselele kum inkunzi entsha, ithole lenkomo, libe lidini lesono.

<span id="an_43:20">43:20</span> Wothabatha egazini layo, uliqabe
ezimpondweni zaso zone, nasezimbombeni zone zamacala, naseludinini
ngeenxa zonke; usenze nyulu, usicamagushele;

<span id="an_43:21">43:21</span> uyithabathe inkunzi entsha yedini
lesono, bayitshise endaweni emisiweyo yayo indlu, ngaphandle kwengcwele.

<span id="an_43:22">43:22</span> Ngomhla wesibini wosondeza inkunzi
yebhokhwe exhonti egqibeleleyo, ibe lidini lesono; basenze nyulu
isibingelelo, njengoko senziwa nyulu ngenkunzi entsha.

<span id="an_43:23">43:23</span> Ekugqibeni kwakho ukusenza nyulu,
wosondeza inkunzi entsha, ithole lenkomo eligqibeleleyo, nenkunzi
egqibeleleyo yasempahleni emfutshane.

<span id="an_43:24">43:24</span> Wozisondeza phambi koYehova,
ababingeleli bagalele ityuwa phezu kwazo, bazinyuse zibe lidini
elinyukayo kuYehova.

<span id="an_43:25">43:25</span> Iintsuku ezisixhenxe uya kunikela
inkunzi yebhokhwe exhonti eyedini lesono ngemini; balungiselele nenkunzi
entsha elithole lenkomo, nenkunzi yasempahleni emfutshane egqibeleleyo.

<span id="an_43:26">43:26</span> Iintsuku ezisixhenxe bosicamagushela
isibingelelo, basihlambulule; basimisele.

<span id="an_43:27">43:27</span> Baya kuzigqiba ezo ntsuku, kuthi
ngomhla wesibhozo, nanini, ababingeleli benze amadini enu anyukayo
nemibingelelo yenu yoxolo esibingelelweni, ndize ndinamkele; itsho
iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_44:1">44:1</span> Wandibuyisa ngendlela yesango lengcwele
elingaphandle, elibheke empumalanga; laye livaliwe.

<span id="an_44:2">44:2</span> UYehova wathi kum, Eli sango liya kuhlala
livaliwe; aliyi kuvulwa, akuyi kungena mntu ngalo; ngokuba uYehova
uThixo kaSirayeli ungene ngalo; liya kuhlala livaliwe ke.

<span id="an_44:3">44:3</span> Isikhulu, sisikhulu nje, siya kuhlala
kulo, ukuba sidle ukudla phambi koYehova. Songena ngendlela
yasevarandeni yesango, siphume kwangendlela yayo.

<span id="an_44:4">44:4</span> Wandisa ngendlela yesango langasentla,
ebeyiphambi kwayo indlu; ndakhangela, nabo ubuqaqawuli bukaYehova
buyizalisile indlu kaYehova; ndawa ngobuso.

<span id="an_44:5">44:5</span> Wathi kum uYehova, Nyana womntu, gqala
ngentliziyo yakho, ubone ngamehlo akho, uve ngeendlebe zakho, konke
endisukuba ndikuthetha kuwe, ngokusingisele kwimimiselo yonke yendlu
kaYehova, nangokusingisele kwimiyalelo yayo yonke; ukugqale ngentliziyo
yakho ukungena endlwini le, ezindaweni zonke zengcwele ekuphunywa ngazo.

<span id="an_44:6">44:6</span> Uze uthi kwabaneenkani, kwabendlu
kaSirayeli, Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Yanelani, ndlu kaSirayeli,
ngamasikizi enu onke,

<span id="an_44:7">44:7</span> okubangenisa kwenu oonyana bolunye
uhlanga, abangalukileyo ngentliziyo, abangalukileyo ngenyama, ukuba babe
sengcweleni yam, ukuba bayihlambele indlu yam le, nakusondeza ukudla
kwam, amanqatha negazi. Umnqophiso wam nawaphula ke phezu kwamasikizi
enu onke;

<span id="an_44:8">44:8</span> anasigcina isigxina sengcwele yam;
nabamisa abaya ukuba banigcinele isigxina sam engcweleni yam.

<span id="an_44:9">44:9</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Bonke
oonyana bolunye uhlanga, abangalukileyo ngentliziyo, abangalukileyo
ngenyama, abayi kungena engcweleni yam, bakubo bonke oonyana bolunye
uhlanga, abaphakathi koonyana bakaSirayeli.

<span id="an_44:10">44:10</span> Ke kwanabaLevi, abakhwelelayo kude kum,
ekundwendweni kwamaSirayeli awandwendwayo kum, alandela izigodo zawo,
aya kubuthwala ubugwenxa bawo.

<span id="an_44:11">44:11</span> Baya kwanela ukuba ngabalungiseleli
engcweleni yam, bengabaveleli bamasango endlu le, belungiselela endlwini
le. Abo baya kuxhelela abantu idini elinyukayo nombingelelo, bona beme
phambi kwabo, ukuba babalungiselele.

<span id="an_44:12">44:12</span> Ngenxa enokuba babalungiselelayo phambi
kwezigodo zabo, baba sisikhubekiso sobugwenxa kwindlu kaSirayeli, ngenxa
yoko ndibaphakamisele isandla sam, itsho iNkosi uYehova, ukuba
babuthwale ubugwenxa babo.

<span id="an_44:13">44:13</span> Abayi kufika kum, ukuba benzelelele
kum, bangafiki kwiingcwele zam zonke, kwingcwele kangcwele yam; baya
kuthwala ke ihlazo labo namasikizi abo abawenzileyo.

<span id="an_44:14">44:14</span> Ndobenza babe ngabagcini besigxina
sendlu le ngokwenkonzo yayo yonke, nangokwezinto zonke ezenzelwa kuyo.

<span id="an_44:15">44:15</span> Ke bona ababingeleli abaLevi, oonyana
bakaTsadoki, abasigcinayo isigxina sengcwele yam, ekundwendweni koonyana
bakaSirayeli kum, bosondela bona kum, ukuba bandilungiselele, beme
phambi kwam, ukuba basondeze kum inqatha negazi; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_44:16">44:16</span> Bongena bona engcweleni yam, basondele
bona esithebeni sam, ukuba bandilungiselele, bagcine isigxina sam.

<span id="an_44:17">44:17</span> Kothi, ekungeneni kwabo ngamasango
entendelezo ephakathi, bambathe iingubo zelinen; kungabikho nto yoboya
kubo ekulungiseleleni kwabo emasangweni entendelezo ephakathi, naxa
bakuyo indlu.

<span id="an_44:18">44:18</span> Zoba ziinkontsho zelinen ezintlokweni
zabo, ibe ziibhulukhwe zelinen ezinqeni zabo; abayi kubhinqa,
bazibilise.

<span id="an_44:19">44:19</span> Bothi, ekuphumeni kwabo, besinga
entendelezweni engaphandle, entendelezweni engaphandle besiya ebantwini,
bazihlube iingubo zabo ababelungiselela benazo, bezibeke emagumbini
angcwele, bambathe ngubo zimbi, bangabangcwalisi abantu ngeengubo zabo.

<span id="an_44:20">44:20</span> Mabangazichebi iintloko, bangaziyeki
iinwele zabo zibe ngamayakayaka; bozinquthula iintloko.

<span id="an_44:21">44:21</span> Mabangaseli wayini bonke ababingeleli
ekungeneni kwabo entendelezweni ephakathi.

<span id="an_44:22">44:22</span> Umhlolokazi nomfazi owaliweyo
mabangabazeki babe ngabafazi babo; bozeka iintombi eziziintombi kwimbewu
yendlu kaSirayeli, kwanomhlolokazi othe waba ngumhlolokazi wombingeleli.

<span id="an_44:23">44:23</span> Bobayala abantu bam, ukuba bahlule
okungcwele kokuhlambeleyo, babazise okuyinqambi nokuhlambulukileyo.

<span id="an_44:24">44:24</span> Ekubambaneni kwabantu mabeme bona,
bagwebe ngokwamasiko am, bagcine imiyalelo yam nemimiselo yam ngamaxesha
am onke amisiweyo, bazingcwalise iisabatha zam.

<span id="an_44:25">44:25</span> Mabangayi emntwini ofileyo, bazenze
iinqambi; kungaba kungoyise, nonina, nonyana, nentombi yabo, nomzalwana,
nodade wabo ongabanga nandoda, abangazenza iinqambi ngabo, bona bodwa.

<span id="an_44:26">44:26</span> Bombalela imihla esixhenxe emva
kokuhlanjululwa kwakhe.

<span id="an_44:27">44:27</span> Ngomhla ke wokungena kwakhe engcweleni,
entendelezweni ephakathi, ukuze alungiselele engcweleni, wosondeza idini
lakhe lesono; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_44:28">44:28</span> Oko koba lilifa labo, ibe ndim ilifa
labo; ningabaniki nzuzo kwaSirayeli; ndim inzuzo yabo.

<span id="an_44:29">44:29</span> Umnikelo wokudla, nedini lesono, nedina
letyala, bodla ezo zinto bona; zonke izinto ezisingelwe phantsi
kwaSirayeli ziya kuba zezabo.

<span id="an_44:30">44:30</span> Iingqalo zeentlahlela zonke ezintweni
zonke, nemirhumo yonke yeento zonke, kwimirhumo yenu yonke, yoba
yeyababingeleli; nengqalo yomgrayo wenu noyinika umbingeleli, ukuze
ahlise intsikelelo phezu kwendlu yakho.

<span id="an_44:31">44:31</span> Ababingeleli abayi kudla nto izifeleyo
neqwengiweyo, nokuba kusezintakeni, nokuba kusezinkomeni.

<span id="an_45:1">45:1</span> Ekulabeni kwenu ilizwe ngamaqashiso,
ukuba libe lilifa, nomrhumela uYehova umrhumo oyinto engcwele kulo
ilizwe elo: ubude bube ngamashumi omabini anamahlanu amawaka
eengcongolo, ububanzi bube lishumi lamawaka. Woba ngcwele emdeni wawo
wonke ngeenxa zonke.

<span id="an_45:2">45:2</span> Kuwo apha oba ngawasengcweleni amakhulu
amahlanu ubude, ngamakhulu amahlanu obubanzi, ube mbombo-ne ngeenxa
zonke, ube ziikubhite ezimashumi mahlanu zephandle elingeenxa zonke
kuwo.

<span id="an_45:3">45:3</span> Kuyo loo ndawo ilinganisiweyo,
wolinganisa ubude obungamashumi omabini anamahlanu amawaka, nobubanzi
obulishumi lamawaka; ibe khona ingcwele le, ingcwele kangcwele.

<span id="an_45:4">45:4</span> Yona yoba yinto engcwele kulo ilizwe elo;
ilunge nababingeleli, abalungiseleli bengcwele, abasondela ukuba
balungiselele kuYehova; ibe yindawo yezindlu zabo, indawo engcwele
ilunge nengcwele.

<span id="an_45:5">45:5</span> Amashumi amabini anamahlanu amawaka
obude, neli shumi lamawaka obubanzi, alunge nabaLevi, abalungiseleli
bendlu; oba yinzuzo yabo eyimizi yokuba bahlale.

<span id="an_45:6">45:6</span> Okomzi koba ngamawaka amahlanu obubanzi,
anamashumi amabini anamahlanu amawaka obude, elungelelene nomrhumo
ongcwele; ibe ngawendlu yonke kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_45:7">45:7</span> Isikhulu nosinika ngapha nangapha
komrhumo ongcwele, nakokomzi phambi komrhumo ongcwele, naphambi kokomzi
ngecala lasentshonalanga, nise entshonalanga, nangecala lasempumalanga,
nise empumalanga; ubude bulungelelane nesinye isahlulo sezizwe,
buthabathele emdeni wasentshonalanga, buse emdeni wasempumalanga.

<span id="an_45:8">45:8</span> Loba lilizwe laso, libe yinzuzo kuso
kwaSirayeli; izikhulu zam zingabuyi zibe sabaxinzelela phantsi abantu
bam; ke ilizwe zilinike indlu kaSirayeli ngokwezizwe zayo.

<span id="an_45:9">45:9</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Yanelani,
nina zikhulu zakwaSirayeli; yekani ukugonyamela nokubhuqa, nenze
okusesikweni nobulungisa; yekani ukubagxotha abantu bam emafeni abo;
itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_45:10">45:10</span> Yibani nesikali sobulungisa, ne-efa
yobulungisa, nebhate yobulungisa.

<span id="an_45:11">45:11</span> Iefa nebhate yoba mlinganiso mnye,
ibhate ikhongozele isahlulo seshumi sehomere, ne-efa isahlulo seshumi
sehomere, sibe ngokwehomere isilinganiselo sayo.

<span id="an_45:12">45:12</span> Ishekele yoba ngamashumi amabini
eegera; amashumi amabini eeshekele, amashumi amabini anesihlanu
eeshekele, ishumi elinesihlanu leeshekele, ibe yimina kum.

<span id="an_45:13">45:13</span> Nguwo lo umrhumo eniya kurhuma ngawo;
isahlulo sesithandathu se-efa ehomereni yengqolowa, nirhume isahlulo
sesithandathu se-efa ehomereni yerhasi;

<span id="an_45:14">45:14</span> nomlinganiso omisiweyo weoli, webhate
yeoli, nirhume isahlulo seshumi sebhate ekoreni, ezibhateni ezilishumi
ehomereni ke; kuba iibhate ezilishumi ziyihomere.

<span id="an_45:15">45:15</span> Norhuma ixhwane libe linye empahleni
emfutshane engamakhulu amabini, yasemakriweni anamanzi akwaSirayeli, ibe
yeyomnikelo wokudla, neyedini elinyukayo, neyemibingelelo yoxolo, ukuba
bacanyagushelwe; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_45:16">45:16</span> Bonke abantu belizwe eli bosirhumela lo
mrhumo isikhulu sakwaSirayeli.

<span id="an_45:17">45:17</span> Orholwa sisikhulu amadini anyukayo,
nomnikelo wokudla, nothululwayo, emithendelekweni nasekuthwaseni
kwenyanga, nasezisabatheni, nasemaxesheni amisiweyo endlu kaSirayeli.
Lolungiselelwa siso idini lesono, nomnikelo wokudla, nedini elinyukayo,
nemibingelelo yoxolo, ukuze icanyagushelwe indlu kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_45:18">45:18</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ngenyanga
yokuqala, ngolokuqala enyangeni leyo, wothabatha inkunzi entsha, ithole
lenkomo eligqibeleleyo, uyihlambulule ingcwele ngedini lesono.

<span id="an_45:19">45:19</span> Umbingeleli wothabatha egazini ledini
lesono elo, aliqabe emigubasini yendlu le, nasezimbombeni zone zamacala
esibingelelo, nasemigubasini yesango lentendelezo ephakathi.

<span id="an_45:20">45:20</span> Uya kwenjenjalo nangolwesixhenxe
enyangeni leyo, ngenxa yomntu olahlekayo, nangenxa yosisiyatha,
niyicamagushele indlu le.

<span id="an_45:21">45:21</span> Ngeyokuqala inyanga, ngosuku lweshumi
elinesine enyangeni leyo, noba nepasika, umthendeleko weentsuku
ezisixhenxe; kodliwa izonka ezingenagwele.

<span id="an_45:22">45:22</span> Ngaloo mini isikhulu, ngenxa yaso
nangenxa yabantu bonke belizwe eli, solungiselela inkunzi entsha
yenkomo, ibe lidini lesono.

<span id="an_45:23">45:23</span> Iintsuku ezisixhenxe zomthendeleko
somenzela uYehova idini elinyukayo; iinkunzi ezintsha zeenkomo zibe
zisixhenxe, neenkunzi zeegusha ezigqibeleleyo zibe zisixhenxe ngemini,
ngeentsuku zosixhenxe; nenkunzi yebhokhwe exhonti ibe lidini lesono
ngemini.

<span id="an_45:24">45:24</span> Solungiselela umnikelo wokudla, iefa
enkunzini entsha, iefa enkunzini yegusha, ihin yeoli kuyo iefa.

<span id="an_45:25">45:25</span> Ngenyanga yesixhenxe, ngosuku lweshumi
elinesihlanu enyangeni leyo, emthendelekweni, siya kwenjenjalo
ngeentsuku ezisixhenxe ngokusingisele kwidini lesono, nakwidini
elinyukayo, nakumnikelo wokudla, nakwioli.

<span id="an_46:1">46:1</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Isango
lentendelezo ephakathi, elikhangele empumalanga, lohlala livaliwe
ngeentsuku ezintandathu zokusebenza; ngomhla wesabatha livulwe, ngomhla
wokuthwasa kwenyanga livulwe.

<span id="an_46:2">46:2</span> Songena isikhulu ngendlela yasevarandeni
yesango, sivela ngaphandle, sime emigubasini yesango, ababingeleli
balungiselele idini laso elinyukayo, nemibingelelo yaso yoxolo, siqubude
embundwini wesango; siphume ke; lingavalwa isango elo kude kuhlwe.

<span id="an_46:3">46:3</span> Abantu belizwe eli boqubuda ekungeneni
kwesango ngesabatha nasekuthwaseni kwenyanga, phambi koYehova.

<span id="an_46:4">46:4</span> Idini elinyukayo, esosondeza lona
isikhulu kuYehova ngomhla wesabatha, loba ziimvana ezintandathu
ezigqibeleleyo, nenkunzi yegusha egqibeleleyo.

<span id="an_46:5">46:5</span> Nomnikelo wokudla woba yiefa enkunzini
leyo yegusha; ezimvaneni ezo umnikelo wokudla ube ngumnikelo wesandla
saso, ihin yeoli kuyo iefa.

<span id="an_46:6">46:6</span> Ngosuku lokuthwasa kwenyanga, liya kuba
yinkunzi entsha egqibeleleyo, ithole lenkomo, neemvana ezintandathu,
nenkunzi yegusha, zigqibelele zonke.

<span id="an_46:7">46:7</span> Solungiselela umnikelo wokudla, iefa kuyo
inkunzi entsha yenkomo, ne-efa kuyo inkunzi yegusha, kuzo iimvana ibe
yinto esinokufikelela kuyo isandla saso, ibe yihin yeoli kuyo iefa.

<span id="an_46:8">46:8</span> Ekuzeni kwesikhulu, songena ngendlela
yasevarandeni yesango, siphume kwangendlela yayo.

<span id="an_46:9">46:9</span> Ekuzeni ke kwabantu belizwe eli phambi
koYehova ngamaxesha amisiweyo, ongene ngendlela yesango langasentla,
esiza kunqula, wophuma ngendlela yesango langasezantsi; ongene ngendlela
yesango langasezantsi, wophuma ngendlela yesango langasentla; akayi
kubuya ngendlela yesango angene ngalo; bothi gca ukuphuma.

<span id="an_46:10">46:10</span> Isikhulu songena siphakathi kwabo
ekungeneni kwabo; bathi ekuphumeni kwabo, siphume kunye nabo.

<span id="an_46:11">46:11</span> Umnikelo wokudla ngemithendeleko
nangamaxesha amisiweyo woba yiefa kuyo inkunzi entsha yenkomo, ne-efa
kuyo inkunzi yegusha, uthi ezimvaneni uligane nesandla saso, ibe yihin
yeoli kuyo iefa.

<span id="an_46:12">46:12</span> Xa sithe isikhulu samenzela uYehova
idini elinyukayo ngokuqhutywa yintliziyo, nokuba yimibingelelo yoxolo
ngokuqhutywa yintliziyo, malivulwe isango elibheke empumalanga,
silungiselele idini laso elinyukayo, nemibingelelo yaso yoxolo, njengoko
silungiselelayo ngomhla wesabatha; siphume ke; balivale isango emva
kokuphuma kwaso.

<span id="an_46:13">46:13</span> Boyilungiselela imvana emnyaka mnye,
egqibeleleyo, ibe lidini elinyukayo ngemini kuYehova, balilungiselele
imiso ngemiso yonke.

<span id="an_46:14">46:14</span> Bolungiselela umnikelo wokudla kunye
nalo imiso ngemiso yonke, ube sisahlulo sesithandathu se-efa, neoli ibe
sisahlulo sesithathu sehin yokunyakamisa umgubo ocoliweyo; ube
ngumnikelo wokudla kuYehova; leyo yoba yimimiselo engunaphakade emiyo.

<span id="an_46:15">46:15</span> Bolungiselela imvana, nomnikelo
wokudla, neoli, imiso ngemiso yonke, ibe lidini elinyukayo elimiyo.

<span id="an_46:16">46:16</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Xa sithe
isikhulu sampha omnye koonyana baso isipho, soba lilifa lakhe, sibe
sesoonyana bakhe; yinzuzo yabo ngokwelifa.

<span id="an_46:17">46:17</span> Xa sithe sampha omnye kubakhonzi baso
isipho elifeni laso, soba sesalowo, kude kuse kumnyaka wenkululeko,
sibuyele kwisikhulu; ilifa laso loba leloonyana baso bodwa.

<span id="an_46:18">46:18</span> Isikhulu eso asiyi kuthabatha elifeni
labantu, ukuze sibaxinzelele phantsi, bahlukane nenzuzo yabo. Sobadlisa
oonyana baso ilifa kweyeyaso inzuzo; ukuze bangabi lusali abantu bam,
elowo ahlukane nenzuzo yakhe.

<span id="an_46:19">46:19</span> Ekungeneni ngasecaleni lesango, wandisa
emagumbini angcwele ababingeleli, akhangele ngentla; nanko, kukho indawo
khona esiphelweni, ngasentshonalanga.

<span id="an_46:20">46:20</span> Wathi kum, Le yindawo apho ababingeleli
bophekela khona idini letyala, nedini lesono. Bosela khona umnikelo
wokudla, ukuze bangaphumi nawo, baye entendelezweni engaphandle, ukuba
bangcwalise abantu.

<span id="an_46:21">46:21</span> Waphuma waya nam entendelezweni
engaphandle, wandidlulisa emagumbini omane entendelezo; nanko, kukho
intendelezo emagumbini onke entendelezo, iyintendelezo egumbini
lentendelezo.

<span id="an_46:22">46:22</span> Emagumbini omane ayo intendelezo ibe
izintendelezo ezivaliweyo: ubude buziikubhite ezimashumi mane, ububanzi
buziikubhite ezimashumi mathathu, umlinganiso umnye kuloo magumbi omane.

<span id="an_46:23">46:23</span> Bekukho ucamba lwezakhiwo
olujikelezileyo kuzo, lujikelezile kuzo zone; kukho amaziko okupheka,
enziwe ngaphantsi kweengcamba ngeenxa zonke.

<span id="an_46:24">46:24</span> Wathi kum, Ezi zizindlu zokupheka, apho
abalungiseleli bayo indlu baphekela khona umbingelelo wabantu.

<span id="an_47:1">47:1</span> Wandibuyisela emnyango wayo indlu; nanko,
kuphuma amanzi ngaphantsi kombundu womnyango wendlu leyo, esinga
ngasempumalanga; ngokuba ubuso bayo indlu bebungasempumalanga. Amana
esihla amanzi, evela ngaphantsi, ecaleni lokunene kwindlu leyo,
ngasezantsi kwesibingelelo.

<span id="an_47:2">47:2</span> Waphuma nam ngendlela yesango
langasentla, wandijikelezisa ngendlela engaphandle, wandisa esangweni
elingaphandle, ngendlela yelibheke empumalanga; nango, amanzi equkuqela,
evela ecaleni lokunene lesango.

<span id="an_47:3">47:3</span> Ekuphumeni komntu obephethe ulutya
lokulinganisa ngesandla, esiya ngasempumalanga, walinganisa iwaka
leekubhite; wandiweza emanzini, amanzi abetha emaqatheni.

<span id="an_47:4">47:4</span> Walinganisa iwaka, wandiweza emanzini,
amanzi abetha emadolweni. Walinganisa iwaka, wandiweza emanzini, amanzi
abetha esinqeni.

<span id="an_47:5">47:5</span> Walinganisa iwaka, aba ngumlambo
endingenakuwuwela; ngokuba amanzi ahamba phezulu, amanzi aba
ngawokudadwa, umlambo ongenakuwelwa.

<span id="an_47:6">47:6</span> Wathi kum, Ubonile na, nyana womntu?
Wandihambisa, wandibuyisa phezu kodini lomlambo lowo.

<span id="an_47:7">47:7</span> Ekubuyeni kwam, nanko kukho eludinini
lomlambo imithi emininzi kunene, ngapha nangapha.

<span id="an_47:8">47:8</span> Wathi kum, La manzi aphuma aye kummandla
wasempumalanga, ehle aye eArabha, aye elwandle, athi ele elwandle,
aphiliswe amanzi alo.

<span id="an_47:9">47:9</span> Kuye kuthi ke, yonke imiphefumlo
ephilileyo, enyakazelayo ezindaweni zonke othe wafika kuzo umlambokazi
lowo, iphile; zibe zininzi kunene iintlanzi; ngokuba efikile khona la
manzi, ophiliswa lawa; iphile yonke into ofike kuyo umlambo lowo.

<span id="an_47:10">47:10</span> Kothi ke kume ababambisi beentlanzi
phezu kwawo, bathabathele e-En-gedi, bade baye e-En-heglayim, indawo
yokwaneka iminatha; ziya kuba ngokohlobo lwazo iintlanzi zabo,
njengeentlanzi zolwandle olukhulu, ukuba zininzi kunene.

<span id="an_47:11">47:11</span> Ke imigxobhozo yalo, namadike alo,
akayi kuphila; aya kunikelwa ekubeni mtyuba.

<span id="an_47:12">47:12</span> Kophuma phezu komlambo, phezu kodini
lwawo, ngapha nangapha, imithi yonke edliwayo. Amagqabi ayo akayi
kubuna, zingapheli iziqhamo zayo; iya kuvuthwa iziqhamo ezitsha
ngeenyanga zonke; ngokuba amanzi awo wona aphuma engcweleni. Iziqhamo
zayo ziya kuba zezokudliwa, namagqabi ayo abe ngawokuphilisa.

<span id="an_47:13">47:13</span> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Nguwo lo
umda, eniya kuzabela ngawo ilizwe, ngokwezizwe ezilishumi elinazibini
zikaSirayeli; uYosefu woba namacandelo amabini.

<span id="an_47:14">47:14</span> Ilizwe niya kulidla ilifa, elowo alidle
njengowabo; ngokuba ndaphakamisa isandla sam sokuba ndilinike oyihlo;
lowela kuni eli lizwe ngokwelifa.

<span id="an_47:15">47:15</span> Nguwo lo umda welizwe elo: ngecala
langasentla wothabathela kulwandle olukhulu ngendlela yaseHetelon, ukuba
uye eTsedada;

<span id="an_47:16">47:16</span> eHamati, naseBherota, naseSibrayim,
ephakathi komda waseDamasko nomda waseHamati, naseHatsere ephakathi,
esemdeni waseHawuran.

<span id="an_47:17">47:17</span> Umda uthabathela elwandle, ume
ngeHatsare-enon, umda waseDamasko; owasentla ngasentla umda waseHamati.
Licala lasentla ke elo.

<span id="an_47:18">47:18</span> Icala langasempumalanga, phakathi
kweHawuran neDamasko neGiliyadi nelizwe lakwaSirayeli, yiYordan;
nothabathela emdeni lowa, nise phezu kolwandle lwangasempumalanga
ukulinganisa. Licala lasempumalanga ke elo.

<span id="an_47:19">47:19</span> Icala lasezantsi ngasezantsi
lothabathela kwaTamare, lise emanzini embambano aseKadeshe, lihambe
ngomlambo, lise kulo ulwandle olukhulu. Licala lasezantsi ngasezantsi ke
elo.

<span id="an_47:20">47:20</span> Icala lasentshonalanga lulwandle
olukhulu, luthabathela emdeni lowo, lude lulunge nokuya eHamati. Licala
lasentshonalanga ke elo.

<span id="an_47:21">47:21</span> Nozabela ke eli lizwe ngokwezizwe
zakwaSirayeli.

<span id="an_47:22">47:22</span> Kothi ke nilabe ngamaqashiso, libe
lilifa kuni, nakubasemzini, abaphambukela kuni, abazele oonyana phakathi
kwenu. Kuni boba njengabazalelwe kuloo ndawo abaphakathi koonyana
bakaSirayeli; bolamkela ngamaqashiso ilifa phakathi kwezizwe
zakwaSirayeli kunye nani.

<span id="an_47:23">47:23</span> Kuya kuthi, esizweni aphambukele kuso
owasemzini, nimnike ilifa lakhe apho; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_48:1">48:1</span> Ngawo la amagama ezizwe ezo, ethabathela
ekupheleni ngentla, ehamba ecaleni kwendlela yaseHetelon, ukuya eHamati,
naseHatsare-enon, umda waseDamasko, ngasentla ecaleni laseHamati, libe
lelakhe icala lasempumalanga nelasentshonalanga: uDan woba necandelo
elinye.

<span id="an_48:2">48:2</span> Ngasemdeni ke kaDan, kuthabathela ecaleni
lasempumalanga, kuse ecaleni lasentshonalanga: uAshere, libe linye.

<span id="an_48:3">48:3</span> Ngasemdeni ke ka-Ashere, kuthabathela
ecaleni lasempumalanga, kuse ecaleni lasentshonalanga: uNafetali, libe
linye.

<span id="an_48:4">48:4</span> Ngasemdeni kaNafetali, kuthabathela
ecaleni lasempumalanga, kuse ecaleni lasentshonalanga: uManase, libe
linye.

<span id="an_48:5">48:5</span> Ngasemdeni kaManase, kuthabathela ecaleni
lasempumalanga, kuse ecaleni lasentshonalanga: uEfrayim, libe linye.

<span id="an_48:6">48:6</span> Ngasemdeni kaEfrayim, kuthabathele
ecaleni lasempumalanga, kuse ecaleni lasentshonalanga: uRubhen, libe
linye.

<span id="an_48:7">48:7</span> Ngasemdeni kaRubhen, kuthabathela ecaleni
lasempumalanga, kuse ecaleni lasentshonalanga: uYuda, libe linye.

<span id="an_48:8">48:8</span> Ngasemdeni kaYuda, kuthabathela ecaleni
lasempumalanga, kuse ecaleni lasentshonalanga, yoba ngumrhumo eniya
kuwurhuma; ube ngamawaka angamashumi amabini anamahlanu eengcongolo
ububanzi, ubude ke bube njengobesinye isahlulo, kuthabathela ecaleni
lasempumalanga, kude kuye ecaleni lasentshonalanga; ingcwele
isesazulwini sawo.

<span id="an_48:9">48:9</span> Umrhumo eniya kuwurhumela uYehova woba
ngamashumi amabini anamahlanu amawaka ubude, ube ngamawaka alishumi
ububanzi.

<span id="an_48:10">48:10</span> Woba ngowaba umrhumo ongcwele:
ngowababingeleli; ngasentla ube ngamashumi amabini anamahlanu amawaka
ubude, ngasentshonalanga ube lishumi lamawaka ububanzi, ngasempumalanga
ube lishumi lamawaka ububanzi, ngasezantsi ube ngamashumi amabini
anamahlanu amawaka ubude; ingcwele kaYehova yoba sesazulwini sawo.

<span id="an_48:11">48:11</span> Ababingeleli abangcwalisiweyo koonyana
bakaTsadoki, abasigcinayo isigxina sam, abangandwendwanga ekundwendweni
koonyana bakaSirayeli, njengoko bandwendwayo abaLevi,

<span id="an_48:12">48:12</span> woba ngowabo umrhumo emrhumeni welizwe;
uyingcwele kangcwele ngasemdeni wabakaLevi.

<span id="an_48:13">48:13</span> Ke abaLevi bozuza isahlulo esinxulumene
nomda wababingeleli, sibe ngamashumi amabini anamahlanu amawaka ubude,
sibe lishumi lamawaka ububanzi; bonke ubude bube ngamashumi amabini
anamahlanu amawaka, nobubanzi bube lishumi lamawaka.

<span id="an_48:14">48:14</span> Ke abayi kuthengisa ngento yaso,
bangananisi ugayo, bangayidluliseli kwabanye intlahlela yelo zwe;
ngokuba ingcwele kuYehova.

<span id="an_48:15">48:15</span> Ke amawaka amahlanu aseleyo ebubanzini,
kumawaka angamashumi amabini anamahlanu, akangcwele; ngawomzi,
ngawendawo yokuma neyephandle. Umzi woba sesazulwini sawo.

<span id="an_48:16">48:16</span> Yiyo le imilinganiso: icala langasentla
loba ngamawaka amane anamakhulu amahlanu, icala langasezantsi libe
ngamawaka amane anamakhulu amahlanu, icala lasempumalanga libe ngamawaka
amane anamakhulu amahlanu, icala lasentshonalanga libe ngamawaka amane
anamakhulu amahlanu.

<span id="an_48:17">48:17</span> Iphandle lomzi ngasentla loba
ngamakhulu amabini anamashumi amahlanu, ngasezantsi libe ngamakhulu
amabini anamashumi amahlanu, ngasempumalanga libe ngamakhulu amabini
anamashumi amahlanu, ngasentshonalanga libe ngamakhulu amabini
anamashumi amahlanu.

<span id="an_48:18">48:18</span> Okuseleyo ebudeni obunxulumene nomrhumo
ongcwele, koba ngamawaka alishumi ngasempumalanga, kube ngamawaka
alishumi ngasentshonalanga; onxulumana nomrhumo ongcwele; ungeniselo
lwawo lube kukudla kwabasebenzi bawo umzi.

<span id="an_48:19">48:19</span> Abasebenzi abo ke bomzi bowalima,
bengabasezizweni zonke zakwaSirayeli.

<span id="an_48:20">48:20</span> Umrhumo wonke woba ngamashumi amabini
anamahlanu amawaka ubude, ube ngamashumi amabini anamahlanu amawaka
ububanzi; isahlulo sesine somrhumo ongcwele nosirhumela ukuba sibe
sesomzi lowo.

<span id="an_48:21">48:21</span> Indawo eseleyo yoba yeyesikhulu, ngapha
nangapha komrhumo ongcwele, nakwinzuzo yomzi; ngaphambi kwamawaka
angamashumi amabini anamahlanu omrhumo, ide iye emdeni wasempumalanga,
nangasentshonalanga phambi kwamawaka angamashumi amabini anamahlanu,
ngasemdeni wentshonalanga, inxulumene nezinye izahlulo, yoba
yeyesikhulu; umrhumo ongcwele nengcwele yayo indlu yoba sesazulwini
sayo.

<span id="an_48:22">48:22</span> Kuthabathela ke enzuzweni yabaLevi,
kuthabathela enzuzweni yomzi, esazulwini senzuzo yesikhulu, phakathi
komda kaYuda nomda kaBhenjamin, koba kokwesikhulu.

<span id="an_48:23">48:23</span> Eziseleyo ke izizwe: kuthabathela
ecaleni lasempumalanga, kuse ecaleni lasentshonalanga: uBhenjamin woba
necandelo elinye.

<span id="an_48:24">48:24</span> Ngasemdeni ke kaBhenjamin, kuthabathela
ecaleni lasempumalanga, kuse ecaleni lasentshonalanga: uSimon, libe
linye.

<span id="an_48:25">48:25</span> Ngasemdeni ke kaSimon, kuthabathela
ecaleni lasempumalanga, kuse ecaleni lasentshonalanga: uIsakare, libe
linye.

<span id="an_48:26">48:26</span> Ngasemdeni ke kaIsakare, kuthabathela
ecaleni lasempumalanga, kuse ecaleni lasentshonalanga: uZebhulon, libe
linye.

<span id="an_48:27">48:27</span> Ngasemdeni ke kaZebhulon, kuthabathela
ecaleni lasempumalanga, kuse ecaleni lasentshonalanga: uGadi, libe
linye.

<span id="an_48:28">48:28</span> Ngasemdeni ke kaGadi, ngasecaleni
lasezantsi, ngasezantsi, umda wothabathela kwaTamare, use emanzini
embambano aseKadeshe, ukhweze umlambo, use kulo ulwandle olukhulu.

<span id="an_48:29">48:29</span> Lilo elo ilizwe eniya kulabela izizwe
zakwaSirayeli ngamaqashiso, ngokwamafa. Zizo ezo izahlulo zalo, itsho
iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_48:30">48:30</span> Zizo ezi iziphelo zamacala omzi:
ngecala langasentla ngamawaka amane anamakhulu amahlanu, umlinganiso
ngengcongolo;

<span id="an_48:31">48:31</span> amasango omzi oba ngokwamagama ezizwe
zakwaSirayeli, ibe ngamasango amathathu ngasentla: ibe lisango
likaRubhen elinye, ibe lisango likaYuda elinye, ibe lisango likaLevi
elinye.

<span id="an_48:32">48:32</span> Ngecala lasempumalanga yoba ngamawaka
amane anamakhulu amahlanu eengcongolo; amasango ke mathathu: ibe lisango
likaYosefu elinye, ibe lisango likaBhenjamin elinye, ibe lisango likaDan
elinye.

<span id="an_48:33">48:33</span> Ngecala langasezantsi, umlinganiso yoba
ngamawaka amane anamakhulu amahlanu; amasango ke mathathu: ibe lisango
likaSimon elinye, ibe lisango likaIsakare elinye, ibe lisango
likaZebhulon elinye.

<span id="an_48:34">48:34</span> Ngecala lasentshonalanga yoba ngamawaka
amane anamakhulu amahlanu; amasango ke awo mathathu: ibe lisango
likaGadi elinye, ibe lisango lika-Ashere elinye, ibe lisango
likaNafetali elinye.

<span id="an_48:35">48:35</span> Ukujikeleza ke lishumi elinesibhozo
lamawaka eengcongolo. Igama lawo umzi kothiwa kususela kuloo mini,
nguYehova-ekhona.

------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Next: Daniel](dan)
